śrīlakṣmīnṛsiṃhāya namaḥ । śrīvedavyāsāya namaḥ । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet ।। vajrādhikanakhasparśa divyasiṃha namo astu te ।।
hiraṇyakaśipor vakṣaḥkṣetrāsṛkkardamāruṇāḥ ।। trikālajñā mahātmāno naimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ ।। mahendrādriratā ye ca ye ca vindhyanivāsinaḥ ।। śrīśailaniratā ye ca kurukṣetranivāsinaḥ ।।
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ saśiṣyā munayo amalāḥ ।। tatra snātvā yathānyāyaṃ kṛtvā karma japādikam ।। dṛṣṭvā tatra bharadvājaṃ puṇyatīrthanivāsinam ।। āsaneṣu vicitreṣu vṛṣyādiṣu yathākramam ।।
kṛṣṇāśritāḥ kathāḥ sarve parasparam athābruvan ।। ājagāma mahātejās tatra sūto mahāmatiḥ ।। tān praṇamya yathānyāyaṃ sa ca taiś cābhipūjitaḥ ।। sa papraccha bharadvājo munīnām agratas tadā ।।
tvattaḥ śrutā purā sūta etair asmābhir eva ca ।। śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ sūta śrotukāmā ime sthitāḥ ।। ṛṣīṇām agrataḥ sūta prātar hy eṣāṃ mahātmanām ।। kasmin vā layam abhyeti jagad etac carācaram ।।
karmaṇā tu mahābhāga tan me brūhi mahāmate ।। kathaṃ yugasya gaṇanā kiṃ vā syāt tu caturyugam ।। katham ārādhyate devo narasiṃho apy amānuṣaiḥ ।। nadyaś ca kāḥ parāḥ puṇyā nṛṇāṃ pāpaharāḥ śubhāḥ ।।
tathā vidyādharādīnāṃ sṛṣṭir ādau kathaṃ bhavet ।। etat sarvaṃ mahābhāga kathayasva yathākramam ।। taṃ praṇamya pravakṣyāmi purāṇaṃ nārasiṃhakam ।। śaśvacchāntaṃ śamitaviṣayaṃ śuddhatejo viśālam vedavyāsaṃ vigataśamalaṃ sarvadāhaṃ namāmi ।।
yasya prasādād vakṣyāmi vāsudevakathām imām ।। viṣṇuprasādena vinā vaktuṃ kenāpi śakyate ।। pravakṣyāmi mahāpunyaṃ bhāradvāja śṛṇuṣva me ।। purāṇaṃ narasiṃhasya pravakṣyāmi yathātathā ।।
tenaiva pālyate sarvaṃ narasiṃhādimūrtibhiḥ ।। yathaiva devaḥ sṛjati tathā vakṣyāmi tac chṛṇu ।। śloko yas taṃ mune śrutvā niḥśeṣaṃ tvaṃ tataḥ śṛṇu ।। vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva purāṇaṃ pañcalakṣaṇam ।।
vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva vakṣyāmy anusamāsataḥ ।। yasmād ārabhya devānāṃ rājñāṃ caritam eva ca ।। prāk sṛṣṭeḥ pralayād ūrdhvaṃ nāsīt kiṃcid dvijottama ।। nityaṃ nirañjanaṃ śāntaṃ nirguṇaṃ nityanirmalam ।।
sarvajñaṃ jñānarūpatvād anantam ajam avyayam ।। antarlīnaṃ vikāraṃ ca tat sraṣṭum upacakrame ।। sāttviko rājasaś caiva tāmasaś ca tridhā mahān ।। trividho ayam ahaṃkāro mahattattvād ajāyata ।।
bhūtādis tu vikurvāṇaḥ śabdatanmātrakaṃ tataḥ ।। śabdamātraṃ tathākāśaṃ bhūtādiḥ sa samāvṛṇot ।। balavān abhavad vāyus tasya sparśo guṇo mataḥ ।। tato vāyur vikurvāṇo rūpamātraṃ sasarja ha ।।
sparśamātraṃ tu vai vāyū rūpamātraṃ samāvṛṇot ।। saṃbhavanti tato ambhāṃsi rasādhārāṇi tāni tu ।। vikurvāṇāni cāmbhāṃsi gandhamātraṃ sasarjire ।। saṃghāto jāyate tasmāt tasya gandhaguṇo mataḥ ।।
tanmātrāṇy aviśeṣāṇi viśeṣāḥ karmaśo aparāḥ ।। kīrtitas te samāsena bharadvāja mayā tava ।। ekādaśaṃ manaś cātra kīrtitaṃ tatra cintakaiḥ ।। tāni vakṣyāmi teṣāṃ ca karmāṇi kulapāvana ।।
śabdādijñānasiddhyarthaṃ buddhiyuktāni pañca vai ।। visargānandaśilpī ca gatyuktī karma tat smṛtam ।। śabdādibhir guṇair vipra saṃyuktāny uttarottaraiḥ ।। nāśaknuvan prajāṃ sraṣṭum asamāgamya kṛtsnaśaḥ ।।
ekasaṃghātalakṣyāś ca saṃprāpyaikyam aśeṣataḥ ।। mahadādyā viśeṣāntās tv aṇḍam utpādayanti te ।। bhūtebhyo aṇḍaṃ mahābuddhe bṛhat tad udakeśayam ।। tatrāvyaktasvarūpo asau viṣṇur viśveśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।।
garbhodakaṃ samudrāś ca tasyābhūvan mahātmanaḥ ।। tasminn aṇḍe abhavat sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।। brahmarūpaṃ samāsthāya jagatsṛṣṭau pravartate ।। narasiṃhādirūpeṇa rudrarūpeṇa saṃharet ।।
rāmādirūpaṃ sa tu gṛhya pāti bhūtvātha rudraḥ prakaroti nāśam ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sarganirūpaṇaṃ nāma prathamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। yathā te kathayiṣyāmi bharadvāja nibodha me ।। utpannaḥ procyate vidvan nityo asāv upacārataḥ ।।
tat parākhyaṃ tadardhaṃ ca parārdham abhidhīyate ।। tena tasya nibodha tvaṃ parimāṇopapādanam ।। bhūbhūbhṛtsāgarādīnām aśeṣāṇāṃ ca sattama ।। aṣṭādaśa nimeṣās tu kāṣṭhaikā parikīrtitā ।।
triṃśatsaṃkhyair ahorātraṃ muhūrtair mānuṣaṃ smṛtam ।। taiḥ ṣaḍbhir ayanaṃ māsair dve ayane dakṣiṇottare ।। ayanadvitayaṃ varṣaṃ martyānām iha kīrtitam ।। vasvādīnām ahorātram mānuṣo vatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
caturyugaṃ dvādaśabhis tadvibhāgaṃ nibodha me ।। divyābdānāṃ sahasrāṇi yugeṣv āhuḥ purāvidaḥ ।। saṃdhyāṃśakaś ca tattulyo yugasyānantaro hi saḥ ।। yugākhyaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ kṛtatretādisaṃjñakaḥ ।।
procyate tatsahasraṃ tu brahmaṇo divasaṃ dvija ।। bhavanti parimāṇaṃ ca teṣāṃ kālakṛtaṃ śṛṇu ।। ekakālaṃ hi sṛjyante saṃhriyante ca pūrvavat ।। manvantaraṃ manoḥ kālaḥ śakrādīnām api dvija ।।
dvipañcāśat tathānyāni sahasrāṇy adhikāni tu ।। saptaṣaṣṭis tathānyāni niyutāni mahāmune ।। manvantarasya saṃkhyeyaṃ mānuṣair vatsarair dvija ।। viśvasyādau sumanasā sṛṣṭvā devāṃs tathā pitṛn ।।
ṛṣīn vidyādharāṃś caiva manuṣyāṃś ca paśūṃs tathā ।। cāturvarṇyaṃ tathā sṛṣṭvā niyujyādhvarakarmaṇi ।। śete cānantaśayane tāvantīṃ rātrim avyayaḥ ।। yasmin matsyāvatāro abhūn mathanaṃ ca mahodadheḥ ।।
uddhartuṃ vasudhāṃ devīṃ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ ।। naimittikākhye pralaye samastaṃ saṃhṛtya śete harir ādidevaḥ ।। ।। iti śrinarasiṃhapurāṇe sargaracanāyāṃ dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। tasmin padme mahābhāga vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।।
evam uktvā tirobhāvaṃ gato nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। āste kiṃcij jagadbījaṃ nādhyagacchata kiṃcana ।। tato bālaḥ samutpannas tasyāṅke roṣasaṃbhavaḥ ।। nāma me dehi cetyuktas tasya rudrety asau dadau ।।
aśaktas tatra salile mamajja tapasādṛtaḥ ।। brahmā sasarja bhūteśo dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhato aparam ।। sa tasyāṃ janayāmasa manuṃ svāyaṃbhuvaṃ prabhuḥ ।। sṛjato jagatīṃ tasya kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchasi ।।
vistareṇa punar brūhi ādisargaṃ mahāmate ।। sattvodriktas tadā brahmā śūnyaṃ lokam avaikṣata ।। brahmasvarūpī bhagavān anādiḥ sarvasaṃbhavaḥ ।। brahmasvarūpiṇaṃ devaṃ jagataḥ prabhavātmakam ।।
ayanaṃ tasya tāḥ pūrvaṃ tena nārāyaṇa smṛtaḥ ।। abuddhipūrvakaṃ tasya prādurbhūtaṃ tamas tadā ।। avidyā pañcaparvaiṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ ।। mukhyasargaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sargasiddhivicakṣaṇaiḥ ।।
tiryaksrotas tatas tasmāt tiryagyonis tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tam apy asādhakaṃ matvā tiryagyoni caturmukhaḥ ।। tadā tuṣṭo anyasargaṃ ca cintayāmasa vai prabhuḥ ।। arvāksrotāḥ samutpannā manuṣyāḥ sādhakā matāḥ ।।
tasmāt te duḥkhabahulā bhūyo bhūyaś ca kāriṇaḥ ।। prathamo mahataḥ sargas tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyakaḥ ।। mukhyasargaś caturthas tu mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tatoūrdhvasrotasāṃ ṣaṣṭho devasargas tu sa smṛtaḥ ।।
aṣṭamo anugrahaḥ sargaḥ sāttviko ya udāhṛtaḥ ।। prākṛto vaikṛtaś caiva kaumāro navamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sṛjato brahmaṇaḥ sṛṣṭim utpannā ye mayeritā ।। avyaktarūpī paramātmasaṃjñaḥ saṃpreryamāṇo nikhilātmavedyaḥ ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sṛṣṭiracanāprakāro nāma tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। kathaṃ sā vavṛdhe sūta etat kathaya me adhunā ।। marīcir atriś ca tathā aṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।। nārado daśamaś caiva vasiṣṭhaś ca mahāmatiḥ ।।
pravṛttākhye marīcyādyā muktvaikaṃ nāradaṃ munim ।। tasya dauhitravaṃśena jagad etac carācaram ।। sarve dakṣasya kanyāsu jātāḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ।। vṛddhiṃ gatāni tāny evam anusargodbhavāni tu ।।
vasiṣṭhāntā mahābhāga brahmaṇo mānasodbhavāḥ ।। sa eva paścāc caturāsyarūpī munisvarūpī ca sṛjaty anantaḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe caturtho adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। punaḥ sarve marīcyādyāḥ sasṛjus te kathaṃ punaḥ ।।
brahmaṇo manasaḥ pūrvam utpannasya mahāmate ।। pratisargaṃ munīnāṃ tu vistarād vadataḥ śṛṇu ।। prādurāsīt prabhor aṅke kumāro nīlalohitaḥ ।। tejasā bhāsayan sarvā diśaś ca pradiśaś ca saḥ ।।
vibhajātmānam adya tvaṃ mama vākyān mahāmate ।। strībhāvaṃ puruṣatvaṃ ca pṛthak pṛthag athākarot ।। teṣāṃ nāmāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇu me dvijasattama ।। haraś ca bahurūpaś ca tryambakaś cāparājitaḥ ।।
ekādaśaite kathitā rudrās tribhuvaneśvarāḥ ।। umaiva bahurūpeṇa patnī saiva vyavasthitā ।। tadā sa sṛṣṭavān devo rudras tatra pratāpavān ।। piśācān rākṣasāṃś caiva siṃhoṣṭramakarānanān ।।
vināyakānām ugrāṇāṃ triṃśatkoṭy ardham eva ca ।। evaṃprakāro rudro asau mayā te kīrtitaḥ prabhuḥ ।। devādisthāvarāntāś ca prajāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā ।। tadā mānasaputrān sa sadṛśān ātmano asṛjat ।।
pracetasaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca bhṛguṃ caiva mahāmatim ।। agniś ca pitaraś caiva brahmaputrau tu mānasau ।। śatarūpāṃ ca sṛṣṭvā tu kanyāṃ sa manave dadau ।। priyavratottānapādau prasūtiṃ caiva kanyakām ।।
prasūtyāṃ ca tadā dakṣaś caturviṃśatikaṃ tathā ।। śraddhā lakṣmīr dhṛtis tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭir medhā tathā kriyā ।। apatyārthaṃ prajagrāha dharmo dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ ।। dharmasya putrapautrādyair dharmavaṃśo vivardhitaḥ ।।
saṃbhūtiś cānasūyā ca smṛtiḥ prītiḥ kṣamāḥ tathā ।। tadvat putrau mahābhāgau mātariśvātha satyavān ।। etāś ca dattā dakṣeṇa ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।। patnī marīceḥ saṃbhūtir jajñe sā kaśyapaṃ munim ।।
sinīvālī kuhūs caiva rākā cānumatis tathā ।। somaṃ durvāsasaṃ caiva dattātreyaṃ ca yoginam ।। tasmāt svāhā sutāṃl lebhe trīn udāraujaso dvija ।। teṣāṃ tu saṃtatāv anye catvāriṃśac ca pañca ca ।।
evam ekonapañcāśad vahnayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। tebhyaḥ svadhā sute jajñe menāṃ vai dhāriṇīṃ tathā ।। yathā sasarja bhūtāni tathā me śṛṇu sattama ।। devān ṛṣīṃś ca gandharvān asurān pannagāṃs tathā ।।
tadā saṃcintya sa muniḥ sṛṣṭihetoḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। asiknīm udvahan kanyāṃ vīraṇasya prajāpateḥ ।। dadau sa daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayodaśa ।। dve caiva bahuputrāya dve caivāṅgirase tathā ।।
viśvedevāṃs tu viśvā yā sādhyā sādhyān asūyata ।। bhānos tu bhānavo devā muhūrtāyāṃ muhūrtajāḥ ।। pṛthivīviṣayaṃ sarvam arundhatyām ajāyata ।। ye tv anekavasuprāṇā devā jyotiḥpurogamāḥ ।।
āpo dhruvaś ca somaś ca dharmaś caivānilo analaḥ ।। teṣāṃ putrāś ca pautrāś ca śataśo atha sahasraśā ।। aditir ditir danuś caiva ariṣṭā surasā khasā ।। kadrur muniś ca dharmajña tadapatyāni me śṛṇu ।।
tān ahaṃ nāmato vakṣye śṛṇuṣva gadato mama ।। savitā caiva dhātā ca vivasvāṃś ca mahāmate ।। dityāḥ putradvayaṃ jajñe kaśyapād iti naḥ śrutaṃ ।। hiraṇyakaśipuś caiva narasiṃhena yo hataḥ ।।
ariṣṭāyāṃ tu gandharvā jajñire kaśyapāt tathā ।। gā vai sa janayāmasa surabhyāṃ kaśyapo muniḥ ।। garuḍo devadevasya viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ ।। tāmrāyāṃ kaśyapāj jātāḥ ṣaṭ putrās tān nibodha me ।।
krodhāyāṃ jajñire tadvad ye bhūmyāṃ duṣṭajātayaḥ ।। khasā tu yakṣarakṣāṃsi munir apsarasas tathā ।। saptaviṃśati yāḥ proktāḥ somapatnyo atha savratāḥ ।। ariṣṭanemipatnīnām apatyānīha ṣoḍaśa ।।
pratyaṅgirassutāḥ śreṣṭhā ṛṣayaś carṣisatkṛtāḥ ।। ete yugasahasrānte jāyante punar eva hi ।। sthitau sthitasya devasya narasiṃhasya dharmataḥ ।। kathitā dakṣakanyānāṃ mayā te apatyasaṃtatiḥ ।।
śraddhāvān saṃsmared etāṃ sa susaṃtānavān bhavet ।। paṭhanti ye viṣṇuparāḥ sadā narā idaṃ dvijās te vimalā bhavanti ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sṛṣṭikathane pañcamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। devadānavayakṣādyā yathotpannā mahātmanaḥ ।।
mitrāvaruṇaputratvaṃ vasiṣṭhasya kathaṃ tv iti ।। śṛṇuṣvaikāgramanasā bharadvāja viśeṣataḥ ।। pāragaḥ sarvavidyānāṃ dakṣo nāma prajāpatiḥ ।। sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇāḥ kaśyapāya trayodaśa ।।
aditir ditir danuḥ kālā muhūrtā siṃhikā muniḥ ।। kadrū saramā caiva yā tu devaśunī smṛtā ।। tāsāṃ jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā ca aditir nāmato dvija ।। teṣāṃ nāmāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣva gadato mama ।।
bhago aṃśus tv aryamā caiva mitro atha varuṇas tathā ।। tvaṣṭā pūṣā tathaivendro viṣṇur dvādaśamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tasyāś ca madhyamaḥ putro varuṇo nāma nāmataḥ ।। paścimasya samudrasya pratīcyāṃ diśi rājate ।।
sarvaratnamayaiḥ śṛṅgair dhātuprasravaṇānvitaiḥ ।। mahādarīguhābhiś ca siṃhaśārdūlanāditaḥ ।। yasmin gate dinakare tamasāpūryate jagat ।। ramyā maṇimayaiḥ stambhair vihitā viśvakarmaṇā ।।
tasyāṃ varuṇa ādityo dīpyamānaḥ svatejasā ।। upāsyamāno gandharvais tathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।। kadācid varuṇo yāto mitreṇa sahito vanam ।। nānāpuṣpaphalopete nānātīrthasamākule ।।
tasmiṃs tīrthe samāśritya bahupuṣpaphalodake ।। tatraikasmin vanoddeśe vimalodo hradaḥ śubhaḥ ।। nānātaruvanacchanno nalinyā copaśobhitaḥ ।। taṃ tu deśaṃ gatau devau vicarantau yadṛcchayā ।।
gāyantī ca hasantī ca viśvastā nirjane vane ।। padmapatraviśālākṣī raktauṣṭhī mṛdubhāṣiṇī ।। subhrūḥ sunāsā sumukhī sulalāṭā manasvinī ।। madhurālāpacaturā sumadhyā cāruhāsinī ।।
pūrṇacandranibhā bālā mattadviradagāminī ।। tasyā hāsyena lāsyena smitena lalitena ca ।। mattabhramaragītena puṃskokilarutena ca ।। nimeḥ śāpād athotkramya svadehān munisattama ।।
retas tribhāgaṃ kamale acarat tad vasiṣṭha evaṃ tu pitāmahokteḥ ।। sthale tv agastyaḥ saṃbhūto jale matsyo mahādyutiḥ ।। sthānatraye tat patitaṃ samānaṃ mitrasya yasmād varuṇasya retaḥ ।। yamāv api tu tapyete punar ugraṃ paraṃ tapaḥ ।।
tapasyantau suraśreṣṭhau brahmāgatyedam abravīt ।। siddhir bhaviṣyati yathā yuvayor vaiṣṇavī punaḥ ।। ity uktvāntardadhe brahmā tau sthitau svādhikārakau ।। mitrāvaruṇaputratvam agastyasya ca dhīmataḥ ।।
acirād eva putrāṃs te labhante nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। devāś ca pitaras tasya tṛptā yānti paraṃ sukham ।। nandate sa sukhaṃ bhūmau viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। paṭhiṣyate yas tu śṛṇoti sarvadā sa yāti śuddho harilokam añjasā ।।
।। iti śrinarasiṃhapurāṇe puṃsavanākhyānaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭho adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। etad ākhyāhi me sūta tvayaitat sūcitaṃ purā ।। śṛṇvantu ṛṣayaś ceme purāvṛttaṃ bravīmy aham ।। tatrāsīnaṃ munivaraṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ munim ।।
vedavedārthatattvajñaṃ sarvaśāstraviśāradam ।। imam evārtham uddiśya taṃ papraccha kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। narasiṃhasya bhaktena kṛtatīrthanivāsinā ।। etad ākhyāhi me tāta śrotum icchāmi te adhunā ।।
tathā te kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu vatsa mahāmate ।। macchiṣyāś caiva śṛṇvantu mahad ākhyānam uttamam ।। sumitrā nāma vai patnī mṛkaṇḍos tu mahātmanaḥ ।। tasyāṃ tasya suto jāto mārkaṇḍeyo mahāmatiḥ ।।
vavṛdhe vallabho bālaḥ pitrā tatra kṛtakriyaḥ ।। varṣe dvādaśame pūrṇe mṛtyur asya bhaviṣyati ।। vidūyamānahṛdayau taṃ nirīkṣya mahāmate ।। cakāra sarvāṃ medhāvī upanīto guror gṛhe ।।
svīkṛtya vedaśāstrāṇi sa punar gṛham āgataḥ ।। tasthau tatra gṛhe dhīmān mārkaṇḍeyo mahāmuniḥ ।। duḥkhitau tau bhṛśaṃ tatra tanmātāpitarau śucā ।। uvāca vacanaṃ tatra kimarthaṃ duḥkham īdṛśam ।।
vaktum arhasi duḥkhasya kāraṇaṃ mama pṛcchataḥ ।। kathayāmasa tat sarvam āgamī yad uvāca ha ।। pitrā sārdhaṃ tvayā mātar na kāryaṃ duḥkham aṇv api ।। yathā cāhaṃ cirāyuḥ syāṃ tathā kuryām ahaṃ tapaḥ ।।
vallīvaṭaṃ nāma vanaṃ nānāṛṣiniṣevitam ।। bhṛguṃ dadarśa dharmajñaṃ mārkaṇḍeyo mahāmatiḥ ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā tasthau tatpurato damī ।। bhṛgur āha mahābhāgaṃ mārkaṇḍeyaṃ tadā śiśum ।।
mātuś ca bāndhavānāṃ ca kim āgamanakāraṇam ।। uvāca sakalaṃ tasmai ādeśivacanaṃ tadā ।। evaṃ sati mahābuddhe kiṃ tvaṃ karma cikīrṣasi ।। śaraṇaṃ tvāṃ prapanno asmi tatropāyaṃ vadasva naḥ ।।
ko jetuṃ śaknuyān mṛtyuṃ tasmāt taṃ tapasārcaya ।। bhaktapriyaṃ suraśreṣṭhaṃ bhaktyā tvaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ।। tapasā mahatā vatsa nārāyaṇam anāmayam ।। jarāṃ mṛtyuṃ vijityāśu dīrghāyur vardhate sukham ।।
kaḥ kuryān mānavo vatsa mṛtyusattānivāraṇam ।। govindaṃ gopatiṃ devaṃ satataṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ।। vatsa jetāsi mṛtyuṃ tvaṃ satataṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। mārkaṇḍeyo mahātejā vinayāt svapitāmaham ।।
yenāsau mama tuṣṭas tu mṛtyuṃ sadyo apaneṣyati ।। tatra bhadravaṭe vatsa tvaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya keśavam ।। hṛdi kṛtvendriyagrāmaṃ manaḥ saṃyamya tattvataḥ ।। dhyāyann ekamanā vatsa dvādaśākṣaram abhyasan ।।
oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya । prīto bhavati viśvātmā mṛtyuṃ yenāpaneṣyati ।। ityuktas taṃ praṇamyātha sa jagāma tapovanam ।। nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ nānāpuṣpopaśobhitam ।।
tatra viṣṇuṃ pratiṣṭhāpya gandhadhūpādibhiḥ kramāt ।। pūjayitvā hariṃ tatra tapas tepe suduṣkaram ।। mātroktakāle tv āsanne dine tatra mahāmatiḥ ।। hṛdi kṛtvendriyagrāmaṃ viśuddhenāntarātmanā ।।
oṃkāroccāraṇād dhīmān hṛtpadmaṃ sa vikāsayan ।। kalpayitvā hareḥ pīṭhaṃ tasmin deśe sanātanam ।। bhāvapuṣpaiḥ samabhyarcya manas tasmin niveśya ca ।। oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya ।।
manas tatraiva saṃlagnaṃ devadeve jagatpatau ।। pāśahastās tu taṃ netuṃ viṣṇudūtais tu te hatāḥ ।। vayaṃ nivartya gacchāmo mṛtyur evāgamiṣyati ।। ko yamas tatra mṛtyur vā kālaḥ kalayatāṃ varaḥ ।।
mārkaṇḍeyasya babhrāma viṣṇukiṃkaraśaṅkayā ।। viṣṇvājñayā haniṣyāmo mṛtyum adyeti saṃsthitāḥ ।। tuṣṭāva praṇato bhūtvā devadevaṃ janārdanam ।। subhāṣitena manasā tena tuṣṭāva mādhavam ।।
praṇato asmi hṛṣīkeśaṃ kiṃ me mṛtyuḥ kariṣyati ।। keśavaṃ ca prapanno asmi kiṃ me mṛtyuḥ kariṣyati ।। dāmodaraṃ prapanno asmi kiṃ me mṛtyuḥ kariṣyati ।। adhokṣajaṃ prapanno asmi kiṃ me mṛtyuḥ kariṣyati ।।
mādhavaṃ ca prapanno asmi kiṃ me mṛtyuḥ kariṣyati ।। lokanāthaṃ prapanno asmi kiṃ me mṛtyuḥ kariṣyati ।। viśvarūpaṃ prapanno asmi kiṃ me mṛtyuḥ kariṣyati ।। mahāyogaṃ prapanno asmi kiṃ me mṛtyuḥ kariṣyati ।।
apayātas tato mṛtyur viṣṇudūtaiś ca pīḍitaḥ ।। prasanne puṇḍarīkākṣe nṛsiṃhe nāsti durlabham ।। mārkaṇḍeyahitārthāya svayaṃ viṣṇur uvāca ha ।। nākāle tasya mṛtyuḥ syān narasyācyutacetasaḥ ।।
saṃcintya sūryād api rājamānaṃ mṛtyuṃ sa yogī jitavāṃs tadaiva ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe mārkaṇḍeyamṛtyuṃjayo nāma saptamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। svarājñas te anu nirveśaṃ gatvā te cukruśur bhṛśam ।। tvadādeśād vayaṃ gatvā mṛtyuṃ saṃsthāpya dūrataḥ ।।
taṃ dhyāyamānaṃ kamapi devam ekāgramānasam ।। yāvat tāvan mahākāyaiḥ puruṣair muśalair hatāḥ ।। asmān nirbhartsya tatrāyaṃ tair narair muśalair hataḥ ।। aśaktā vayam evātra mṛtyunā saha vai prabho ।।
devaṃ kaṃ dhyāyate vipraḥ ke vā te yair hatā vayam ।। dhyātvā kṣaṇaṃ mahābuddhiḥ prāha vaivasvato yamaḥ ।। satyam etat pravakṣyāmi jñānaṃ yad yogamārgataḥ ।। sa jñātvādyātmanaḥ kālaṃ gato mṛtyujigīṣayā ।।
harim ārādhya medhāvī japan vai dvādaśākṣaram ।। satataṃ yogayuktas tu sa munis tatra kiṃkarāḥ ।। nānyad vai prāptakālasya balaṃ paśyāmi kiṃkarāḥ ।। paśyan taṃ viṣṇubhūtaṃ nu ko hi syāt keśavāśrayam ।।
ata ūrdhvaṃ na gantavyaṃ yatra vai vaiṣṇavāḥ sthitāḥ ।। bhavatāṃ jīvanaṃ citraṃ yakṣair dattaṃ kṛpālubhiḥ ।। samānetuṃ kṛto yatnaḥ samīcīnaṃ na tat kṛtam ।। teṣāṃ pārśve na gantavyaṃ yuṣmābhir mama śāsanāt ।।
yamo nirīkṣya ca janaṃ narakasthaṃ prapīḍitam ।। janasyānugrahārthāya tenoktāś ca giraḥ śṛṇu ।। kiṃ tvayā nārcito devaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ ।। yo dadāti svakaṃ lokaṃ sa tvayā kiṃ na pūjitaḥ ।।
smaraṇān muktido nṛṇāṃ sa tvayā kiṃ na pūjitaḥ ।। vaivasvato yamaḥ sākṣād viṣṇubhaktisamanvitaḥ ।। anyebhyo vaiṣṇavebhyaś ca siddhebhyaḥ satataṃ śrutam ।। śikṣārthaṃ kiṃkarāḥ sarve śṛṇuta praṇatā hareḥ ।।
jalaṃ bhittvā yathā padmaṃ narakād uddharāmy aham ।। tvām ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ prāpta iti yas taṃ samuddhare ।। iti yaḥ śaraṇaṃ prāptas taṃ kleśād uddharāmy aham ।। nārakāḥ kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti nārasiṃheti cukruśuḥ ।।
tathā tathā harer bhaktim udvahanto abruvann idam ।। yannāmakīrtanāt sadyo narakāgniḥ praśāmyati ।। lokanāthāya śāntāya yajñeśāyādimūrtaye ।। nārāyaṇāya gurave śaṅkhacakragadābhṛte ।।
vārāhāyāpratarkyāya vedāṅgāya mahībhṛte ।। vāmanāya bahujñāya vedavedāṅgadhāriṇe ।। viṣṇave suranāthāya vyāpine paramātmane ।। jāmadagnyāya rāmāya duṣṭakṣatrāntakāriṇe ।।
asmān uddhara govinda pūtigandhān namo astu te ।। tadā sā nārakī pīḍā gatā teṣāṃ mahātmanām ।। divyagandhānuliptāṅgā divyābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ।। tarjayitvā yamabhaṭān nītās te keśavālayam ।।
viṣṇulokaṃ yamo bhūyo namaś cakre tadā harim ।। taṃ namāmi sadā devaṃ narasiṃham ahaṃ gurum ।। praṇāmaṃ ye api kurvanti tebhyo apīha namo namaḥ ।। punaḥ sa śikṣārtham athātmadūtān yamo hi vaktuṃ kṛtavān manaḥ svayam ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe yamagītā nāmāṣṭamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। parihara madhusūdanaprapannān prabhur aham anyanṛṇāṃ na vaiṣṇavānām ।। hariguruvimukhān praśāsmi martyān haricaraṇapraṇatān namas karomi ।। madhuvadhavaśago asmi na svatantraḥ prabhavati saṃyamane mamāpi kṛṣṇaḥ ।।
varṣaśatam apīha pacyamānaṃ vrajati na kāñcanatām ayaḥ kadācit ।। bhagavati ca harāv ananyacetā bhṛśamalino api virājate manuṣyaḥ ।। suragurusudṛḍhaprasādadau tau haricaraṇau smaratāpavargahetoḥ ।। ramayati kurute na mokṣamārgaṃ dahayati candanam āśu bhasmahetoḥ ।।
avihatagataye sanātanāya jagati janiṃ harate namo agrajāya ।। mucyate sarvapāpebhyo viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। punaḥ pravakṣyāmi purātanīṃ kathāṃ bhṛgos tu pautreṇa ca yā purā kṛtā ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe navamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
sa jagāma pitur gehaṃ mārkaṇḍeyo mahāmatiḥ ।। sa vedaśirasaṃ putram utpādya ca vidhānataḥ ।। śrāddhena tu pitṛn iṣṭvā annadānena cātithīn ।। mārkaṇḍeyo mahātejās tepe vaṭatale tapaḥ ।।
taṃ devaṃ draṣṭum icchan yaḥ sa tepe paramaṃ tapaḥ ।। ekadā tu mahātejā mārkaṇḍeyo mahāmatiḥ ।। śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ tuṣṭāva garuḍadhvajam ।। kṣitīśvarair arcitapādapaṅkajaṃ namāmi viṣṇuṃ puruṣaṃ purātanam ।।
śriyaḥ patiṃ śrīdharam īśam īśvaraṃ namāmi govindam anantavarcasam ।। sahasrasūryadyutimantam acyutaṃ namāmi bhaktyā harim ādyamādhavam ।। paraṃ parāṇām api kāraṇaṃ hariṃ namāmi lokatrayakarmasākṣiṇam ।। kṣīrodavīcīkaṇikāmbunokṣitaṃ taṃ śrīnivāsaṃ praṇato asmi keśavam ।।
samastalokārtiharaṃ hiraṇyakaṃ namāmi viṣṇuṃ satataṃ namāmi tam ।। yogeśvarair eva sadā namaskṛtaṃ namāmi bhaktyā satataṃ janārdanam ।। aṇor aṇīyāṃsam avṛddhim akṣayaṃ namāmi bhaktapriyam īśvaraṃ harim ।। mārkaṇḍeyaṃ mahābhāgaṃ tīrthe anu tapasi sthitam ।।
mādhavaḥ sarvatīrtheṣu yāvan na snānam ācareḥ ।। tad vada tvaṃ mama prītyā yo asi so asi namo astu te ।। nānyathā sarvatīrthānāṃ phalaṃ prāpsyasi suvrata ।। yena japtena sakalaṃ tīrthasnānaphalaṃ labhet ।।
jaya padmapalāśākṣa jaya govinda gopate ।। jaya padma hṛṣīkeśa jaya dāmodarācyuta ।। jaya śaṅkhagadāpāṇe jaya bhūdharasūkara ।। jaya yogeśa yogajña jaya yogapravarttaka ।।
kṛtapriya jaya jaya yajñeśa yajñāṅga jaya ।। jaya puṇyavatāṃ geha jaya vaidikabhājana ।। jaya sarvajña sarvātman jaya śaṃkara śāśvata ।। prasādaṃ kuru deveśa darśayādya svakāṃ tanum ।।
prādur babhūva bhagavān pītavāsā janārdanaḥ ।। tejasā dyotayan sarvā diśo viṣṇuḥ sanātanaḥ ।। prayātaḥ śirasā vaśyo bhaktyā sa bhṛgunandanaḥ ।। prabaddhasaṃpuṭakaro govindaṃ purataḥ stuvan ।।
namo astu te devadeva mahācitta mahākāya mahāprājña mahādeva mahākīrte brahmendracandrarudrārcitapādayugala śrīpadmahasta saṃmarditadaityadeha ।। anantabhogaśayanārpitasarvāṅga sanakasanandanasanatkumārādyair yogibhir nāsāgranyastalocanair anavaratam abhicintitamokṣatattva । gandharvavidyādharayakṣakiṃnarakiṃpuruṣair aharaho gīyamānadivyayaśaḥ ।। nṛsiṃha nārāyaṇa padmanābha govinda govardhanaguhānivāsa yogīśvara deveśvara jaleśvara maheśvara ।। yogadhara mahāmāyādhara vidyādhara yaśodhara kīrtidhara triguṇanivāsa tritattvadhara tretāgnidhara ।।
trivedabhāk triniketa trisuparṇa tridaṇḍadhara ।। snigdhameghābhārcitadyutivirājita pītāmbaradhara kirīṭakaṭakakeyūrahāramaṇiratnāṃśudīptividyotitasarvadiśa ।। kanakamaṇikuṇḍalamaṇḍitagaṇḍasthala madhusūdana viśvamūrte ।। lokanātha yajñeśvara yajñapriya tejomaya bhaktipriya vāsudeva duritāpahārārādhya puruṣottama namo astu te ।।
devadevaḥ prasannātmā mārkaṇḍeyam uvāca ha ।। stotrair api mahābuddhe naṣṭapāpo asi sāṃpratam ।। nātaptatapasā brahman draṣṭuṃ sādhyo aham añjasā ।। tvadbhaktim acalām ekāṃ mama dehi jagatpate ।।
cirāyuṣyaṃ hṛṣīkeśa yena tvāṃ ciram arcaye ।। bhaktir astv acalā te me vaiṣṇavī muktidāyinī ।। punas tvaṃ drakṣyase māṃ vai kṣīrābdhau yogaśāyinam ।। mārkaṇḍeyo api dharmātmā cintayan madhusūdanam ।।
vedaśāstrāṇi puṇyāni purāṇāny akhilāni ca ।। itihāsāni puṇyāni pitṛtattvaṃ ca sattamaḥ ।। bhraman samudraṃ sa jagāma draṣṭuṃ hariṃ sureśaṃ munir ugratejāḥ ।। kṣīrābdhim āsādya hariṃ sureśaṃ nāgendrabhoge kṛtanidram aikṣata ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe mārkaṇḍeyacaritre daśamo adhyāya ।। narp ।। mārkaṇḍeyo abhituṣṭāva bhogaparyaṅkaśāyinam ।। prasīda devadeveśa prasīda garuḍadhvaja ।। prasīda lokanāthādya prasīda parameśvara ।।
prasīda mandaradhara prasīda madhusūdana ।। prasīdādya mahādeva prasīda mama keśava ।। jaya viśva jayāvyakta jaya viṣṇo namo astu te ।। jaya kāla jayeśāna jaya sarva namo astu te ।।
jaya bhūtapate nātha jaya sarvapate vibho ।। jaya pāpaharānanta jaya janmajarāpaha ।। jaya kāmada kākutstha jaya mānada mādhava ।। jaya kuṅkumaraktābha jaya paṅkajalocana ।।
jaya deva jagannātha jaya devakinandana ।। jaya sundarasarvāṅga jaya vandya namo astu te ।। jaya kāmada bhaktānāṃ prabhaviṣṇo namo astu te ।। lokanātha namas te astu vīrabhadra namo astu te ।।
namo devādhidevāya namo nārāyaṇāya te ।। namas te narasiṃhāya namas te śārṅgadhāriṇe ।। namaḥ śivāya devāya namas te bhuvaneśvara ।। namas te sakalādhyakṣa namas te śrīdharāacyuta ।।
tvaṃ mātā sarvalokānāṃ tvam eva jagataḥ pitā ।। tvaṃ gurus tvaṃ gatiḥ sākṣī tvaṃ patis tvaṃ parāyaṇaḥ ।। tvaṃ śivas tvaṃ vasur dhātā tvaṃ brahmā tvaṃ sureśvaraḥ ।। tvaṃ dhṛtis tvaṃ śriyaḥ kāntis tvaṃ kṣamā tvaṃ dharādharaḥ ।।
tvam eva goptā sarvasya jagatas tvaṃ carācara ।। śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇe bho samuddhara mādhava ।। tvām eva bhaktyā satataṃ namāmi puruṣottamam ।। namāmi te vapur deva kalikalmaṣanāśanam ।।
cārupṛṣṭhaṃ mahābāhuṃ cārubhūṣaṇabhūṣitam ।। dīrghatuṅgamahāghrāṇaṃ nīlajīmūtasaṃnibham ।। subhrūlalāṭamukuṭaṃ snigdhadantaṃ sulocanam ।। vṛttakaṇṭhaṃ supīnāṃsaṃ sarasaṃ śrīdharaṃ harim ।।
unnatāṃsaṃ mahoraskaṃ karṇāntāyatalocanam ।। sarvalokavidhātāraṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ harim ।। viṣṇum acyutam īśānam anantaṃ puruṣottamam ।। varadaṃ kāmadaṃ kāntam anantaṃ sūnṛtaṃ śivam ।।
asminn ekārṇave ghore vāyuskambhitacañcale ।। vicitraśayane ramye sevite mandavāyunā ।। iha tvāṃ manasā sarvam idānīṃ dṛṣṭavān aham ।। ekodake nirālambe naṣṭasthāvarajaṅgame ।।
śītātapajarārogaśokatṛṣṇādibhiḥ sadā ।। śokamohagrahagrasto vicaran bhavasāgare ।। ekārṇave mahāghore dustare duḥkhapīḍitaḥ ।। prasīda sumahāmāya viṣṇo rājīvalocana ।।
ananyaśaraṇaṃ prāptam ato atra kulanandana ।। namas te puṇḍarīkākṣa purāṇapuruṣottama ।। mām uddhara mahābāho magne saṃsārasāgare ।। māṃ samuddhara govinda varadeśa namo astu te ।।
devadeva namas te astu śrīvallabha namo astu te ।। saṃsārārṇavamagnānāṃ prasīda madhusūdana ।। janārdanaṃ janmajarārtināśanaṃ sureśvaraṃ sundaram indirāpatim ।। taraṃgabhaṅgāyatakuntalaṃ hariṃ sukāntam īśaṃ praṇato asmi śāśvatam ।।
tāv eva kevalau ślāghyau yau tvatpūjākarau karau ।। tan me hara tvaṃ govinda vāsudeveti kīrtanāt ।। saṃtuṣṭaḥ prāha viśvātmā taṃ muniṃ garuḍadhvajaḥ ।। varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te prārthitaṃ dadmi te varam ।।
yadi tuṣṭo mamādya tvam anyad ekaṃ vṛṇomy aham ।। svarlokavasatiṃ tasya dehi deva jagatpate ।। tat sarvaṃ saphalaṃ jātam idānīṃ tava darśanāt ।। atraiva bhagavan nityaṃ janmamṛtyuvivarjitaḥ ।।
bhaktyā muktir bhavaty eva tava kālena sattama ।। mayi bhaktiṃ dṛḍhāṃ kṛtvā mama loke sa modate ।। tatra tatra sameṣyāmi dānto bhaktavaśo asmi bhoḥ ।। virarāma sa sarvatra paśyan viṣṇuṃ yatas tataḥ ।।
mārkaṇḍeyasya ca munes tenaivoktaṃ purā mama ।। te muktapāpā narasiṃhaloke vasanti bhaktair abhipūjyamānāḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe mārkaṇḍeyacaritaṃ nāma ekādaśo adhyāya ।। narp ।। avitṛptaḥ sa dharmātmā śuko vyāsam abhāṣata ।।
yena dṛṣṭo hariḥ sākṣād yena mṛtyuḥ parājitaḥ ।। puṇyāṃ pāpaharāṃ tāta tasmād anyat tu me vada ।। yat puṇyam ṛṣibhiḥ proktaṃ tan me vada mahāmate ।। puṇyaṃ yat syān muniśreṣṭha tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।।
yamyā ca saha saṃvādaṃ yamasya ca mahātmanaḥ ।। jajñāte sa yamaś caiva yamī cāpi yavīyasī ।। krīḍamānau svabhāvena svacchandagamanāv ubhau ।। yamī yamaṃ samāsādya svasā bhrātaram abravīt ।।
bhrātṛbhūtena kiṃ tasya svasur yo na patir bhavet ।। anāthāṃ nātham icchantīṃ svasāraṃ yo na nāthati ।। bhrāteti nocyate loke sa pumān munisattamaḥ ।। īkṣatas tu svasā bhrātuḥ kāmena paridahyate ।।
anyathāhaṃ mariṣyāmi tvām icchantī vicetanā ।। kāmāgninā bhṛśaṃ taptā pralīyāmy aṅga mā ciram ।। svena kāyena me kāyaṃ saṃyojayitum arhasi ।। akāryam iha kaḥ kuryāt pumān bhadre sucetanaḥ ।।
na bhrātā madanārtāyāḥ svasuḥ kāmaṃ prayacchati ।। paśūnām eṣa dharmaḥ syāt tiryagyonivatāṃ śubhe ।। mātṛgarbhe tathaivāyaṃ saṃyogo nau na duṣyati ।। svasāraṃ nirṛtī rakṣaḥ saṃgacchati ca nityaśaḥ ।।
pradhānapuruṣācīrṇaṃ loko ayam anuvartate ।। ninditaṃ varjayed yatnād etad dharmasya lakṣaṇam ।। sa yat pramāṇaṃ kurute lokas tad anuvartate ।। viruddhaṃ sarvadharmeṣu lokeṣu ca viśeṣataḥ ।।
tena sārdhaṃ pramodasva na te bhartā bhavāmy aham ।। munayaḥ pāpam āhus taṃ yaḥ svasāraṃ nigṛhṇati ।। yatra rūpaṃ vayaś caiva pṛthivyāṃ kva pratiṣṭhitam ।। ātmarūpaguṇopetāṃ na kāmayasi mohitām ।।
bāhubhyāṃ saṃpariṣvajya nivasāmi śucismitā ।। tasya devasya devī tvaṃ bhavethā varavarṇini ।। subhadrāṃ cārusarvāṅgīṃ saṃskṛtāṃ paricakṣate ।। paritāpaṃ mahāprājñe na kariṣye dṛḍhavrataḥ ।।
ataḥ pāpaṃ nu necchāmi dharmacitto dṛḍhavrataḥ ।। kṛtavān na yamaḥ kāryaṃ tena devatvam āptavān ।। anantaṃ phalam ity āhus teṣāṃ svargaphalaṃ bhavet ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ śrotavyam anasūyayā ।।
saṃtṛptāḥ pitaras tasya na viśanti yamālayam ।। vaivasvatībhyas tīvrābhyo yātanābhyaḥ pramucyate ।। purātanaṃ pāpaharaṃ sadā nṛṇāṃ kim anyad adyaiva vadāmi śaṃsa me ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe yamīyamasaṃvādo nāma dvādaśo adhyāya ।। narp ।।
anyāḥ puṇyāś ca me brūhi kathāḥ pāpapraṇāśinīḥ ।। pativratāyāḥ saṃvādaṃ kasyacid brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। sarvaśāstrārthatattvajño vyākhyāne pariniṣṭhitaḥ ।। ṛtukālābhigāmī ca agnihotraparāyaṇaḥ ।।
atithīn āgatān gehaṃ narasiṃhaṃ ca pujayat ।। pativratā mahābhāgā patyuḥ priyahite ratā ।। parokṣajñānam āpannā kalyāṇī guṇasaṃmatā ।। nandigrāme vasan dhīmān svānuṣṭhānaparāyaṇaḥ ।।
tasya bhāryābhavat sādhvī rohiṇī nāma nāmataḥ ।। sā prasūtā sutaṃ tv ekaṃ tasmād bhartur aninditā ।। jātakarma tadā cakre snātvā putrasya mantrataḥ ।। puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā tu nāma cakre yathāvidhi ।।
tathānnaprāśanaṃ ṣaṣṭhe māsi cakre yathāvidhi ।। kṛtvā garbhāṣṭame varṣe vratabandhaṃ cakāra saḥ ।। svīkṛte tv ekavede tu pitā svarlokam āsthitaḥ ।। dhairyam āsthāya medhāvī sādhubhiḥ preritaḥ punaḥ ।।
gaṅgādiṣu sutīrtheṣu snānaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi ।। saṃprāpya viśrutaḥ so atha brahmacārī mahāmate ।। kurvann evāgnikāryaṃ tu nandigrāme ca tasthivān ।। duḥkhād duḥkham anuprāptā niyataṃ rakṣakaṃ vinā ।।
kṣitau prasārya śoṣārthaṃ japann āsīta vāgyataḥ ।। tau dṛṣṭvā bhartsayāmasa devaśarmā tato dvijaḥ ।। roṣeṇa vīkṣayāmasa khe yāntau pakṣiṇau tu saḥ ।। sa dṛṣṭvā tau kṣitiṃ yātau pakṣiṇau vismayaṃ gataḥ ।।
iti matvā gato bhikṣām aṭituṃ grāmam añjasā ।। praviṣṭas tad gṛhaṃ vatsa gṛhe yatra pativratā ।। vāgyatā pūrvaṃ vijñāya bhartuḥ kṛtvānuśāsanam ।। āśvāsya svapatiṃ sā tu bhikṣāṃ dātuṃ pracakrame ।।
sāvitrī tu nirīkṣyaivaṃ hasantī sā tam abravīt ।। nadītīre adya kopātman bhikṣāṃ matto yadīcchasi ।। cintayan manasā tasyāḥ śaktiṃ dūrārthavedinīm ।। pativratāyāṃ bhuktāyāṃ gṛhasthe nirgate patau ।।
punar āgamya tadgehaṃ tām uvāca pativratām ।। b prabrūhy etan mahābhāge pṛcchato me yathārthataḥ ।। d ityuktā tena sā sādhvī sāvitrī tu pativratā ।। śṛṇuṣvāvahito brahman yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi ।।
strīṇāṃ tu patiśuśrūṣā dharma eṣa paristhitaḥ ।। divārātram asaṃdigdhaṃ śraddhayā paritoṣaṇam ।। anyac ca te pravakṣyāmi nibodha tvaṃ yadīcchasi ।। mṛte pitari kṛtvā tu pretakāryam ihāgataḥ ।।
anāthāṃ vidhavām atra nityaṃ svodaraposakaḥ ।। tāṃ tyaktvā vipine dharmaṃ caran vipra na lajjase ।। duḥkhitāṃ tāṃ gṛhe tyaktvā kiṃ bhaved vipine aṭataḥ ।। pitraiva saṃskṛto yasmāt tasmāc chaktir abhūd iyam ।।
vṛthā snānaṃ vṛthā tīrthaṃ vṛthā japtaṃ vṛthā hutam ।। yo rakṣet satataṃ bhaktyā mātaraṃ mātṛvatsalaḥ ।। mātuś ca vacanaṃ brahman pālitaṃ yair narottamaiḥ ।। atas tvaṃ tatra gatvādya yatra mātā vyavasthitā ।।
krodhaṃ parityajainaṃ tvaṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭavighātakam ।। yāthātathyena kathitam etat sarvaṃ mayā tava ।। ity uktvā virarāmātha dvijaputraṃ pativratā ।। ajñānāt kṛtapāpasya kṣamasva varavarṇini ।।
tat kṣamasva mahābhāge hitam uktaṃ pativrate ।। kāryāṇi tāni me brūhi yathā me sugatir bhavet ।। yāni kāryāṇi vakṣyāmi tvayā karmāṇi me śṛṇu ।। atra vā tatra vā brahman prāyaścittaṃ ca pakṣiṇoḥ ।।
tāṃ gṛhṇīṣva ca dharmeṇa gate tvayi sa dāsyati ।। yāyāvaradhanād vṛttiḥ pitṛvat te bhaviṣyati ।। narasiṃhaprasādena vaiṣṇavaṃ padam āpsyasi ।। manyase nānṛtaṃ tv etat kuru sarvaṃ hi me vacaḥ ।।
kariṣye tvadvacaḥ sarvaṃ tatra gatvā śubhekṣaṇe ।। saṃrakṣya mātaraṃ yatnāt krodhamohavivarjitaḥ ।। narasiṃhaprasādena parāṃ siddhim avāptavān ।। saṃsāravṛkṣaṃ ca nihatya bandhanaṃ chitvā ca viṣṇoḥ padam eti mānavaḥ ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe brahmacārisaṃvādo nāma trayodaśo adhyāya ।। narp ।। mayocyamānāṃ śṛṇvantu sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm ।। mṛtabhāryo gatas tīrthaṃ cakre snānaṃ yathāvidhi ।। bhikṣāhāraḥ pravasito japasnānaparāyaṇaḥ ।।
gayāṃ samāsādya pitṛn pitāmahān saṃtarpayan san gatavān mahendram ।। kṛtvā pitṛbhyas tu tathaiva tṛptiṃ vrajan vanaṃ pāpaharaṃ praviṣṭaḥ ।। śirasy aśeṣāghavināśinīṃ tadā viśuddhadehaḥ sa babhūva vipraḥ ।। ārādhya puṣpair girisaṃbhavair śubhais tatraiva siddhiṃ tv abhikāṅkṣya saṃsthitaḥ ।।
anāśramitvaṃ gṛhabhaṅgakāraṇaṃ hy ato gṛhāṇāśramam uttamaṃ dvija ।। tathāpi niṣṭhāṃ tava vīkṣya sattama tvayi prasannena mayety udīritam ।। harer alaṅghyaṃ narasiṃhamūrter bhādhaṃ ca kṛtvā sa yatir babhūva ।। japan sadā mantram apāstadoṣaṃ sāvitryam īśaṃ hṛdaye smaran harim ।।
abhyarcya viṣṇuṃ narasiṃhamūrtiṃ dhyātvā ca nityaṃ hṛdi śuddham ādyam ।। bāhyaṃ samastaṃ guṇam indriyāṇāṃ vilīya bhedaṃ bhagavaty anante ।। saṃcintya tasmin pravihāya dehaṃ babhūva muktaḥ paramātmarūpī ।। prayāgatīrthaplavane tu yat phalaṃ tat prāpya te yānti hareḥ padaṃ mahat ।।
saṃsāravṛkṣasya vināśanaṃ paraṃ punaḥ kam icchasy abhivāñchitaṃ vada ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe caturdaśo adhyāya ।। narp ।। saṃsāravṛkṣaṃ sakalaṃ yenedaṃ parivartate ।। nānyo vetti mahābhāga saṃsāroccāralakṣaṇam ।।
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prāha saṃsāratarulakṣaṇam ।। saṃsāravṛkṣaṃ vakṣyāmi yena cedaṃ samāvṛtam ।। buddhiskandhamayaś caiva indriyāṅkarakoṭaraḥ ।। dharmādharmasupuṣpaś ca sukhaduḥkhaphalodayaḥ ।।
etad brahma paraṃ caiva brahma vṛkṣasya tasya tat ।। vṛkṣaṃ enaṃ samārūḍhā moham āyānti dehinaḥ ।। prāyeṇa prākṛtā martyā brahmajñānaparāṅmukhāḥ ।। karmakriye mahāprājña nainaṃ chindanti duṣkṛtāḥ ।।
tato amaratvaṃ te yānti yasmān nāvartate punaḥ ।। toṣaṇaṃ narasiṃhasya jñānahīnaḥ paśuḥ pumān ।। jñānaṃ narāṇām adhikaṃ hi loke jñānena hīnāḥ paśubhiḥ samānāḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe pañcadaśo adhyāya ।। narp ।।
badhyamānaḥ sutaiśvaryaiḥ patito yonisāgare ।। baddhaḥ svakarmabhir gauṇaiḥ putradāraiṣaṇādibhiḥ ।। pṛcchām ākhyāhi me tāta tasya muktiṃ kathaṃ bhavet ।। tac ca vakṣyāmi te divyaṃ nāradena śrutaṃ purā ।।
svakarmabhir mahāduḥkhaṃ prāptā yatra yamālaye ।। ālokya nāradaḥ śīghraṃ gatvā yatra trilocanaḥ ।। praṇamya vidhivad devaṃ nāradaḥ paripṛcchati ।। śabdādiviṣayair baddhaḥ pīḍyamānaḥ ṣaḍūrmibhiḥ ।।
bhagavan brūhi me tattvaṃ śrotum icchāmi śaṃkara ।। uvāca tam ṛṣiṃ śaṃbhuḥ prasannavadano haraḥ ।। vakṣyāmi śṛṇu duḥkhaghnaṃ sarvabandhabhayāpaham ।। carācaraṃ jagat sarvaṃ prasuptaṃ yasya māyayā ।।
sa nistarati saṃsāraṃ devānām api dustaram ।। saṃsārasumahāpaṅke jīrṇā gaur iva majjati ।। tasya muktiṃ na paśyāmi janmakoṭiśatair api ।। ārādhayet sadā saṃyag dhyāyed viṣṇuṃ samāhitaḥ ।।
sarvajñam amalaṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। vāsudevam ajaṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। devagarbhaṃ vibhuṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। nirvāṇam anaghaṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।।
brahmaṇyaṃ śaṃkaraṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā saṃkīrtya mucyate ।। amātram avyayaṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। acintyam amalaṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। apratarkyam ajaṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।।
taṃ sarvahṛdgataṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। ekāgramanasā viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। śubhram ekākṣaraṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। ekaṃ nūtnaṃ sadā viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।।
sthānatrayātigaṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। yogibhiḥ sevitaṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। viśveśvaram ajaṃ viṣṇuṃ kīrtayann eva mucyate ।।
bhaktyaiva varadaṃ viṣṇuṃ sadā dhyāyan vimucyate ।। yad uvāca tadā tasmai tan mayā kathitaṃ tava ।। avāpsyasi dhruvaṃ tāta śāśvataṃ padam avyayam ।। sa viṣṇuṃ saṃyag ārādhya parāṃ siddhim avāptavān ।।
śatajanmakṛtaṃ pāpam api tasya praṇaśyati ।। prātaḥ snātvā paṭhen nityam amṛtatvaṃ sa gacchati ।। upāsakānāṃ prabhum īśvaraṃ paraṃ te yānti siddhiṃ paramāṃ tu vaiṣṇavīm ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe viṣṇoḥ stavarājanirūpaṇe ṣoḍaśo adhyāya ।। narp ।।
saṃsāraduḥkhāt sarveṣāṃ hitāya vada me pitaḥ ।। yaṃ japan mucyate martyo janmasaṃsārabandhanāt ।। ekāgramanasā dhyātvā viṣṇuṃ kuryāj japaṃ dvijaḥ ।। japed aṣṭākṣaraṃ mantraṃ citte viṣṇuṃ nidhāya vai ।।
chandaś ca daivī gāyatrī paramātmā ca devatā ।। mokāraṃ varṇataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ nākāraṃ raktam ucyate ।। ṇākāram añjanābhaṃ tu yakāraṃ bahuvarṇakam ।। vedānāṃ praṇayenaiṣa siddho mantraḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
enam aṣṭākṣaraṃ mantraṃ japan nārāyaṇaṃ smaret ।। eṣa eva paro mantra eṣa eva paraṃ tapaḥ ।। sarvavedarahasyebhyaḥ sāra eṣa samuddhṛtaḥ ।। evaṃ jñātvā tato vipro hy aṣṭākṣaram imaṃ smaret ।।
jape dāne ca home ca gamane dhyānaparvasu ।। japet sahasraṃ niyutaṃ śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ ।। snātvā śucir japed yas tu namo nārāyaṇaṃ śatam ।। gandhapuṣpādibhir viṣṇum anenārādhya yo japet ।।
hṛdi kṛtvā hariṃ devaṃ mantram enaṃ tu yo japet ।। prathamena tu lakṣeṇa ātmaśuddhir bhaviṣyati ।। tṛtīyena tu lakṣeṇa svargalokam avāpnuyāt ।। pañcamena tu lakṣeṇa nirmalaṃ jñānam āpnuyāt ।।
saptamena tu lakṣeṇa svarūpaṃ pratipadyate ।। svasvadharmasamāyuktaṃ japaṃ kuryād dvijottamaḥ ।। duḥsvapnāsurapaiśācā uragā brahmarākṣasāḥ ।। ekāgramanasāvyāgro viṣṇubhakto dṛḍhavrataḥ ।।
mantrāṇāṃ paramo mantro devatānāṃ ca daivatam ।। āyuṣyaṃ dhanaputrāṃś ca paśūn vidyāṃ mahad yaśaḥ ।। etat satyaṃ ca dharmyaṃ ca vedaśrutinidarśanāt ।। ṛṣayaḥ pitaro devāḥ siddhās tv asurarākṣasāḥ ।।
antakāle japann eti tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। śṛṇvantu bhavyamatayo muditās tvarāgā uccais tarām upadiśāmy aham ūrdhvabāhuḥ ।। he putra śiṣyāḥ śṛṇuta na mantro aṣṭākṣarāt paraḥ ।। vedāc chāstraṃ paraṃ nāsti na devaḥ keśavāt paraḥ ।।
idam ekaṃ suniṣpannaṃ dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā ।। kathāś ca vividhāḥ proktā mayā bhaja janārdanam ।। japa putra mahābuddhe yadi siddhim abhīpsasi ।। te dhautapāṇḍurapaṭā iva rājahaṃsāḥ saṃsārasāgaram apetabhayās taranti ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe aṣṭākṣaramantramāhātmyaṃ nāma saptadaśo adhyāya ।। narp ।। nānāvidhā muniśreṣṭhāḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāt punaḥ ।। siddhair anyaiś ca sahito nārāyaṇaparo abhavat ।। mayā vicitrāḥ pāpaghnyaḥ kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchasi ।।
aśvinor marutāṃ caiva noktotpattis tu tāṃ vada ।। purāṇe śaktiputreṇa purotpatiś ca vāyunā ।। saṃkṣepāt tava vakṣyāmi sṛṣṭim etāṃ śṛṇuṣva me ।। ḥdakṣakanyāditiḥ ।
ḥaditer ādityaḥ putraḥ । ḥtasmai tvaṣṭā duhitaraṃ saṃjñāṃ nāma kanyāṃ dattavān ।। so api tvāṣṭrīṃ rūpavatīṃ manojñāṃ prāpya tayā saha reme । sā katipayāt kālāt svabhartur ādityasya tāpam asahantī pitur gṛhaṃ jagāma ।। tām avalokya sutāṃ pitovāca kiṃ putri tava bhartā savitā snehāt tvāṃ rakṣaty uta paruṣa iti ।।
evaṃ pitur vacanaṃ śrutvā saṃjñā taṃ pratyuvāca । dagdhāhaṃ bhartuḥ pracaṇḍatāpād iti ।। evaṃ śrutvā tām āha pitā gaccha putri bhartur gṛham iti ।। yuvatīstrīṇāṃ bhartuḥ śuśrūṣaṇam eva dharmaḥ śreyān । aham api katipayadivasād āgatyādityasyoṣṇatāṃ jāmātur uddhariṣyāmi ।। ityuktā sā ca punar bhartur gṛhaṃ prāpya katipayadivasān manuṃ yamīṃ yamaṃ cāpatyatrayam ādityāt prāsūta । punas taduṣṇatām asahantī chāyāṃ bhartur apabhogāya svaprajñābalenotpādya tatra saṃsthāpya gatvottarakurūn adhiṣṭhāyāśvī bhūtvā vicacāra ।।
ādityo api saṃjñeyam iti matvā tasyāṃ jāyāṃ punar apatyatrayam utpādayāmasa ।। manuṃ śanaiścaraṃ tapatīṃ ca । sveṣv apatyeṣu pakṣapātena vartatīṃ chāyāṃ dṛṣṭvā yamaḥ svapitaram āha neyam asmanmāteti ।। pitāpi tac chrutvā bhāryāṃ prāha । sarveṣv apatyeṣu samam eva vartatām iti ।। punar api sveṣv apatyeṣu snehāt pravartatīṃ chāyāṃ dṛṣṭvā yamo yamī ca tāṃ bahuvidham apīttham uvāca । ādityasaṃnidhānāt tūṣṇīṃ babhūvataḥ ।।
tataś chāyā tayoḥ śāpaṃ dattavatī । yama tvaṃ pretarājo bhava yami tvaṃ yamunā nāma nadī bhavet ।। tataḥ krodhād ādityo api chāyāputrayoḥ śāpaṃ dattavān he putra śanaiścara tvaṃ graho bhava krūradṛṣṭir mandagāmī ca pāpagrahas tvaṃ ca ।। putri tapatī nāma nadī bhaveti athādityo dhyānam āsthāya saṃjñā kva sthiteti vicārayāmasa ।। sa dṛṣṭavān uttarakuruṣu dhyānacakṣuṣāśvībhūya vicarantī । svayaṃ cāśvarūpeṇa tatra gatvā tayā saha saṃparkaṃ kṛtavān ।।
tasyām evādityād aśvināv utpannau tayor atiśayavapuṣoḥ sākṣāt prajāpatir āgatya devatvaṃ yajñabhāgatvaṃ mukhyaṃ ca devānāṃ bhiṣajatvaṃ dattvā jagāma । ādityaś cāśvarūpaṃ vihāya svabhāryāṃ saṃjñāṃ tvāṣṭrīṃ svarūpadhāriṇīṃ nītvā svarūpam āsthāya divaṃ jagāma ।। viśvakarmā cāgatya ādityaṃ nāmabhiḥ stutvā tadatiśayoṣṇatāṃśatām apaśātayāmasa ।। puṇyā pavitrā pāpaghnī bharadvāja mahāmate ।। śrutvā tayor janma naraḥ pṛthivyāṃ bhavet surūpo divi modate ca ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe aśvinor utpattir nāma aṣṭādaśo adhyāya ।। narp ।। tāny ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi vada sūta vivasvataḥ ।। savitā tāni vakṣyāmi sarvapapaharāṇi te ।। timironmathanaḥ śaṃbhus tvaṣṭā mārtaṇḍa āśugaḥ ।।
agnigarbho aditeḥ putraḥ śaṃbhus timiranāśanaḥ ।। ātapī maṇḍalī mṛtyuḥ kapilaḥ sarvatāpanaḥ ।। aṃśumālī timirahā ṛgyajussāmabhāvitaḥ ।। yajñeśo gopatiḥ śrīmān bhūtajñaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ ।।
śuddho virocanaḥ keśī sahasrāṃśuḥ pratardanaḥ ।। durvijñeyagatiḥ śūras tejorāśir mahāyaśāḥ ।। prabhaviṣṇuḥ prakāśātmā jñānarāśiḥ prabhākaraḥ ।। vimalo vīryavān īśo yogajño yogabhāvanaḥ ।।
dhanadaḥ prāṇadaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kāmadaḥ kāmarūpadhṛk ।। vedagarbho vibhur vīraḥ śāntaḥ sāvitrivallabhaḥ ।। mahendro varuṇo dhātā viṣṇur agnir divākaraḥ ।। uvāca viśvakarmāṇaṃ prasanno bhagavān raviḥ ।।
tvadbuddhisthaṃ mayā jñātam evam auṣṇyaṃ śamaṃ vrajet ।। śāntoṣṇaḥ savitā tasya duhitur viśvakarmaṇaḥ ।। tvayā yasmāt stuto ahaṃ vai nāmnām aṣṭaśatena ca ।। ityukto bhānunā so atha viśvakarmābravīd idam ।।
etais tu nāmabhis yas tvāṃ naraḥ stoṣyati nityaśaḥ ।। tasya pāpakṣayaṃ deva kuru bhaktasya bhāskara ।। saṃjñāṃ viśaṅkāṃ ravimaṇḍalasthitāṃ kṛtvā jagāmātha raviṃ prasādya ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe ekonaviṃśo adhyāya ।। narp ।।
purā devāsure yuddhe devair indrādibhir diteḥ ।। putrāḥ parābhūtā ditiś ca vinaṣṭaputrā mahendradarpaharaṃ putram icchantī kaśyapam ṛṣiṃ svapatim ārādhayāmasa ।। sa ca tapasā saṃtuṣṭo garbhādhānaṃ cakāra tasyām । punas tām evam uktavān ।। yadi tvaṃ śuciḥ satī śaracchatam imaṃ garbhaṃ dhārayiṣyasi tataś ca mahendradarpahantā putro bhaviṣyati । ity evam uktā sā ca taṃ garbhaṃ dhārayāmasa ।।
indro api taj jñātvā vṛddhabrāhmaṇarūpeṇāgatya ditipārśvaṃ sthitavān । kiṃcid ūnapūrṇe varṣaśate pādaśaucam akṛtvā ditiḥ śayanam āruhya nidrāṃ gatā ।। so api labdhāvasaro vajrapāṇis tatkukṣiṃ praviśya vajreṇa taṃ garbhaṃ saptadhā ciccheda । so api tena pracchidyamāno ruroda ।। mā rodīr iti vadann indras tān saptadhaikaikaṃ ciccheda ।। saptadhā te sarve maruto yato jātamātrān mā rodīr ity uktavān । mahendrasya sahāyā amī maruto nāma devā babhūvuḥ ।।
viyanmukhānām api yaḥ paṭhed idaṃ śṛṇvaṃś ca bhaktyā harilokam eti saḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe viṃśatitamo adhyāya ।। narp ।। vaṃśamanvantare brūhi vaṃśānucaritaṃ ca me ।। saṃkṣepāt kathayiṣyāmi vaṃśamanvantarāṇi te ।।
śṛṇvantu munayaś ceme śrotum āgatya ye sthitāḥ ।। ādau tāvad brahmā brahmaṇo marīciḥ । marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ kaśyapād ādityaḥ ।। ḥādityān manuḥ । ḥmanor ikṣvākuḥ ikṣvākor vikukṣiḥ ।
ḥvikukṣer dyotaḥ dyotād veno venāt pṛthuḥ pṛthoḥ pṛthāśvaḥ ।। pṛthāśvād asaṃkhyātāśvaḥ । asaṃkhyātāśvān māndhātā ।। māndhātuḥ purukutsaḥ purukutsād dṛṣado dṛṣadād abhiśaṃbhuḥ ।। abhiśaṃbhor dāruṇo dāruṇāt sagaraḥ ।।
sagarād dharyaśvo haryaśvād dhārītaḥ ।। hārītād rohitāśvo rohitāśvād aṃśumān । aṃśumato bhagīrathaḥ ।। bhagīrathāt saudāsaḥ saudāsāc chatruṃdamaḥ ।। śatruṃdamād anaraṇyaḥ anaraṇyād dīrghabāhuḥ dīrghabāhor ajaḥ ।।
ajād daśarathaḥ । daśarathād rāmaḥ rāmāl lavaḥ lavāt padmaḥ ।। padmād anuparṇaḥ । anuparṇād vastrapāṇiḥ ।। ḥvastrapāṇeḥ śuddhodanaḥ । ḥśuddhodanād budhaḥ ।
ḥbudhād ādityavaṃśo nivartate ।। sūryavaṃśabhavās te prādhānyena prakīrtitāḥ । yair iyaṃ pṛthivī bhuktā dharmataḥ kṣatriyaiḥ purā ।। mayocyamānāñ chaśinaḥ samāhitaḥ śṛṇuṣva vaṃśe atha nṛpān anuttamān ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sūryavaṃśakathanaṃ nāmaikaviṃśo adhyāya ।। narp ।।
purāṇe vistareṇoktaṃ saṃkṣepāt kathaye adhunā ।। ādau tāvad brahmā । brahmaṇo mānasaḥ putro marīcir marīcer dākṣāyaṇyāṃ dākṣāyiṇyāṃ kaśyapaḥ ।। kaśyapād aditer ādityaḥ । ādityāt suvarṇalāyāṃ manuḥ ।। ḥmanor surūpāyāṃ somaḥ ।
ḥsomād rohiṇyāṃ budhaḥ । ḥbudhād ilāyāṃ purūravāḥ ।। purūravasa āyuḥ । āyo rūpavatyāṃ nahuṣaḥ ।। nahuṣāt pitṛvatyāṃ yayātiḥ । yayāteḥ śarmiṣṭhāyāṃ pūruḥ ।।
ḥpūror vaṃśadāyāṃ saṃpātiḥ । ḥsaṃpāter bhānudattāyāṃ sārvabhaumaḥ । ḥsārvabhaumasya vaidehyāṃ bhojaḥ ।। bhojasya liṅgāyāṃ duṣyantaḥ । duṣyantasya śakuntalāyāṃ bharataḥ ।।
bharatasya nandāyām ajamīḍhaḥ । ajamīḍhasya sudevyāṃ pṛśniḥ । pṛśner ugrasenāyāṃ prasaraḥ । ḥprasarasya bahurūpāyāṃ śaṃtanuḥ । ḥśaṃtanor yojanagandhāyāṃ vicitravīryaḥ । ḥvicitravīryasyāmbikāyāṃ pāṇḍuḥ ।।
pāṇḍoḥ kuntidevyām arjunaḥ । arjunāt subhadrāyām abhimanyuḥ ।। ḥabhimanyor uttarāyāṃ parīkṣitaḥ । ḥparīkṣitasya mātṛvatyāṃ janamejayaḥ । ḥjanamejayasya puṇyavatyāṃ śatānīkaḥ ।।
ḥśatānīkasya puṣpavatyāṃ sahasrānīkaḥ । ḥsahasrānīkasya mṛgavatyām udayanaḥ । ḥtasya vāsavadattāyāṃ naravāhanaḥ ।। naravāhanasyāśvamedhāyāṃ kṣemakaḥ । kṣemakāntāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ somavaṃśo nivartate ।।
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। vaṃśānukīrtanaṃ puṇyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ dattam akṣayam ।। śṛṇuṣva viprendra mayocyamānaṃ manvantaraṃ cāpi caturdaśākhyam ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe somavaṃśānukīrtanaṃ nāma dvāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
prathamaṃ tāvat svāyaṃbhuvaṃ manvantaraṃ tatsvarūpaṃ kathitam । sargādau svārociṣo nāma dvitīyo manuḥ ।। tasmin svārociṣe manvantare vipaścin nāma devendraḥ । pārāvatāḥ satuṣitā devāḥ ।। ūrjastambaḥ suprāṇo danto nirṛṣabho varīyān īśvaraḥ somaḥ saptarṣayaś caivaṃ kiṃpuruṣādyāḥ svārociṣasya manoḥ putrā rājāno bhavanti ।। ḥtṛtīya uttamo nāma manuḥ ।
ḥsudhāmānaḥ satyāḥ śivāḥ pratardanā vaṃśavartinaś ca devāḥ । ḥpañcaite dvādaśagaṇāḥ ।। teṣāṃ suśāntir indraḥ ।। vandyāḥ saptarṣayo abhavan । atra paraśucitrādyā manoḥ sutāḥ ।।
caturthas tāmaso nāma manuḥ । tatra manvantare surāḥ parāḥ satyā sudhiyaś ca saptaviṃśatikā gaṇāḥ ।। tatra bhṛśuṇḍī nāma devendraḥ । hiraṇyaromā devaśrīr ūrdhvabāhur devabāhuḥ sudhāmā ha parjanyo munir ity ete saptarṣayaḥ ।। jyotirdhāmā pṛthuḥ kāśyo agnir dhanaka ity ete tāmasasya manoḥ putrā rājānaḥ ।। pañcamo nāma raivato manuḥ ।
ḥtasyāntare amitā niratā vaikuṇṭhāḥ sumedhasa ity ete devagaṇāś caturdaśakā gaṇāḥ । ḥasurāntako nāma devendraḥ । ḥsaptakādyā manoḥ sutā rājāno vai babhūvuḥ ।। śāntaḥ śāntabhayo vidvāṃs tapasvī medhāvī sutapāḥ saptarṣayo abhavan ।।
ḥṣaṣṭhaś cākṣuṣo nāma manuḥ । ḥpuruśatadyumnapramukhās tasya sutā rājānaḥ । ḥsuśāntā āpyāḥ prasūtā bhavyāḥ prathitāś ca mahānubhāvāḥ lekhādyāḥ pañcaite hy aṣṭakā gaṇās tatra devāḥ ।। teṣām indro manojavaḥ । medhāḥ sumedhā virajā haviṣmān uttamo matimān nāmnā sahiṣṇuś caite saptarṣayaḥ ।।
saptamo vaivasvato manuḥ sāṃprataṃ vartate । tasya putrā ikṣvākuprabhṛtayaḥ kṣatriyā bhūbhujaḥ ।। ādityaviśvavasurudrādyā devāḥ puraṃdaro atra devendraḥ ।। vaśiṣṭhaḥ kaśyapo atrir jamadagnir gautamaviśvāmitrabharadvājāḥ saptarṣayo bhavanti ।। ḥbhaviṣyāṇi manvantarāṇi kathyante ।
ḥtad yathā ādityāt saṃjñāyāṃ jāto yo manuḥ pūrvoktaś chāyāyām utpanno manur dvitīyaḥ sa tu । ḥpūrvajasya sāvarṇasya manvantaraṃ sāvarṇikam aṣṭamaṃ śṛṇu ।। manuḥ sāvarṇo aṣṭamo bhavitā tatra sutapādyā devagaṇās teṣāṃ balir indro bhavitā ।। dīptimān gālavo nāma kṛpadrauṇivyāsarṣyaśṛṅgāś ca saptarṣayo bhavitāraḥ । virājorvarīyanirmokādyāḥ sāvarṇasya manoḥ sutā rājāno bhaviṣyanti ।।
navamo dakṣasāvarṇir manur bhavitā । dhṛtiḥ kīrtir dīptiḥ ketuḥ pañcahasto nirāmayaḥ pṛthuśravādyā dakṣasāvarṇā rājāno asya manoḥ putrāḥ ।। marīcigarbhāḥ sudharmāṇo haviṣmantas tatra devatāḥ । teṣāṃ indro adbhutaḥ ।। savanaḥ kṛtimān havyo vasumedhātithir jyotiṣmān ity ete saptarṣayaḥ ।। daśamo brahmasāvarṇir manur bhavitā ।
ḥviruddhādayas tatra devāḥ । ḥteṣāṃ śāntir indraḥ । ḥhaviṣmān sukṛtiḥ satyas tapomūrtir nābhāgaḥ pratimokaḥ saptaketur ity ete saptarṣayaḥ ।। sukṣetra uttamo bhūriṣeṇādayo brahmasāvarṇiputrā rājāno bhaviṣyanti ।।
ekādaśe manvantare dharmasāvarṇiko manuḥ ।। siṃhasavanādayo devagaṇāḥ । teṣāṃ divaspatir indraḥ ।। nirmohas tattvadarśī nikaṃpo nirutsāho dhṛtimān rucya ity ete saptarṣayaḥ । citrasenavicitrādyā dharmasāvarṇiputrā bhūbhṛto bhaviṣyanti ।। rudrasāvarṇir bhavitā dvādaśo manuḥ ।।
kṛtadhāmā tatrendro haritā rohitāḥ sumanasaḥ sukarmāṇaḥ sutapāś ca devāḥ ।। tapasvī cārutapās tapomūrtis taporatis tapodhṛtir jyotis tapa ity ete saptarṣayaḥ ।। devavān devaśreṣṭhādyās tasya manoḥ sutā bhūpālā bhaviṣyanti ।। ḥtrayodaśo rucir nāma manuḥ ।
ḥsragvī bāṇaḥ sudharmā prabhṛtayo devagaṇāḥ । ḥteṣām indra ṛṣabho nāma bhavitā ।। niścito agnitejā vapuṣmān dhṛṣṭo vāruṇir haviṣmān nahuṣo bhavya iti saptarṣayaḥ । sudharmā devānīkādayas tasya manoḥ putrāḥ pṛthvīśvarā bhaviṣyanti ।। ḥbhaumaś caturdaśo manur bhavitā ।
ḥsurucis tatrendraḥ । ḥcakṣuṣmantaḥ pavitrāḥ kaniṣṭhābhā devagaṇāḥ ।। agnibāhuśuciśukramādhavaśivābhīmajitaśvāsā ity ete saptarṣayaḥ । urugaṃbhīrabrahmādyās tasya manoḥ sutāḥ rājanaḥ ।। evaṃ te caturdaśa manvantarāṇi kathitāni । rājānaś ca yair iyaṃ vasudhā pālyate ।।
manvantare bhavanty ete śakrāś caivādhikāriṇaḥ ।। sahasrayugaparyantaḥ kālo gacchati vāsaraḥ ।। brahmarūpadharaḥ śete sarvātmā nṛhariḥ svayam ।। svamāyām āsthito vipra sarvarūpī janārdanaḥ ।।
yugavyavasthāṃ kurute sṛṣṭiṃ ca puruṣottamaḥ ।। vibhūtayas tasya sthitau sthitasya tasyaiva sarvaṃ tvam avehi vipra ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe trayoviṃśo adhyāya ।। narp ।। śṛṇvatām api pāpaghnaṃ sūryasomanṛpātmakam ।।
ikṣvākur nāma bhūpālaś caritaṃ tasya me śṛṇu ।। sarayūtīram āsādya ayodhyā nāma nāmataḥ ।। hastyaśvarathapattyoghair drumaiḥ kalpadrumaprabhaiḥ ।। virājamānā sarvatra suvibhaktacatuṣpathā ।।
padmotpalaśubhais toyair vāpībhir upaśobhitā ।। vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgaiś ca śabdair utkṛṣṭakair yutā ।। tathaivāmrakapitthādyair aśokair upaśobhitā ।। mallikāmālatījātipāṭalānāgacampakaḥ ।।
kvacic candanagandhādyair nāraṅgaiś ca suśobhitā ।। naranārībhir āḍhyābhī rūpadraviṇaprekṣaṇaiḥ ।। devatulyaprabhāyuktair nṛpaputraiś ca saṃyutā ।। vipraiḥ satkavibhir yuktā bṛhaspatisamaprabhaiḥ ।।
aśvair uccaiḥśravastulyair dantibhir diggajair iva ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā nāradaḥ ślokaṃ sabhāmadhye puroktavān ।। jātāyodhyādhikā svargāt kāmabhogasamanvitā ।। jitavān sarvabhūpālān dharmeṇa sa mahābalaḥ ।।
namadbhir bhaktibhītibhyāṃ pādau tasya kiṇīkṛtau ।। tejasendreṇa sadṛśo manoḥ sūnuḥ pratāpavan ।। pālayāmasa dharmātmā āsamudrāṃ mahīm imām ।। avajitya sutīkṣṇais tu tanmaṇḍalam athāharat ।।
dānaiś ca vividhair brahman rājekṣvākuḥ pratāpavān ।। babhāra padmām urasā bhaktiṃ cittena mādhave ।। śayānam apy anantaṃ tu kārayitvā paṭe amalam ।। gandhapuṣpādibhir nityaṃ reme dṛṣṭvā paṭe harim ।।
padmākṣaṃ pītavāsaṃ ca svapneṣv api sa dṛṣṭavān ।। pakṣapātaṃ ca tannāmni mṛge padme ca tādṛśe ।। atīva tṛṣṇā saṃjātā apūrvaiva hi sattama ।। cintayāmasa matimān rājyabhogam asāravat ।।
vairāgyajñānapūrveṇa loke asmin nāsti tatsamaḥ ।। vasiṣṭhaṃ paripapraccha tatropāyaṃ purohitam ।। draṣṭum icchāmy ahaṃ tatra upāyaṃ taṃ vadasva me ।। vasiṣṭhaḥ sarvadharmajñaḥ sadā tasya hite rataḥ ।।
tapasā sukṛteneha ārādhaya janārdanam ।। draṣṭuṃ na śakyate jātu tasmāt taṃ tapasārcaya ।। gālavapramukhānāṃ ca ṛṣīṇām asti cāśramaḥ ।। nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ nānāpuṣpasamākulam ।।
svarājyabhāraṃ vinyasya karmakāṇḍam api dvija ।। tapaḥsiddhyartham anvicchaṃs tasmāt tatra tapaḥ kuru ।। dhyāyan nārāyaṇaṃ devam imaṃ mantraṃ sadā japa ।। oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya ।
japtvainaṃ munayaḥ siddhiṃ parāṃ prāptāḥ purātanāḥ ।। adyāpi na nivartante dvādaśākṣaracintakāḥ ।। nṛpa saṃjapa tan mantraṃ draṣṭavyo madhusūdanaḥ ।। pṛcchataḥ sāṃprataṃ bhūyo yadīcchasi kuruṣva tat ।।
stutvā gaṇeśaṃ sumanobhir arcya gataḥ purāt svāt tapase dhṛtātmā ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe ikṣvākucaritraṃ caturviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। yathā tena tapas taptaṃ tan me vada mahāmate ।। raktāmbaradharo bhūtvā raktagandhānulepanaḥ ।।
raktacandanatoyena snānapūrvaṃ yathāvidhi ।। naivedyaṃ caiva hāridraṃ guḍakhaṇḍaghṛtaplutam ।। evaṃ suvidhinā pūjya vināyakam athāstavīt ।। b namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ stoṣye aham taṃ vināyakam ।। d
ekadantaṃ dvidantaṃ ca caturdantaṃ caturbhujam ।। āmbikeyaṃ śūrpakarṇaṃ pracaṇḍaṃ ca vināyakam ।। anarcito vighnakaraḥ sarvakāryeṣu yo nṛṇām ।। madamattaṃ virūpākṣaṃ bhaktavighnanivārakam ।।
baddhaṃ sunirmalaṃ śāntaṃ namasyāmi vināyakam ।। merumandararūpāya namaḥ kailāsavāsine ।। bhaktastutāya devāya namas tubhyaṃ vināyaka ।। gajarūpaṃ samāsthāya trāsitāḥ sarvadānavāḥ ।।
yatas tataḥ surair agre pūjyase tvaṃ bhavātmaja ।। kāryārthaṃ raktakusumai raktacandanavāribhiḥ ।। trikālaṃ ekakālaṃ vā pūjayen niyatāśanaḥ ।। rājyaṃ ca sarvavighneśa vaśaṃ kuryāt sarāṣṭrakam ।।
mayetthaṃ saṃstuto bhaktyā pūjitaś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। tat phalaṃ pūrṇam āpnoti stutvā devaṃ vināyakam ।। na ca vighno bhavet tasya jāto jātismaro bhavet ।। saṃvatsareṇa siddhiṃ ca labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
tāpasaṃ veṣam āsthāya tapaś cartum gato vanam ।। kaṭhināṃ tu tvacaṃ vārkṣīṃ kaṭyāṃ dhatte nṛpottamaḥ ।। akṣasūtram alaṃkāraṃ phalaiḥ padmasya śobhanam ।। tyaktvā jaṭākalāpaṃ tu taporthe bibhṛyān nṛpaḥ ।।
praviśya ca tapas tepe śākamūlaphalāśanaḥ ।। varṣākāle nirālambo hemante ca sarojale ।। mano viṣṇau samāveśya mantraṃ vai dvādaśākṣaram ।। āvir babhūva bhagavān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।।
praṇamya bhaktibhāvena stutyā ca paryatoṣayat ।। vedaśāstrārthaviduṣe caturvaktrāya te namaḥ ।। iti stuto jagatsraṣṭā brahmā prāha nṛpottamam ।। b tapasy abhirataṃ śāntaṃ tyaktarājyaṃ mahāsukham ।। d
lokaprakāśako rājan sūryas tava pitāmahaḥ ।। f kṛtavantau tapaḥ pūrvaṃ tīvraṃ pitṛpitāmahau ।। tapaḥ karoṣi ghoraṃ tvaṃ samācakṣva mahāmate ।। dṛṣṭum icchaṃs tapaścaryābalena madhusūdanam ।।
ityuktaḥ prāha rājānaṃ padmajanmā hasann iva ।। mādṛśair api no dṛśyaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ ।। niśānte pralaye lokān ninīya kamalekṣaṇaḥ ।। sanandanādyair munibhiḥ stūyamāno mahāmate ।।
tasmin padme śubhe rājan jāto ahaṃ vedavit purā ।। anantabhogaparyaṅke bhinnāñjananibhaṃ harim ।। divyaratnavicitrāṅgaṃ mukuṭena virājitam ।। sahasraphaṇamadhyasthair maṇibhir dīptimattaram ।।
duḥkhena mahatāviṣṭo babhūvāhaṃ nṛpottama ।। kautūhalena taṃ draṣṭuṃ nārāyaṇam anāmayam ।। śrīśaṃ punas tam evāhaṃ padmam āśritya cintayan ।। tato mām antarikṣasthā vāg uvācāśarīriṇī ।।
na dṛśyo bhagavān viṣṇus tapasā mahatāpi te ।। śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśanāgaparyaṅkaśāyinam ।। pratibhāniyataṃ rūpaṃ vimānasthaṃ mahāmate ।। tayetthaṃ codito rājaṃs tyaktvā taptam anukṣaṇam ।।
āvir babhūva manasi viśvakarmā prajāpatiḥ ।। vimānastho yathāpūrvaṃ mayā dṛṣṭo jale nṛpa ।। tatprasādāt tapaḥ śreṣṭhaṃ mayā jñānam anuttamam ।। tad ahaṃ te pravakṣyāmi hitaṃ nṛpavareśvara ।।
prajānāṃ pālanaṃ dharmas tapaś caiva mahībhṛtām ।। tatrārādhaya deveśaṃ bāhyārthair akhilaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। niṣkāmo nṛpaśārdūla prajā dharmeṇa pālaya ।। ity uktvā taṃ jagāmātha brahmalokaṃ pitāmahaḥ ।।
āvir babhūva purato vimānaṃ tan mahībhṛtaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā parayā bhaktyā natvā ca puruṣottamam ।। paurair janaiś ca nārībhir dṛṣṭaḥ śobhāsamanvitaiḥ ।। svamandire viśāle tu vimānaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ śubham ।।
mahiṣyaḥ śobhanā yās tu piṣṭvā tu haricandanam ।। paurāḥ karpūraṃ śrīkhaṇḍaṃ kuṅkumādy aguruṃ tathā ।। puṣpāṇi viṣṇuyogyāni dadur ānīya bhūpateḥ ।। trisaṃdhyaṃ parayā bhaktyā japaiḥ stotraiś ca vaiṣṇavaiḥ ।।
prekṣaṇair api śāstroktaiḥ prītaiś ca niśi jāgaraiḥ ।। yāgaiś ca toṣayitvā taṃ sarvadevamayaṃ harim ।। yajan yajñaṃ mahīṃ rakṣan sa kurvan keśavārcanam ।। dhyāyan vai kevalaṃ brahma prāptavān vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।।
vihāya saṃsāram anantaduḥkhaṃ jagāma tad viṣṇupadaṃ hi rājā ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe ikṣvākucarite pañcaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। ikṣvākor vikukṣināmaputraḥ । sa tu siddhe pitari maharṣibhir abhiṣikto dharmeṇa pṛthivīṃ pālayan vimānastham anantabhogaśāyinam acyutam ārādhya yāgair api devān iṣṭvā svaputraṃ rājye subāhum abhiṣicya divam āruroha । subāhor bhrājamānād udyoto abhigīyate । sa tu saptadvīpāṃ pṛthvīṃ dharmeṇa pālayitvā bhaktiṃ parāṃ nārāyaṇe pitāmahavat kṛtvā kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇair yajñeśvaraṃ niṣkāmena manaseṣṭvā nityaṃ nirañjanaṃ nirvikalpaṃ paraṃ jyotir amṛtākṣaraṃ paramātmarūpaṃ dhyātvā harim anantaṃ ca param ārādhya svargalokaṃ gataḥ ।। tasya yuvanāśvo yuvanāśvasya ca māndhātā putro abhavat । sa cābhiṣikto maharṣibhir nisargād eva viṣṇubhakto anantaśayanam acyutaṃ bhaktyārādhayan yāgaiś ca vividhair iṣṭvā saptadvīpavatīṃ pṛthivīṃ paripālya divaṃ gataḥ ।।
yasyaiṣa śloko gīyate । sarvaṃ tad yauvanāśvasya māndhātuḥ kṣetram ucyate ।। tasya purukuśyo abhavad yena devā brāhmaṇāś ca yāgadānaiḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ ।। purukuśyād dṛṣado dṛṣadād abhiśaṃbhuḥ । abhiśaṃbhor dāruṇo dāruṇāt sagaraḥ ।।
sagarād dharyaśvo haryaśvād dhārīto hārītād rohitāśvaḥ । rohitāśvād aṃśumān ।। aṃśumato bhagīrathaḥ । ḥyena mahatā tapasā purā divo gaṅgā aśeṣakalmaṣanāśinī caturvidhapuruṣārthadāyinī bhuvam ānītā । ḥasthiśarkarābhūtāḥ kapilamaharṣinirdagdhāś ca guravaḥ sagarākhyā gaṅgātoyasaṃspṛṣṭā divam āropitāḥ ।
ḥbhagīrathāt saudāsaḥ saudāsāt satrasavaḥ ।। satrasavād anaraṇyo anaraṇyād dīrghabāhuḥ ।। dīrghabāhor ajo ajād daśarathaḥ । tasya gṛhe rāvaṇavināśārthaṃ sākṣān nārāyaṇo avatīrṇo rāmaḥ ।। ḥsa tu pitṛvacanād bhrātṛbhāryāsahito daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ prāpya tapaś cacāra ।
ḥvane rāvaṇāpahṛtabhāryo bhrātrā saha duḥkhito anekakoṭivānaranāyakasugrīvasahāyo mahodadhau setuṃ nibadhya tair gatvā laṅkāṃ rāvaṇaṃ devakaṇṭakaṃ sabāndhavaṃ hatvā sītām ādāya punar ayodhyāṃ prāpya bharatābhiṣikto vibhīṣaṇāya laṅkārājyaṃ vimānaṃ vā dattvā taṃ preṣayāmasa । ḥsa tu parameśvaro vimānastho vibhīṣaṇena nīyamāno laṅkāyām api rākṣasapuryāṃ vastum anicchan puṇyāraṇyaṃ tatra sthāpitavān ।। tan nirīkṣya tatraiva mahāhibhogaśayane bhagavān śete । so api vibhīṣaṇas tatas tadvimānaṃ netum asamarthaḥ tadvacanāt svāṃ purīṃ jagāma ।। nārāyaṇasaṃnidhānān mahad vaiṣṇavaṃ kṣetram abhavad adyāpi dṛśyate ।
ḥrāmāl lavo lavāt padmaḥ padmād ṛtuparṇa ṛṭuparṇād astrapāṇiḥ । ḥastrapāṇeḥ śuddhodanaḥ śuddhodanād buddhaḥ । ḥbuddhād vaṃśo nivartate ।। purātanair yair vasudhā prapālitā yajñakriyābhiś ca divaukasair nṛpaiḥ ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sūryavaṃśānucaritaṃ nāma ṣaḍviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। atha somavaṃśodbhavānāṃ bhūbhujāṃ saṃkṣepeṇa caritam ucyate ।। ādau tāvat samastaṃ trailokyaṃ kukṣau kṛtvā ekārṇave mahāmbhasi nāgabhogaśayane ।। ḥṛṅmayo yajurmayaḥ sāmamayo atharvamayo bhagavān nārāyaṇo yoganidrāṃ samārebhe ।
ḥtasya suptasya nābhau mahāpadmam ajāyata । ḥtasmin padme caturmukho brahmābhavat ।। ḥtasya brahmaṇo mānasaḥ putro atrir abhavat । ḥatrer anasūyāyāṃ somaḥ ।
ḥsa tu prajāpater dakṣasya trayastriṃśat kanyā rohiṇyādyā bhāryārthaṃ gṛhītvā priyāyāṃ jyeṣṭhāyāṃ viśeṣāt prasannamanāḥ rohiṇyāṃ budhaṃ putram utpādayāmasa ।। ḥbudho api sarvaśāstrajñaḥ pratiṣṭhāne pure avasat । ḥilāyāṃ purūravasaṃ putram utpādayāmasa । ḥtasyātiśayarūpānvitasya svargabhogān vihāya urvaśī bahukālaṃ bhāryā babhūva ।।
purūravasaḥ urvaśyām āyuḥ putro jajñe । sa tu rājyaṃ dharmataḥ kṛtvā divam āruroha ।। ḥāyo rūpavatyāṃ nahuṣaḥ putro abhavat । ḥyenendratvaṃ prāptam । ḥnahuṣasyāpi pitṛmatyāṃ yayātiḥ ।।
yasya vaṃśajā vṛṣṇayaḥ । yayāteḥ śarmiṣṭhāyāṃ pūrur abhavat ।। pūror vaṃśadāyāṃ saṃyātiḥ putro abhavat । yasya pṛthivyāṃ saṃpannāḥ sarve kāmāḥ ।। saṃyāter bhānudattāyāṃ sārvabhaumaḥ । sa tu sarvāṃ pṛthivīṃ dharmeṇa paripālayan narasiṃhaṃ bhagavantam ārādhya yāgadānaiḥ siddhim āpa ।। tasya sārvabhaumasya vaidehyāṃ bhojaḥ । yasya vaṃśe purā devāsurasaṃgrāme viṣṇucakrahataḥ kālanemiḥ kaṃso bhūtvā vṛṣṇivaṃśajena vāsudevena ghātito nidhanaṃ gataḥ ।।
ḥtasya bhojasya kaliṅgāyāṃ duṣyantaḥ । ḥsa tu narasiṃhaṃ bhagavantam ārādhya tatprasādān niṣkaṇṭakaṃ rājyaṃ dharmeṇa kṛtvā divaṃ prāptavān । ḥduṣyantasya śakuntalāyāṃ bharataḥ sa tu dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kurvan kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ sarvadevatāmayaṃ bhagavantam ārādhya nivṛttādhikāro brahmadhyānaparo vaiṣṇave pare jyotiṣi layam avāpa ।। bharatasya ānandāyām ajamīḍhaḥ । sa ca paramavaiṣṇavo narasiṃham ārādhya jātaputro dharmeṇa kṛtarājyo viṣṇupuram āruroha ।।
ḥajamīḍhasya sudevyāṃ vṛṣṇiḥ putro abhavat । ḥso api bahuvarṣaṃ dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kurvan duṣṭanigrahaṃ śiṣṭaparipālanaṃ saptadvīpāṃ vaśe cakre । ḥvṛṣṇer ugrasenāyāṃ pratyañcaḥ putro babhūva ।। ḥso api dharmeṇa medinīṃ pālayan pratisaṃvatsaraṃ jyotiṣṭomaṃ cakāra ।
ḥnirvāṇam api labdhavān । ḥpratyañcasya bahurūpāyāṃ śāṃtanuḥ ।। tasya devadattasyandanārohaṇam aśakyaṃ babhūva purataḥ śakyaṃ ca ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe somavaṃśavarṇanaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
paścāc chaktiḥ kathaṃ cāsīt tasya vai tad vadasva naḥ ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ tad dhi caritaṃ śāṃtanor nṛṇām ।। nāradoktavidhānena pūjayāmasa mādhavam ।। rājñā śāṃtanunā vipra tasmāt syandanam uttamam ।।
kim iyaṃ me gatir bhagnā sahasā vai rathāt tataḥ ।। kiṃ viṣaṇṇaḥ sthito rājann iti pṛṣṭaḥ sa śāṃtanuḥ ।। ityukto nārado dhyātvā jñātvā tatkāraṇaṃ tataḥ ।। yatra kvāpi tvayā rājan narasiṃhasya vai dhruvam ।।
gatir bhagnā mahārāja śrūyatām atra kāraṇam ।। mālākāro ravir nāmnā tena vṛndāvanaṃ kṛtam ।। mallikāmālatījātibakulādīni sarvaśaḥ ।। alaṅghyam apraveśyaṃ ca kṛtvā cakre svakaṃ gṛham ।।
evaṃ kṛtvā nu vasato mālākārasya dhīmataḥ ।। bhāryayā saha puṣpāṇi samāhṛtya dine dine ।। dadau kāścid dvijebhyaś ca kāścid vikrīya poṣaṇam ।। atha svargād upāgamya indraputro rathena vai ।।
tadgandhalipsuḥ sarvāṇi vicityāhṛtya gacchati ।। nānyad dvāraṃ vanasyāsyālaṅghyaprākāram unnatam ।। ahaṃ śaktiṃ na paśyāmi kim idaṃ nu parīkṣaye ।। tathaivāgatya puṣpāṇi saṃgṛhītva gataḥ pumān ।।
tato nidrāṃ gataḥ svapne dṛṣṭavāṃs taṃ nṛkesarim ।। ānīya kṣipyatāṃ kṣipraṃ puṣpārāmasamīpataḥ ।। iti śrutvā harer vākyaṃ narasiṃhasya dhīmataḥ ।। so apy āgatya yathāpūrvaṃ rathenālakṣitena tu ।।
nirmālyaṃ laṅghayāmasa indrasūnur aniṣṭakṛt ।। uktaḥ sārathinā caiva rathasyārohaṇe tava ।। gacchāmi divam evāhaṃ tvaṃ bhūmyāṃ vasa māruha ।। pāpasya nodanaṃ tv atra karmaṇā yena me bhavet ।।
tad uktvā gaccha nākaṃ tvaṃ karmāsmān sārathe drutam ।। b rāmasattre kurukṣetre dvādaśābde tu nityaśaḥ ।। d ity uktvāsau gataḥ svargaṃ sārathir devasevitam ।। rāmasattre tathā kuryād dvijocchiṣṭasya mārjanam ।।
kas tvaṃ brūhi mahābhāga nityam ucchiṣṭamārjakaḥ ।। ityuktaḥ kathayitvā tu yathāvṛttam anukramāt ।। tasmāt tvam api bhūpāla brāhmaṇocchiṣṭam ādarāt ।। brāhmaṇebhyaḥ paraṃ nāsti sarvapāpaharaṃ param ।।
bhaviṣyati mahīpāla prāyaścitte kṛte tava ।। narasiṃhasya devasya tathānyeṣāṃ divaukasām ।। kṛtavān dvādaśābdaṃ tu āruroha rathaṃ ca tam ।। paścāt tasyaiva viprendra śaktir evam ajāyata ।।
puṇyaṃ tathā dvijānāṃ tu proktam ucchiṣṭamārjane ।। sa pāpabandhaṃ pravihāya bhuṅkte gavāṃ pradānasya phalaṃ divi sthitaḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe śāṃtanucaritaṃ nāmāṣṭaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। śaṃtanayor yojanagandhāyāṃ vicitravīryaḥ । sa tu hastināpure sthitvā prajāḥ svadharmeṇa pālayan devāṃś ca yāgaiḥ pitṛṃś ca śrāddhaiḥ saṃtarpya saṃjātaputro divam āruroha ।।
ḥvicitravīryasyāmbālikāyāṃ pāṇḍuḥ putro jajñe । ḥso api rājyaṃ dharmataḥ kṛtvā muniśāpāc charīraṃ vihāya devalokam avāpa । ḥtasya pāṇḍoḥ kuntidevyām arjunaḥ ।। sa tu mahatā tapasā śaṃkaraṃ toṣayitvā pāśupatam astram avāpya triviṣṭapādhipateḥ śatrūn nivātakavacān dānavān hatvā khāṇḍavavanam agner yathāruci nivedya tṛptāgnito divyān varān avāpya suyodhanena hṛtarājyo dharmabhīmanakulasahadevadraupadīsahito virāṭanagare ajñātavāsaṃ caritvā gograhe ca bhīṣmadroṇakṛpaduryodhanakarṇādīn jitvā samastagomaṇḍalaṃ nivartayitvā bhrātṛbhiḥ saha virāṭarājakṛtapūjo vāsudevasahitaḥ kurukṣetre dhārtarāṣṭrair bahubalair yuddhaṃ kurvan bhīṣmadroṇakṛpaśalyakarṇādibhir bhūriparākramaiḥ kṣatriyair nānādeśāgatair anekair api rājaputraiḥ saha duryodhanādīn dhārtarāṣṭrān hatvā svarājyaṃ prāpya dharmeṇa rājyaṃ paripālya bhrātṛbhiḥ saha mudito divam āruroha ।।
arjunasya subhadrāyām abhimanyuḥ । yena bhāratayuddhe cakravyūhaṃ praviśyānekabhūbhujo nidhanaṃ prāpitāḥ ।। abhimanyor uttarāyāṃ parīkṣitaḥ । so apy abhiṣikto vanaṃ gacchatā dharmaputreṇa rājyaṃ kṛtvā rājaputro nākaṃ saṃprāpya reme ।। parīkṣitān mātṛvatyāṃ janamejayaḥ । yena brahmahatyāvāraṇārthaṃ mahābhārataṃ vyāsaśiṣyād vaiśaṃpāyanāt sādyantaṃ śrutam ।। rājyaṃ ca dharmataḥ kṛtvā divam āruroha । janamejayasya puṣpavatyāṃ śatānīkaḥ ।।
sa tu dharmeṇa rājyaṃ kurvan saṃsāraduḥkhād viraktaḥ śaunakopadeśena kriyāyogena sakalalokanāthaṃ viṣṇum ārādhya niṣkāmo vaiṣṇavaṃ padam avāpa । tasya śatānīkasya phalavatyāṃ sahasrānīkaḥ ।। sa tu bāla evābhiṣikto narasiṃhe atyantaṃ bhaktimān abhavat । tasya caritam upariṣṭād bhaviṣyati ।। sahasrānīkasya mṛgavantyām udayanaḥ । so api rājyaṃ kṛtvā dharmato nārāyaṇam ārādhya tatpuram avāpa ।। ḥudayanasya vāsavadattāyāṃ naravāhanaḥ ।
ḥsa tu yathānyāyaṃ rājyaṃ kṛtvā divam avāpa । ḥnaravāhanasyāśvamedhadattāyāṃ kṣemakaḥ ।। sa ca rājyasthaḥ prajāḥ paripālya mlecchābhibhūte jagati jñānabalāt kalāpagrāmam āśritaḥ ।। sa saṃtatiṃ prāpya viśuddhakarmakṛd divaṃ samāsādya vasec ciraṃ sukhī ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe śaṃtanusaṃtativarṇanaṃ nāma ekonatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। saṃkṣepāt parvatākīrṇaṃ nadībhiś ca samantataḥ ।। ḥjambuplakṣaśālmalakuśakrauñcaśākapuṣkarasaṃjñāḥ sapta dvīpāḥ । ḥlakṣayojanapramāṇāj jambudvīpād uttarottaradviguṇāḥ ।
ḥlavaṇekṣurasasurāsarpirdadhidugdhasvacchodakasaṃjñaiḥ parasparaṃ dviguṇaiḥ saptasamudrair valayākārais te dvīpāḥ paridhiṣṭhitāḥ ।। yo asau manuputraḥ priyavrato nāma sa saptadvīpādhipatir babhūva । tasya agnīdhrādayo daśa putrā babhūvuḥ ।। ḥtrayaḥ pravrajitāḥ । ḥśiṣṭānāṃ saptānāṃ saptadvīpāḥ pitrā dattāḥ ।
ḥtatra jambudvīpādhipater agnīdhrasya nava putrāḥ jātāḥ ।। ramyo hiraṇyayaś caiva kurur bhadraś ca ketumān ।। ḥnavavarṣāḥ vibhajya putrebhyaḥ pitrā dattā vanaṃ praviśatā । ḥagnīdhrīyaṃ himāhvayam ।
ḥyasyādhipatir nābheḥ ṛṣabhaḥ putro babhūva ।। ṛṣabhād bharato bharatena cirakālaṃ dharmeṇa pālitatvād idaṃ bhārataṃ varṣam abhūt । ḥilāvṛtasya madhye meruḥ suvarṇamayaś caturaśītisahasrāṇi yojanāni tasyocchrāyaḥ । ḥṣoḍaśasahasram apy adhastād avagāḍhaḥ ।
ḥtaddviguṇo mūrdhni vistāraḥ ।। tanmadhye brahmaṇaḥ purī । aindryām indrasya cāmarāvatī । āgneyyām agnes tejovatī । yāmyāṃ yamasya saṃyamanī । nairṛtyāṃ nirṛter bhayaṃkarī । vāruṇyāṃ varuṇasya viśvāvatī । ḥvāyavyāṃ vāyor gandhavatī । ḥudīcyāṃ somasya vibhāvarīti ।
ḥnavavarṣānvitaṃ jambūdvīpaṃ puṇyaparvataiḥ puṇyanadībhir anvitam ।। kiṃpuruṣādīny aṣṭavarṣāṇi puṇyavatāṃ bhogasthānāni sākṣād bhāratavarṣam ekaṃ karmabhūmiś cāturvarṇyayutam ।। adhogatim ito vipra yānti vai pāpakāriṇaḥ ।। ye pāpakāriṇas tān viddhi pātālatale narake koṭisamanvitān ।।
ḥatha sapta kulaparvatāḥ kathyante । ḥmahendro malayaḥ śuktimān ṛṣyamūkaḥ sahyaparvato vindhyaḥ pāriyātraḥ । ḥity ete bhārate kulaparvatāḥ ।। narmadā surasā ṛṣikulyā bhīmarathī kṛṣṇāveṇī candrabhāgā tāmraparṇī ity etāḥ sapta nadyaḥ । gaṅgā yamunā godāvarī tuṅgabhadrā kāverī sarayūr ity etā mahānadyaḥ papaghnyaḥ ।।
lakṣayojanavistīrṇam idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tu bhāratam ।। ḥṛkṣadvīpādipuṇyā janapadāḥ । ḥniṣkāmā ye svadharmeṇa narasiṃhaṃ yajanti te tatra nivasanti । ḥadhikārakṣayān muktiṃ ca prāpnuvanti ।।
ḥjambvādyāḥ svādūdakāntāḥ sapta payodhayaḥ । ḥtataḥ parā hiraṇmayī bhūmiḥ । ḥtato lokālokaparvataḥ eṣa bhūrlokaḥ ।। asyopari antarikṣalokaḥ । khecarāṇāṃ ramyas tadūrdhvaṃ svargalokaḥ ।।
bhārate kṛtapuṇyānāṃ devānām api cālayam ।। yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi caturāśītim ucchritaḥ ।। tāvatpramāṇā pṛthivī parvatasya samantataḥ ।। nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ nānāpuṣpopaśobhitam ।।
madhyamaṃ sphāṭikaṃ śṛṅgaṃ vaiḍūryamaṇikāmayam ।। yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi niyutāni caturdaśa ।। aprabhāntaritaṃ śṛṅgaṃ mūrdhni chatrākṛti sthitam ।। triviṣṭapo nākapṛṣṭhe hy apsarāḥ santi nirvṛtāḥ ।।
śvetaś ca pauṣṭikaś caiva upaśobhanamanmathau ।। nirmamo nirahaṃkāraḥ saubhāgyaś cātinirmalaḥ ।। ekaviṃśāni svargā vai niviṣṭā merumūrdhani ।। tat teṣu nivasanti sma janāḥ krodhavivarjitāḥ ।।
bhṛguprapāte saukhyaṃ ca raṇaṃ caivāsya nirmalam ।। ṛtuyājī nākapṛṣṭhaṃ agnihotrī ca nirvṛtim ।। suvarṇadāyī saubhāgyaṃ labhan svargaṃ tapaḥ phalam ।। sarvasattvahitārthāya svargaṃ so apsarasaṃ labhet ।।
bhūmidānena śuddhena labhate śāntikaṃ padam ।। aśvadānena puṇyāhaṃ kanyādānena maṅgalam ।। śvetaṃ tu labhate svargaṃ yatra gatvā na śocate ।। govṛṣasya pradānena svargaṃ manmathām āpnuyāt ।।
chatropānahadātā ca svargaṃ yāty upaśobhanam ।। tīrthayātrāparaś caiva svargarāje mahīyate ।। upavāsī trirātrādyaiḥ śāntaḥ svargaṃ śubhaṃ labhet ।। vidyādānena medhāvī nirahaṃkāram āpnuyāt ।।
tat tat svargam avāpnoti yad yad icchati mānavaḥ ।। narakād uddharanty ete jayavāhanadohanāt ।। saṃprāpya na nivarteta svargaṃ śāntam anāmayam ।। pūrvaśṛṅge svayaṃ viṣṇuḥ madhye caiva śivaḥ sthitaḥ ।।
vimalaṃ vipulaṃ buddham upary upari saṃsthitaḥ ।। tṛtīye siddhagandharvās turye vidyādharā dvija ।। navame tu tathā dakṣa ādityo daśame pathi ।। yojanānāṃ sahasre dve viṣṭambhanasamaṃ tataḥ ।।
mahendrasyāmarāvatyāṃ tadā tiṣṭhati bhāskaraḥ ।। tadā saṃyamane yāmye tatrodyaṃs tu pradṛśyate ।। dhruvādhāras tathottiṣṭhan vālikhilyādibhiḥ stutaḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe bhūgolakathane triṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
vicintya kathayāśu tvaṃ sūta jīva samāḥ śatam ।। tasya kṣitipater vipra dvau sutau saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।। madhyesabhaṃ narapater upaviṣṭasya caikadā ।। dhruvo dhātreyikāputraiḥ samaṃ vinayatatparaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvottamaṃ tadutsaṅge niviṣṭaṃ janakasya vai ।। ārurukṣum avekṣyāmuṃ surucir dhruvam abravīt ।। bāla bāliśabuddhitvād abhāgyājāṭharodbhavaḥ ।। asmin siṃhāsane sthātuṃ sukṛtaṃ kiṃ tvayā kṛtam ।।
anenaivānumānena budhyasva svalpapuṇyatām ।। sukukṣijaṃ amuṃ paśya tvam uttamam anuttamam ।। adhijānu dharājaner mānena paribṛṃhitam ।। b madhyerājasabhaṃ bālas tayeti paribhartsitaḥ ।। d
ucitaṃ nocitaṃ kiṃcin nocivān so api pārthivaḥ ।। visarjitasabhālokaṃ śokaṃ saṃhṛtya ceṣṭitaiḥ ।। sunītir nītinilayam avalokyātha bālakam ।। atha dṛṣṭvā sunītiṃ tu raho antaḥpuravāsinīm ।।
sāntvayitvā sunītis taṃ vadanaṃ parimārjya ca ।। papraccha tanayaṃ mātā vada rodanakāraṇam ।। vidyamāne narapatau śiśo kenāpamānitaḥ ।। b saṃpṛcche janani tvāhaṃ saṃyak śaṃsa mamāgrataḥ ।। d
kathaṃ na bhavatī mātaḥ priyā kṣitipater asi ।। kumāratve api sāmānye kathaṃ cāham anuttamaḥ ।। kathaṃ nṛpāsanaṃ yogyam uttamasya kathaṃ na me ।। iti śrutvā vacas tasya sunītir nītimacchiśoḥ ।।
svabhāvamadhurāṃ vāṇīṃ vaktuṃ samupacakrame ।। nivedayāmi te sarvaṃ māvamāne matiṃ kṛthāḥ ।। yadi sā mahiṣī rājño rājñīnām ativallabhā ।। uvāsa tasyāḥ puṇyāyā nṛpasiṃhāsanocitaḥ ।।
bhadrāsanaṃ tathoccaṃ ca sindhurāś ca madotkaṭāḥ ।। niḥsapatnaṃ śubhaṃ rājyaṃ prāpyaṃ viṣṇuprasādataḥ ।। saunīteyo dhruvo vācam ādade vaktum uttaram ।। uttānacaraṇād anyan nāstīti me matiḥ śubhe ।।
adyaiva sakalārādhyaṃ tam ārādhya jagatpatim ।। ekam eva hi sāhāyyaṃ mātar me kartum arhasi ।। anujñāṃ dehi me viṣṇuṃ yathā cārādhayāmy aham ।। b anujñātuṃ na śaknomi tvām uttānaśayāṅgaja ।। d
tvadekatanayā tāta tvadādhāraikajīvitā ।। tadā tadā mama prāṇas tāta tvām upagacchati ।। adyaprabhṛti me mātā pitā viṣṇur na śaṃśayaḥ ।। jihvā me śatadhā yāti yadi tvāṃ vārayāmi bhoḥ ।।
parikramya praṇamyātha tapase sa dhruvo yayau ।। tatrendīvarajā mālā dhruvasyopāyanīkṛtā ।। parair avāryaprasarāḥ svāśīrvādāḥ paraḥśatāḥ ।। nārāyaṇo jagadvyāpī prabhuḥ kāruṇyavāridhiḥ ।।
anukūlena marutā darśitādhvāviśad vanam ।। na veda kānanādhvānaṃ kṣaṇaṃ dadhyau nṛpātmajaḥ ।। kiṃ karomi kva gacchāmi ko me sāhāyyado bhavet ।। tāvad dadarśa saptarṣīn atarkitagatīn vane ।।
bhāgyasūtrair ivākṛṣyo-panītān pramumoda ha ।। kṛṣṇājinopaviṣṭāṃś ca brahmasūtrair alaṃkṛtān ।। dhruvo vijñāpayaṃcakre praṇamya lalitaṃ vacaḥ ।। uttānapādatanayaṃ dhruvaṃ nirviṇṇamānasam ।।
anarghyanayane pathyaṃ mṛdugambhīrabhāṣiṇam ।। tavādyāpi na jānīmo vatsa nirvedakāraṇam ।। saptadvīpapate rājñaḥ kumāras tvaṃ tathā katham ।। kim asmābhir aho kāryaṃ kas tavāsti manorathaḥ ।। b
munayo mama yo bandhur uttamaś cottamottamaḥ ।। d bhavatkṛtaṃ hi sāhāyyaṃ etad icchāmi suvratāḥ ।। indrādiduravāpaṃ yat kathaṃ labhyeta tat padam ।। yathārtham eva pratyūcur marīcyādyās tadā dhruvam ।।
manorathapathātītaṃ sphītaṃ nākalayet phalam ।। indrādiduravāpaṃ yan mānavaiḥ sudurāsadam ।। kamalākāntakāntāṅghrikamalaṃ yaḥ suśīlayet ।। paramāntakam āpnoti sa viṣṇuḥ sarvado dhruva ।।
yanmāyayā kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ sa viṣṇu kīrtito arthadaḥ ।। antarātmāsya jagataḥ saṃtuṣṭaḥ kiṃ na yacchati ।। tam ārādhya hṛṣīkeśaṃ caturvargo na dūrataḥ ।। kathaṃ sa bhagavān ijyaḥ sa vidhiś copadiśyatām ।।
bālo ahaṃ rājaputro ahaṃ duḥkhaṃ naiva mayā kṣamam ।। śayānenopaviṣṭena vedyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā ।। vāsudevaṃ japan martyaḥ sarvaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam ।। dhyāyaṃś caturbhujaṃ viṣṇuṃ japtvā siddhiṃ na ko gataḥ ।।
manunā rājyakāmena vaiṣṇavena nṛpātmaja ।। yathābhilaṣitām ṛddhiṃ kṣipraṃ prāpsyasi sattama ।। vāsudevamanā bhūtvā dhruvo api tapase yayau ।। sa cakre yamunātīre munidiṣṭena vartmanā ।।
divyākṛtiṃ sapadi tena tataḥ sa eva harṣāt punaḥ sa prajajāpa nṛpātmabhūtaḥ ।। magne manasy anupameyasukhāmburāśau rājñaḥ śiśur na ca viveda śarīravārtām ।। śītātapādir iva viṣṇumayaṃ muniṃ hi prādeśikā na khalu dharṣayituṃ kṣamante ।। varadaḥ patagendravāhano harir āgāt svajanaṃ tam īkṣitum ।।
sa babhāv udayādrimatsarād dhṛtabālārka ivāsitācalaḥ ।। dantāṃśusaṃjñair amitapravāhaiḥ prakṣālayan reṇum ivāsya gātre ।। dhyānena te cendriyanigraheṇa manonirodhena ca duṣkareṇa ।। sve cintyamānaṃ tv idam eva mūrtaṃ puraḥsthitaṃ brahma caturbhujaṃ saḥ ।।
kiṃ vā karomīti sasaṃbhramaḥ sa tu na cābravīt kiṃcana no cakāra ।। daṇḍapraṇāmāya papāta bhūmau pravepamānabhru hareḥ puraḥ sa hi ।। roroda harṣeṇa ciraṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ jagato gurum ।। anyaiḥ sanatkumārādyair yogibhir yogināṃ varam ।।
dhruvam utthāpayāṃcakre cakrī dhṛtvā kareṇa tam ।। karābhyāṃ komalābhyāṃ sa pariṣvajyāha taṃ hariḥ ।। tad dadāmi na saṃdeho nādeyaṃ vidyate tava ।। taṃ mūrtivijñānanibhena devaḥ pasparśa śaṅkhena mukhe amalena ।।
tribhuvanaguruśaṅkhasparśajajñānabhānān udayati nitarāntaḥ sādhu tuṣṭāva hṛṣṭaḥ ।। akhilamunijananivahanamitacaraṇaḥ । kharakadanakaraḥ । capalacaritaḥ । devārādhitapādajalaḥ । sajalajaladharaśyāmaḥ । śamitasaubhapatiśālvādhāmā । abhirāmarāmātivinayakṛtanavarasarasāpahatendriyasuraramaṇīvihitāntaḥkaraṇānandaḥ । anādinidhanaḥ । adhananijadvijamitroddharaṇadhīraḥ । avadhīritasuranāthanāthitavipakṣapakṣaḥ । ṛkṣarājabilapraveśāpahatasyamantakāpamārjita nijāpavādadūritahṛtatrailokyabhāraḥ । dvārakāvāsanirataḥ । svaritamadhuraveṇuvādanaśravaṇāmṛtaprakaṭita atīndriyajñānaḥ । yamunātaṭacaraḥ । dvijadhenubhṛṅgagaṇais tyaktanijanijāhāraḥ । saṃsāradustarapārāvārasamuttāraṇāṅghripotaḥ । svapratāpānalahutakālayavanaḥ । vanamālādharavaramaṇikuṇḍalālaṃkṛtaśravaṇaḥ । nānāprasiddhābhidhānaḥ । nigamavibudhamunijanavacanamanogocaraḥ । kanakapiśaṅgakauśeyavāso bhagavān bhṛgupadakaustubhavibhūṣitoraḥsthalaḥ । svadayitākrūranijajananīgokulapālakacatur bhujaśaṅkhacakragadāpadmatulasīnavadala dāmahārakeyūrakaṭakamukuṭālaṃkṛtaḥ । sunandanādibhāgavatopāsitaviśvarūpaḥ । purāṇapuruṣottamaḥ । uttamaślokaḥ । lokāvāso vāsudevaḥ । śrīdevakījaṭharasaṃbhūtaḥ । bhūtapativirañcinatacaraṇāravindaḥ । vṛndāvanakṛtakeligopikājanaśramāpahaḥ । satataṃ saṃpāditasujanakāmaḥ । kundanibhaśaṅkhadharam indunibhavaktraṃ sundarasudarśanam udāratarahāsaṃ vidvajjanavanditam idaṃ ye rūpam atihṛdyam akhileśvaraṃ nato asmi । kācaṃ vicinvann iva divyaratnaṃ svāmin kṛtārtho asmi varān na yāci ।। kāmān na yāce sa hi ko api mūḍho yaḥ kalpavṛkṣāt tuṣamātram icchet ।।
ratnākare deva sati svanāthe vibhūṣaṇaṃ kācamayaṃ na yuktam ।। imaṃ varaṃ devavara prayaccha punaḥ punas tvām idam eva yāce ।। ity ātmasaṃdarśanalabdhadivyajñānaṃ gadantaṃ bhagavāñ jagāda ।। sthānaṃ paraṃ prāpnuhi yan mataṃ te kālena māṃ prāpsyasi śuddhabhāvaḥ ।।
mama prasādāt tava sā ca mātā mamāntike yā ca sunītir āryā ।। tyaktvā śanair divyavapuḥ svabhaktaṃ muhuḥ parāvṛttya samīkṣamāṇaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvātha varṣan surapuṣpavṛṣṭiṃ tuṣṭāva harṣād dhruvam avyayaṃ ca ।। yo ayaṃ nṛṇāṃ kīrtanadarśanābhyām āyur yaśo vardhayati śriyaṃ ca ।।
tasmin prasanne dvijarājapatre na durlabhaṃ bhaktajaneṣu kiṃcit ।। pūrṇe śatasahasre dve tasmān nakṣatramaṇḍalam ।। tāvatpramāṇabhāge tu budhasyāpy uśanā sthitaḥ ।। lakṣadvayaṃ tu bhaumasya sthito devapurohitaḥ ।।
tasmāc chanaiścarād ūrdhvaṃ lakṣe saptarṣimaṇḍalam ।। meḍhībhūtaḥ samastasya jyotiścakrasya sattama ।। kālasaṃkhyāṃ trilokasya sa karoti yuge yuge ।। brahmaṇā muniśārdūla viṣṇubhaktivivardhitaḥ ।।
adhogataiś ca bhūrlokaṃ dyotate dīrghadīdhitiḥ ।। chatravat pratipaśyeta maṇḍalān maṇḍalaṃ param ।। trailokyasyeśvaratvaṃ ca viṣṇudattaṃ śatakratoḥ ।। vaset svarge mahābhāga devendraḥ sa tu kīrtimān ।।
na tatra tapate sūryo na rātrir na niśākaraḥ ।। pātālasthā dvijaśreṣṭha dīpyamanāḥ svatejasā ।। tato yojanamātreṇa dviguṇo maṇḍalena tu ।। tatropari tapolokaś caturbhiḥ koṭibhiḥ sthitaḥ ।।
sarve chatrākṛtijñeyā bhuvanoparisaṃsthitāḥ ।। vārāhe tasya māhātmyaṃ kathitaṃ lokacintakaiḥ ।। brahmāṇḍāt paramaḥ sākṣān nirlepaḥ puruṣaḥ sthitaḥ ।। yas tu samyag imāṃ vetti sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।।
yuge yuge viṣṇur anādimūrtimān āsthāya viśvaṃ paripāti duṣṭahā ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe ekatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। sāṃprataṃ śrotum icchāmi tan me vada mahāmate ।। sahasrānīkasya harer avatārāṃś ca me śṛṇu ।।
pālayāmasa dharmeṇa rājyaṃ sa tu nṛpātmajaḥ ।। bhaktir babhūva deveśe narasiṃhe surottame ।। arghyapādyāsanai rājā tam abhyarcyābravīd idam ।। tvaddarśanam apuṇyānāṃ kalāv asmin sudurlabham ।।
ārādhayitum icchāmi vidhānaṃ tatra me vada ।। śrotum icchāmi sakalāṃs tān puṇyān api me vada ।। harau bhaktiṃ karoty atra nṛsiṃhe cātibhaktimān ।। tasyārayaḥ praṇaśyanti kāryasiddhiś ca jāyate ।।
tena te nikhilaṃ vakṣye śṛṇuṣvaikāgramānasaḥ ।। sa sarvapāpanirmukto viṣṇulokam avāpnuyāt ।। sa sarvapāpanirmukto viṣṇulokam avāpnuyāt ।। niṣkāmo naraśārdūla dehabādhāt pramucyate ।।
tasya kāmāḥ prasidhyanti paramaṃ padam āpnuyāt ।। svaṃ svaṃ padam anuprāptāḥ keśavasya prasādataḥ ।। te te viṣṇuṃ samārādhya svargalokam ito gatāḥ ।। sa svargamokṣabhāgī syān nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।।
arcanān narasiṃhasya prāpsyase svābhivāñchitam ।। na tu nirgamanaṃ tasya viṣṇulokād bhaven nṛpa ।। saṃsthāpya bhaktyā vidhivac ca pūjayet payāti sākṣāt parameśvaraṃ harim ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sahasrānīkacarite dvātriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
tvatprasādād viśeṣeṇa bhagavan prabravīhi me ।। yat puṇyaṃ labhate tadvad upalepanakṛṇ naraḥ ।। ghṛtasnānena yat puṇyaṃ pañcagavyena yad bhavet ।। karpūrāgurutoyena miśreṇa snāpitena ca ।।
mantreṇa snāpite yac ca vastradānena yad bhavet ।। puṣpair abhyarcite yac ca yat phalaṃ dhūpadīpayoḥ ।। namaskārakṛte yac ca phalaṃ yas stotragītayoḥ ।। dhvajapradāne yad viṣṇoḥ śaṅkhadānena yad bhavet ।।
tat sarvaṃ kathaya brahman bhaktasya mama keśave ।। mārkaṇḍeyaṃ niyujyātha kathane sa gato muniḥ ।। rājñe pravaktum ārebhe bhṛguṇā codito muniḥ ।। viṣṇubhaktasya vakṣyāmi tavāhaṃ pāṇḍuvaṃśaja ।।
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke sa modate ।। sa cākṣayaphalaṃ prāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। yac chrutvā sarvapāpebhyo muktir bhavati sattama ।। draupadyā saha rājendra kānanaṃ vicacāra ha ।।
nārado api gato nākaṃ juṣṭvedaṃ tīrtham uttamam ।। darśanaṃ munimukhyasya tīrthadharmopadeśinaḥ ।। dānavo bahuromā ca tathā sthūlaśirā nṛpa ।। kṛtvā bhūpa mune rupaṃ bahuromā gatas tadā ।।
bibhrat kamaṇḍaluṃ pārśve darbhasūcīṃ tathā kare ।। sa dṛṣṭaḥ pāṇḍavais tatra revāyāṃ vanacāribhiḥ ।। jagāda vacanaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāgyenāsi mahāmune ।। munīnāṃ darśanaṃ nātha śrutaṃ dharmopadeśakam ।।
tāvat sthūlaśirāḥ prāpto munirūpadharo aparaḥ ।। bhayāturaṃ naro jīvaṃ yo rakṣec charaṇāgatam ।। ekato medinīdānaṃ merubhūdharadakṣiṇam ।। dvijaṃ dhenuṃ striyaṃ bālaṃ piḍyamānaṃ ca durjanaiḥ ।।
atha māṃ hṛtasarvasvaṃ prāṇatyāgaparāyaṇam ।। gṛhītvā cākṣamālāṃ me tathā subhakamaṇḍalum ।। gṛhītaṃ mama sarvasvaṃ dānavena durātmanā ।। yānti romāñcitā bhūyo vidhāyāgniṃ ca taṃ munim ।।
tato dūrataraṃ prāptāḥ saṃrambhāt te ca pāṇḍavāḥ ।। kṛṣṇāsaṃrakṣaṇārthāya vraja vyāvartya cārjuna ।। tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā satyāṃ vācam akalpayat ।। mama satyāc ca sukṛtād dharmasaṃbhāṣaṇāt prabho ।।
tato ambare abhavad vāṇī tadā bhūpāśarīriṇī ।। nāsāv upadrutaḥ kena māyaiṣāsya durātmanaḥ ।। saṃrambhāt kupito atyarthaṃ maulideśe jaghāna tam ।। tatra yuddhaṃ pravavṛte dāruṇaṃ bhīmadaityayoḥ ।।
arjuno api samāyāto naiva paśyati taṃ munim ।। tato vṛkṣaṃ samāruhya yāvat paśyati cārjunaḥ ।। saṃhṛtā yāti duṣṭena rudatī kurarī yathā ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa yayau vīraḥ śabdair saṃnādayan diśaḥ ।।
tato daityo api tāṃ tanvīṃ vihāyāśu palāyitaḥ ।। patito medinīpṛṣṭhe tāvad eva caturbhujaḥ ।। tataḥ sa vismayākrānto natvā pārtho vaco avadat ।। mayāpy apakṛtaṃ nātha tat kṣamasva namo astu te ।।
tat kṣantavyaṃ jagannātha caitanyaṃ mānave kutaḥ ।। upayāto harer dehaṃ pūrvakarmaprabhāvataḥ ।। kena karmavipākena viṣṇoḥ sārūpyam āptavān ।। caritaṃ citram atyarthaṃ śṛṇvatāṃ mudavardhanam ।।
jayadhvaja iti khyāto nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ ।। upaleparataś caiva dīpadāne samudyataḥ ।। mama taccaritaṃ dṛṣṭvā vipro vismayam āgataḥ ।। apṛcchad vītihotras taṃ vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।।
viṣṇubhaktimatāṃ puṃsāṃ śreṣṭho asi puruṣarṣabha ।। tan me vada mahābhāga tvayā kiṃ viditaṃ phalam ।। tathāpi tvaṃ mahābhāga etayoḥ satatodyataḥ ।। tad brūhi yady aguhyaṃ ca prītir mayi tavāsti cet ।।
śṛṇuṣva vipraśārdūla mamaiva caritaṃ purā ।। pūrvajanmani viprendra raivato nāma vāḍavaḥ ।। piśuno niṣṭhuraś caiva apaṇyanāṃ ca vikrayī ।। mahāpāparato nityaṃ brahmadveṣaratas tathā ।।
madyapānarato nityaṃ brahmadveṣaratas tathā ।। kadācit kāmacāro ahaṃ gṛhītvā brāhmaṇastriyaḥ ।। svavastraprāntato brahman kiyadaṃśaḥ sa mārjitaḥ ।। tenāpi mama duṣkarma niḥśeṣaṃ kṣayam āgatam ।।
tadaiva dīpakaṃ dṛṣṭvā āgatāḥ purapālakāḥ ।। khaḍgena tīkṣṇadhāreṇa śiraś chittvā ca te gatāḥ ।। gandharvair gīyamāno ahaṃ svargalokaṃ tadā gataḥ ।। divyabhogasamāyukto divyarūpasamanvitaḥ ।।
jayadhvaja iti khyāto rājā rājīvalocanaḥ ।। indralokam anuprāpya rudralokaṃ tato gataḥ ।। dṛṣṭaś ca namito naiva garvān me hasitaś ca saḥ ।। iti śāpaṃ samākarṇya dattaṃ tena dvijanmanā ।।
yadā revāmaṭhe rājan dharmaputrasya dhīmataḥ ।। so aham arjuna bhūpāla dharmaputra yudhiṣṭhira ।। viṣṇoḥ sārūpyam agamaṃ yāmi vaikuṇṭham adya vai ।। b ity uktvā garuḍārūḍho dharmaputrasya paśyataḥ ।। d
