saṃmārjanopalepābhyāṃ mahimā tena varṇitaḥ ।। bhaktimadbhiḥ praśāntaiś ca kiṃ punaḥ samyagarcanāt ।। sahasrānīkabhūpālo haripūjārato abhavat ।। jñānato ajñānato vāpi pūjakānāṃ vimuktidaḥ ।।
tartuṃ yadīcchatha dvijā dustaraṃ bhavasāgaram ।। te vandyās te prapūjyāś ca namasyāś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasimhapurāṇe sahasrānīkacarite mārkaṇḍeyenopadiṣṭasaṃmārjanopalepaphalaṃ nāma trayastriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। nirmālyāpanayād viṣṇor yat puṇyaṃ tad vadasva me ।।
narasiṃhākṛtiṃ rājan sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। śrīviṣṇoḥ sadanaṃ prāpya modate kālam akṣayam ।। etāvatāpi rājendra sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। devadevasya vidhinā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। viṣṇulokam avāpnoti pūjyamānaḥ surottamaiḥ ।। agniloke sa moditvā punar viṣṇupure vaset ।। narasiṃhākṛteḥ kuryāc chaṅkhabherīnināditam ।।
divyaṃ vimānam āsthāya viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। mantrapūrvaṃ mahārāja tasya puṇyam anantakam ।। prakṣālya devadeveśaṃ vāruṇaṃ lokam āpnuyāt ।। uṣṇāmbunā ca prakṣālya sarvapāpair pramucyate ।।
narasiṃhaṃ tu saṃsnāpya karpūrāguruvāriṇā ।। puṇyodakena govindaṃ snāpya bhaktyā narottama ।। vastrābhyām arcanaṃ bhaktyā paridhāpya hariṃ hareḥ ।। kuṅkumāguruśrīkhaṇḍakardamair acyutākṛtim ।।
mallikāmālatījātiketakyaśokacampakaiḥ ।। tulasīkaravīraiś ca pālāśaiḥ sānukumbakaiḥ ।। arcayed daśasuvarṇasya pratyekaṃ phalam āpnuyāt ।। kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi kalpakoṭiśatāni ca ।।
narasiṃhaṃ tu yo bhaktyā bilvapatrair akhaṇḍitaiḥ ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। māhiṣākhyaṃ guggulaṃ ca ājyayuktaṃ saśarkaram ।। dhūpitaiḥ sarvadigbhyas tu sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ ।।
vāyuloke sa moditvā paścād viṣṇupuraṃ vrajet ।। viṣṇave vidhivad bhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ।। jyotiṣmatā vimānena viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। nivedya narasiṃhāya yāvakaṃ pāyasaṃ tathā ।।
viṣṇuloke mahābhogān bhuñjann āste sa vaiṣṇavaḥ ।। śāntiṃ tasya prayacchanti śriyam ārogyam eva ca ।। kṛtena yat phalaṃ nṝṇāṃ tac chṛṇuṣva nṛpātmaja ।। namaskāraḥ kṛto yena bhaktyā vai mādhavasya ca ।।
stotrair japaiś ca devāgre yaḥ stauti madhusūdanam ।। gītavādyādikaṃ nāṭyaṃ śaṅkhatūryādiniḥsvanaiḥ ।। parvakāle viśeṣeṇa kāmagaḥ kāmarūpavān ।। mahārhamaṇicitreṇa vimānena virājatā ।।
dhvajaṃ tu viṣṇave yas tu garuḍena samanvitam ।। viṣṇulokam avāpnoti sevyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ ।। mukuṭābharaṇādyaiś ca yo viṣṇuṃ pūjayen nṛpa ।। indraloke vased dhīmān yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ।।
ārādhya tam athāgre tu yat kiṃcid dagdham uttamam ।। pitaras tasya modante śvetadvīpe ciraṃ nṛpa ।। tasya svargāpavargau tu bhavato nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। na tatra vyādhidurbhikṣarājacaurādikaṃ bhayam ।।
nānāsvargasukhaṃ bhuktvā na bhūyaḥ stanapo bhavet ।। na bhavet tasya grāmasya bhayaṃ vā tatra kutracit ।। narasiṃhaṃ samārādhya brāhmaṇair vedapāragaiḥ ।। kṛte tasmin mayokte tu āgacchati na tadbhayam ।।
samyagārādhanīyaṃ tu narasiṃhasya mandire ।। kārayet saṃyatair vipraiḥ sabhojanasadakṣiṇaiḥ ।। upasargādimaraṇaṃ prajānām upaśāmyati ।। homaṃ ca bhojanaṃ caiva tasya doṣaḥ praṇaśyati ।।
narasiṃhaṃ samārādhya lakṣahomaṃ tu kārayet ।। evamādiphalopetaṃ narasiṃhārcanaṃ nṛpa ।। ataḥ parataraṃ nāsti svargamokṣaphalapradam ।। santy araṇye hy amūlyāni patrapuṣpāṇi śākhinām ।।
mano niyamayed ekaṃ vidyāsādhanakarmaṇi ।। mano niyamitaṃ yena muktis tasya kare sthitā ।। dine dine tvaṃ kuru viṣṇupūjāṃ vadasva cānyat kathayāmi kiṃ te ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sahasrānīkacarite śrīviṣṇoḥ pūjāvidhir nāma catustriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
suptās te muniśārdūla ye viṣṇuṃ nārcayanti vai ।। bhaktyā taṃ pūjayiṣyāmi koṭihomaphalaṃ vada ।। yat tasmai kathayāmasa śaunakas tad vādami te ।। śaunakaṃ tu sukhāsīnaṃ paryapṛcchad bṛhaspatiḥ ।। b
lakṣahomasya yā bhūmiḥ koṭihomasya yā śubhā ।। d tāṃ me kathaya viprendra homasya carite vidhim ।। b ityukto guruṇā so atha lakṣahomādikaṃ vidhim ।। d śaunako vaktum ārebhe yathāvan nṛpasattama ।। b
pravakṣyāmi yathāvat te śṛṇu devapurohita ।। d yajñakarmaṇi śastāyā bhūmer lakṣaṇam uttamam ।। ūrumātraṃ khanitvā ca śodhayet tāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। pramāṇaṃ bāhumātraṃ tu sarvataḥ kuṇḍalakṣaṇam ।।
upari mekhalāṃ kuryāc caturasrāṃ suvistarām ।। brāhmaṇān vedasaṃpannān brahmakarmasamanvitān ।। brahmacaryavrataṃ kuryus trirātraṃ te dvijātayaḥ ।। te śuklavāsasaḥ snātā gandhasrakpuṣpadhāriṇaḥ ।।
kauśam āsanam āsīnā ekāgramanasaḥ punaḥ ।। bhūmim ālikhya cābhyukṣya yatnād agniṃ nidhāpayet ।। āghārāv ājyabhāgau ca juhuyāt pūrvam eva tu ।। juhuyād ekacittena svāhākārānvitāṃ budhaḥ ।।
savitā devatā tasya viśvāmitras tathā ṛṣiḥ ।। yāvat prapūryate saṃkhyā lakṣaṃ vā koṭir eva vā ।। dīnānāthajanebhyas tu yajamānaḥ prayatnataḥ ।। samāpte dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād ṛtvigbhyaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ ।।
prokṣayed grāmamadhye tu vyādhitāṃs tu viśeṣataḥ ।। sarvabādhāpraśamanī śāntir bhavati sarvadā ।। lakṣahomādikavidhiṃ kāryaṃ rāṣṭre suśāntidam ।। tatrāpi śāntir bhavitā narāṇāṃ gavāṃ ca bhṛtyaiḥ saha bhūpateś ca ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe lakṣahomavidhir nāma pañcatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। tān śṛṇuṣva mahīpāla pavitrān pāpanāśanān ।। madhukaiṭabhau ca nidhanaṃ prāpitau ca mahātmanā ।। yathā pṛthvī dhṛtā rājan vārāheṇa mahātmanā ।।
hiraṇyākṣo mahāvīryo ditiputro mahātanuḥ ।। narasiṃhena devena prāpito nidhanaṃ nṛpa ।। indras tribhuvanādhyakṣaḥ kṛtas tena nṛpātmaja ।। sagaṇāś cādbhutā rājan rākṣasā devakaṇṭakāḥ ।।
balabhadreṇa rāmeṇa yathā daityaḥ purā hataḥ ।। kalau prāpte yathā buddho bhaven nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। samāpte tu kalau bhūyas tathā te kathayāmy aham ।। mayocyamānaṃ ca vimucya pāpaṃ prayāti viṣṇoḥ padam atyudāram ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe hareḥ prādurbhāvānukramaṇe ṣaṭtriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। na śakyaṃ vistarād vaktuṃ tān bravīmi samāsataḥ ।। anantabhogaśayane yoganidrāṃ samāgataḥ ।। śrotrābhyām apatat toye svedabindudvayaṃ nṛpa ।।
mahākāyau mahāvīryau mahābalaparākramau ।। nābhimadhye nṛpaśreṣṭha tasmin brahmābhyajāyata ।। tathety uktvā jagannāthaṃ brahmāpi kamalodbhavaḥ ।। tāvat tatra samāyātau tāv ubhau madhukaiṭabhau ।।
apakṛtya gatau ghorau dānavau baladarpitau ।। duḥkhitaś cintayāmasa kathaṃ srakṣyāmi vai prajāḥ ।। srakṣye ahaṃ jñānahīnas tu aho kaṣṭam upasthitam ।। yatnato vedaśāstrāṇi smarann api na dṛṣṭavān ।।
ekāgramanasā samyak śāstreṇa stotum ārabhat ।। vijñānanidhaye nityaṃ karmaṇāṃ nidhaye namaḥ ।। acintyāya namo nityaṃ sarvajñāya namo namaḥ ।। sāmnāṃ mūrtis tvam evādya sarvadā sarvarūpavān ।।
dehi me tvaṃ sarvajñānaṃ devadeva namo namaḥ ।। brahmāṇam āha deveśo dāsye te jñānam uttamam ।। kenāsya nītaṃ vijñānaṃ kena rūpeṇa cādadhe ।। bahuyojanavistīrṇaṃ sarvajñānamayaṃ nṛpa ।।
praviśya ca sa pātālaṃ dṛṣṭavān madhukaiṭabhau ।। vedaśāstrāṇi munibhiḥ saṃstuto madhusūdanaḥ ।। jagaddhitāya sa punar yoganidrāvaśaṃ gataḥ ।। āgatya dadṛśāte tu śayānaṃ devam avyayam ।।
ānīya vedaśāstrāṇi dattvā śete atra sādhuvat ।। bodhayāmasatus tūrṇaṃ śayānaṃ keśavaṃ nṛpa ।। āvayor dehi saṃgrāmaṃ yudhyasvotthāya sāṃpratam ।। tatheti coktvā tau devaḥ śārṅgaṃ sajjam athākarot ।।
khaṃ diśaḥ pradiśaś caiva pūrayāmasa līlayā ।। yuyudhāte mahāghorau hariṇā madhukaiṭabhau ।। samaṃ yuddhaṃ abhūd evaṃ teṣām astrāṇi muñcatām ।। tāni śastrāṇi sarvāṇi ciccheda tilaśas tadā ।।
hatau śārṅgavinirmuktaiḥ śaraiḥ kṛṣṇena durmadau ।। medinīti tataḥ saṃjñām avāpeyaṃ vasuṃdharā ।। prajāḥ sasarja bhūpāla vedadṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। vasitvā candrasadane vedavid brāhmaṇo bhavet ।।
āsthāya bhīmaṃ janalokasaṃsthaiḥ stuto atha yas taṃ smara bhūmipāla ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapūrāṇe matsyaprādurbhāvo nāma saptatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। sarve te śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ kṣīrābdhitanayāpatim ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭā rājan brahmādyā devatāgaṇāḥ ।।
namas te padmanābhāya lokanāthāya śārṅgiṇe ।। namas te viśvarūpāya sarvadevamayāya ca ।। madhukaiṭabhanāśāya keśavāya namo namaḥ ।। jayopāyaṃ hi no brūhi karuṇākara te namaḥ ।।
tān abravīd dharir devān teṣām evāgrataḥ sthitaḥ ।। manthānaṃ mandaraṃ kṛtvā netraṃ kṛtvā ca vāsukim ।। dānavaiḥ sahitā bhūtvā manthadhvaṃ kṣīrasāgaram ।। bhaviṣyaty amṛtaṃ tatra tatpānād balavattarāḥ ।।
yūyaṃ sarve mahābhāgās tejiṣṭhā raṇavikramāḥ ।। tato hi dānavāñ jetuṃ samarthā nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। praṇamyāgatya nilayaṃ saṃdhiṃ kṛtvātha dānavaiḥ ।। balinā coddhṛto rājan mandarākhyo mahāgiriḥ ।।
sarvauṣadhīṃś ca prakṣipya devadaityaiḥ payonidhau ।। sarve devahitārthāya viṣṇuś ca svayam āgataḥ ।। sarve te maitrabhāvena kṣīrābdhes taṭam āśritāḥ ।। tato mathitum ārabdhaṃ nṛpate tarasāmṛtam ।।
devatāḥ pucchabhāge tu mathanāya niyojitāḥ ।। ādhāreṇa vinā rājan taṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasā hariḥ ।। ātmānaṃ saṃpraviśyātha mandarasya girer adhaḥ ।। upary ākrāntavān śailaṃ pṛthagrūpeṇa keśavaḥ ।।
tatas te tvarayā yuktā mamanthuḥ kṣīrasāgaram ।। mathyamānāt tatas tasmāt kṣīrābdher abhavan nṛpa ।। taṃ nāgā jagṛhuḥ sarve taccheṣaṃ śaṃkaro agrahīt ।। airāvataś ca nāgendro hariś coccaiḥśravāḥ punaḥ ।।
caturthāt parijātaś ca utpannaḥ sa mahādrumaḥ ।। taṃ bhavaḥ śirasā dhatte nārīvat svastikaṃ nṛpa ।। kṣīrodadher utthitāś ca gandharvāś ca sahasraśaḥ ।। abhavan jātaharṣās te tatra sarve surāsurāḥ ।।
kṛṣṇājñayā ca vāyuś ca sukhaṃ vāti surān prati ।। nistejaso abhavan daityā nirvīryāś ca mahāmate ।। vibhrājamānā rājendra diśaḥ sarvāḥ svatejasā ।। divyagandhānuliptāṅgī sumanobhiḥ subhūṣaṇaih ।।
harivakṣaḥsthalaṃ prāptā tataḥ sā kamalālayā ।। dhanvantariḥ samuttasthau tataḥ prītāḥ surā nṛpa ।। nītvāmṛtaghaṭaṃ pūrṇaṃ te ca jagmur yathāsukham ।। ātmānaṃ nṛpaśārdūla sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam ।।
divyarūpāṃ tu tāṃ dṛṣṭvā mohitās te suradviṣaḥ ।। kāmena pīḍitā hy āsann asurās tatra tatkṣaṇāt ।। amṛtaṃ tu samādāya devebhyaḥ pradadau hariḥ ।। balavanto mahāvīryā raṇe jagmus tato asurān ।।
etat te kathitaṃ rājan prādurbhāvo harer ayam ।। divaukasānāṃ tu hitāya kevalaṃ rūpaṃ paraṃ pāvanam eva kīrtitam ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe kūrmaprādurbhāvo nāmāṣṭatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। vārāhaṃ te pravakṣyāmi samāhitamanāḥ śṛṇu ।।
trailokyam akhilaṃ vyāpya tiṣṭhanty ambhāṃsi sattama ।। grastvā viṣṇus tataḥ śete tasminn ekārṇave jale ।। rātriṃ yugasahasrāntāṃ brahmarūpī jagatpatiḥ ।। hiraṇyākṣa iti khyāto mahābalaparākramaḥ ।।
yajvinām apākārāya yatate sa tu bhūtale ।। tena teṣāṃ balaṃ vīryaṃ tejaś cāpi bhaviṣyati ।। bhūmer yā dhāraṇāśaktis tāṃ nītvā sa mahāsuraḥ ।। vinā śaktyā ca jagatī praviveśa rasātalam ।।
saṃcintya jñātvā yogena rasātalatalaṃ gatām ।। vedapādaṃ yūpadaṃṣṭraṃ ketuvaktraṃ narādhipa ।। agnijihvaṃ srucaṃ tuṇḍaṃ candrārkanayanaṃ mahat ।। prāgvaṃśakāyaṃ havirnāsaṃ kuśadarbhatanūruham ।।
nakṣatratārāhāraṃ ca pralayāvartabhūṣaṇam ।। rasātalaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha sanakādyair abhiṣṭutaḥ ।। daṃṣṭrāgreṇa tataḥ pṛthvīm samuddhṛtya rasātalāt ।। saṃsthāpya parvatān sarvān yathāsthānam akalpayat ।।
vaiṣṇavānāṃ hitārthāya kṣetraṃ tad guptam uttamam ।। hanti cānte jagat sarvaṃ rudrarūpī janārdanaḥ ।। dṛḍhāṃ matiṃ yajñatanau viveśya vai vihāya pāpaṃ ca naro hariṃ vrajet ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe vārāhaprādurbhāvo nāma ekonacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
sāṃprataṃ nārasiṃhaṃ tu pravakṣyāmi nibodha me ।। tapas tepe nirāhāro bahuvarṣasahasrakam ।। varaṃ varaya daityendra yas te manasi vartate ।। uvāca natvā deveśaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vinayānvitaḥ ।।
yad yad vṛṇomy ahaṃ brahmaṃs tat tan me dātum arhasi ।। na kāṣṭhena na kīṭena pāṣāṇena na vāyunā ।। na surair asurair vāpi na gandharvair na rākṣasaiḥ ।। na vānarair mṛgair vāpi naiva mātṛgaṇair api ।।
na dine na ca naktaṃ me tvatprasādād bhaven mṛtiḥ ।। iti vai devadeveśa varaṃ tvatto vṛṇomy aham ।। b ityukto daityarājena brahmā taṃ prāha pārthiva ।। d durlabhān api daityendra dadāmi paramādbhutān ।।
tvatprārthitaṃ mayā dattaṃ sarvaṃ te cāstu daityapa ।। ity evaṃ daityarājasya hiraṇyakaśipoḥ purā ।। so api labdhavaro daityo balavān baladarpitaḥ ।। divi rājyaṃ svayaṃ cakre sarvaśaktisamanvitam ।।
vicerur avanau sarve bibhrāṇā mānuṣīṃ tanum ।। āhūya sarvā rājendra vākyaṃ cedam abhāṣata ।। yuṣmābhir aham evādya trailokyādhipatiḥ prajāḥ ।। tāś ca sarvās tathā cakrur daityendrasya bhayān nṛpa ।।
adharmayuktaṃ sakalaṃ babhūva nṛpasattama ।। gate kāle tu mahati devāḥ sendrā bṛhaspatim ।। hiraṇyakaśipor asya vināśaṃ munisattama ।। trailokyahāriṇaḥ śīghraṃ vadhopāyaṃ vadasva naḥ ।। b
śṛṇudhvaṃ mama vākyāni svapadaprāptaye surāḥ ।। d śoko nāśayati prajñāṃ śoko nāśayati śrutam ।। soḍhuṃ śakyo agnisaṃbandhaḥ śastrasparśaś ca dāruṇaḥ ।। kālān nimittāc ca vayaṃ lakṣyāmas tatkṣayaṃ surāḥ ।।
acirād eva duṣṭo asau naśyaty eva parasparam ।। hiraṇyakaśipor nāśaṃ śakunāni vadanti me ।। kṣīrodasyottaraṃ tīraṃ prasupto yatra keśavaḥ ।। sa hi prasanno daityasya vadhopāyaṃ vadiṣyati ।।
prītyā ca parayā yuktā gantuṃ cakrur athodyamam ।। kārayitvā munivaraiḥ prasthitās te divaukasaḥ ।। te śarvam agrataḥ kṛtvā kṣīrābdher uttaraṃ taṭam ।। astuvan vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ pūjayantaḥ pratasthire ।।
astuvan nāmabhiḥ puṇyair ekāgramanasā harim ।। prabhaviṣṇur grasiṣṇuś ca lokātmā lokapālakaḥ ।। karmakṛd vāmanādhīśo vāsudevaḥ puruṣṭutaḥ ।। nārāyaṇo naro haṃso viṣṇuseno hutāśanaḥ ।।
vaikuṇṭhaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sūryaḥ surārcitaḥ ।। ādidevo jagatkartā yogeśo garuḍadhvajaḥ ।। padmanābho hṛṣīkeśo vibhur dāmodaro hariḥ ।। vāmano duṣṭadamano govindo gopavallabhaḥ ।।
kāruṇyaḥ karuṇo vyāsaḥ pāpahā śāntivardhanaḥ ।। badarīnilayaḥ śāntas tapasvī vaidyutaprabhaḥ ।। tapovāso damo vāsaḥ satyavāsaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। pūrṇaḥ pūrtiḥ purāṇajñaḥ puṇyajñaḥ puṇyavardhanaḥ ।।
kirīṭī kuṇḍalī hārī mekhalī kavacī dhvajī ।। śāntaḥ śāntikaraḥ śāstā śaṃkaraḥ śaṃtanustutaḥ ।। sāvanaḥ sāhasī sattvaḥ saṃpūrṇāṃśaḥ samṛddhimān ।। mokṣadaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ kṣīrābdhikṛtaketanaḥ ।।
tvaṃ yajñas tvaṃ vaṣaṭkāras tvam oṃkāras tvam agnayaḥ ।। namo devādidevāya viṣṇave śāśvatāya ca ।। anantāyāprameyāya namas te garuḍadhvaja ।। b ity etair nāmabhir divyaiḥ saṃstuto madhusūdanaḥ ।। d
uvāca prakaṭībhūtvā devān sarvān idaṃ vacaḥ ।। b yuṣmābhiḥ saṃstuto devā nāmabhiḥ kevalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। d ata eva prasanno asmi kim arthaṃ karavāṇi vaḥ ।। b devadeva hṛṣīkeśa puṇḍarīkākṣa mādhava ।। d
tvam eva jānāsi hare kiṃ tasmāt paripṛcchasi ।। b yuṣmadāgamanaṃ sarvaṃ jānāmy asurasūdanāḥ ।। d puṇyanāmaśatenaiva saṃstuto ahaṃ bhavena ca ।। tenāhaṃ pūjito nityaṃ bhavāmīha tvayā yathā ।।
tvayā stuto haniṣyāmi hiraṇyakaśipuṃ bhava ।। yadāsya tanayo dhīmān prahlādo nāma vaiṣṇavaḥ ।। ity uktvā viṣṇunā devā natvā viṣṇuṃ yayur nṛpa ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe viṣṇor nāmastotraṃ nāma catvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
prādurbhāvaṃ nṛsiṃhasya yathāvad vaktum arhasi ।। dhanyā vayaṃ mahāyogiṃs tvatprasādān mahāmune ।। sudhāṃ pibāmo durlabhyāṃ dhanyāḥ śrīśakathābhidhām ।। b purā hiraṇyakaśipos taporthaṃ gacchato vanam ।। d
vārito bandhubhir bhṛtyair mitraiś ca hitakāribhiḥ ।। trailokyādhipatis tvaṃ hi sarve devāḥ parājitāḥ ।। prayojanaṃ na paśyāmo vayaṃ buddhyā samanvitāḥ ।। evaṃ tair vāryamāṇo api durmado madamohitaḥ ।।
tasya saṃtapyamānasya tapaḥ paramaduṣkaram ।। kiṃ karomi kathaṃ daityas tapaso vinivartate ।। praṇamya prāha bhūpāla nārado munisattamaḥ ।। yeṣām manasi govindas te vai nārhanti śocitum ।।
nārāyaṇo jagatsvāmī matiṃ me saṃpradāsyati ।। prayātaḥ parvatenaiva sārdhaṃ sa munipuṃgavaḥ ।। yatrāste ditijaśreṣṭho dvitrair mitraiḥ parīvṛtaḥ ।। śṛṇvatas tasya daityasya prāha gambhīrayā girā ।।
trivāraṃ prajapitvā vai nārado maunam āśritaḥ ।। hiraṇyakaśipur daityaḥ kruddhaś cāpaṃ samādade ।। tāvad uḍḍīya tau bhūpa gatau nāradaparvatau ।। tyaktvā tam āśramaṃ bhūyo nagaraṃ svaṃ mahīpate ।।
tadā rajasvalā bhūtvā snātābhūd daivayogataḥ ।। svāmin yadā tapaścaryāṃ kartuṃ gehād vanaṃ gataḥ ।। tat kimarthaṃ mahārāja sāṃprataṃ tyaktavān vratam ।। tathyaṃ kathaya me nātha snehāt pṛcchāmi daityapa ।। b
śṛṇu cārvaṅgi me tathyāṃ vācaṃ vratavināśinīm ।। d kailāsaśikhare devi mahadānandakānane ।। vāradvayaṃ trayaṃ ceti vyāhṛtaṃ vacanaṃ śubhe ।। kodaṇḍe śaram ādhāya yāvan muñcāmi bhāmini ।।
tyaktvā vrataṃ samāyāto bhāvikāryabalena vai ।। ṛtukāle tu saṃprāpte jāto garbhas tadaiva hi ।। nāradasyopadeśena vaiṣṇavaḥ samajāyata ।। tasya sūnur abhud bhaktaḥ prahlādo janmavaiṣṇavaḥ ।।
yathā kalau harer bhaktiḥ pāśasaṃsāramocanī ।। bālo alpadeho mahatīṃ mahātmā vistārayan bhāti sa viṣṇubhaktim ।। sa bālalīlāsu sahānyaḍimbhaiḥ prahelikākrīḍanakeṣu nityam ।। itthaṃ śiśutve api vicitrakārī vyavardhateśasmaraṇāmṛtāśaḥ ।।
bālaṃ gurugṛhāyātaṃ dadarśa svāyatekṣaṇam ।। mūrdhni cakrāṅkitā paṭṭī kṛṣṇanāmāṅkitādarāt ।। putra te jananī nityaṃ sudhīr me tvā praśaṃsati ।। vicāryānandajananaṃ samyag āyāti tad vada ।।
govindaṃ trijagadvandyaṃ prabhuṃ natvā bravīmi te ।। kruddho api taṃ vañcayituṃ jahāsoccaiḥ prahṛṣṭavat ।। rāma govinda kṛṣṇeti viṣṇo mādhava śrīpate ।। śāsitās tu mayedānīṃ tvayedaṃ kva śrutaṃ vacaḥ ।।
prahlādaḥ prāha he ārya maivaṃ brūyāḥ kadācana ।। kṛṣṇeti yo naro brūyāt so abhayaṃ vindate padam ।। rāma mādhava kṛṣṇeti smara bhaktyātmaśuddhaye ।। śaraṇaṃ vraja sarveśaṃ sarvapāpakṣayaṃkaram ।।
kenāyaṃ bālako nīto daśām etāṃ sumadhyamām ।। uktveti parito vīkṣya punar āha śiśor gurum ।। dhīmān ūce khalaṃ bhūpaṃ devāntaka parīkṣatām ।। asakṛn na hi roṣeṇa kiṃ kruddhasyālpake mayi ।।
viṣṇustavaṃ mama sutaṃ pāpa bālam apīpaṭhaḥ ।। mamātmajasya kiṃ jāḍyāṃ tava caitad dvijaiḥ kṛtam ।। tyaja dvijaprasaṅgaṃ hi dvijasaṅgo hy aśobhanaḥ ।। yasya yat saṃgatiḥ puṃso maṇivat syāt sa tadguṇaḥ ।।
matsutasyocitaṃ tyaktvā viṣṇupakṣīyanāśanam ।। viśvanāthasya me sūnur bhūtvānyaṃ nātham icchasi ।। yaḥ śūraḥ sa śriyaṃ bhuṅkte sa prabhuḥ sa maheśvaraḥ ।। tyaja jāḍyam ataḥ śauryaṃ bhajasva svakulocitam ।।
asuro ayaṃ surān stauti mārjāra iva mūṣakān ।। labdhvāpi mahad aiśvaryaṃ lāghavaṃ yānty abuddhayaḥ ।। re mūḍha dṛṣṭvāpy aiśvasryaṃ mama brūṣe puro harim ।। ity uktvā tanayaṃ bhūpa jātakrodho bhayānakaḥ ।।
yāhi yāhi dvijapaśo sādhu śādhi sutaṃ mama ।। viṣṇuṃ visṛjyānvasarac ca daityaṃ kiṃ vā na kuryur bharaṇāya lubdhāḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe nṛsiṃhaprādurbhāve ekacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। aśeṣavidyānivahena sākaṃ kālena kaumāram avāpa yogī ।।
tasmin vayaḥsthasya bahirviraktir bhavaty abhūc citram aje ca bhaktiḥ ।। ānāyya praṇataṃ prāha prahlādaṃ viditeśvaram ।। idānīṃ bhrājase bhāsvān nīhārād iva nirgataḥ ।। vayasā vardhamānena putrakaivaṃ suśikṣitāḥ ।।
vinyasya svāṃ ciradhṛtāṃ sukhī paśyan śriyaṃ tava ।। tadā tadādhiṃ tyaktvā nu mahat saukhyam avāpnuyāt ।। na citraṃ putra tac chrotuṃ kiṃ nu me vāñchataḥ śrutī ।। yuddhavraṇaṃ ca gātreṣu māyināṃ ca mahotsavaḥ ।।
jagāda yogī niśśaṅkaṃ prahlādaḥ praṇato gurum ।। kiṃtu tā vaiṣṇavīr vāco muktvā nānyā vicārayet ।। yatra saṃsṛtiduḥkhaughakakṣāgnir gīyate hariḥ ।। arthaśātreṇa kiṃ tāta yatra saṃsṛtisaṃtatiḥ ।।
vaiṣṇavaṃ vāṅmayaṃ tasmāc chrāvyaṃ sevyaṃ ca sarvadā ।। iti tasya vacaḥ śṛṇvan hiraṇyakaśipus tadā ।। prahlādasya giraṃ puṇyāṃ janasaṃsṛtināśinīm ।। parito vīkṣya saṃprāha kruddho daityabhaṭān idam ।।
utkṛttyotkṛttya marmāṇi rakṣitāstu hariḥ svayam ।। kākolakaṅkagṛdhrebhyo hy asyāṅgaṃ saṃvibhajyatām ।। acyutasya priyaṃ bhaktaṃ taṃ jagnuḥ patinoditāḥ ।। akṛtrimarasam bhaktaṃ tam itthaṃ dhyānaniścalam ।।
athālabdhapadāny asya gātre śastrāṇi rakṣasām ।। kiṃ prākṛtāni śastrāṇi kariṣyanti haripriye ।। pīḍayanti janāṃs tāvad vyādhayo rākṣasā grahāḥ ।। te tu bhagnāstraśakalaiḥ pratīpotthair itas tataḥ ।।
na citraṃ vibudhānāṃ tad ajñānāṃ vismayāvaham ।। punas tasya vadhopāyaṃ cintayan sa sudurmatiḥ ।। aśastravadhayogyo ayam asmayo haritoṣakṛt ।। tasyājñāṃ jagṛhur mūrdhnā praharṣād deśavartinaḥ ।।
akarṣakā harimahisvakarṣakā haripriyaṃ drutataram āpatan ruṣā ।। alaṃ na te harivapuṣaṃ tu kevalaṃ vidaśya taṃ nijadaśanair vinā kṛtāḥ ।। sametya te ditijapatiṃ vyajijñapan viniḥśvasatpracalaphaṇā bhujaṃgamāḥ ।। mahānubhāvasya tavātmajasya vadhe niyuktvā daśanair vinā kṛtāḥ ।।
vicintayantaḥ pṛthuvismayena prahlādasāmarthyanidānam eva ।। prahlāda duṣṭo api nijāṅgajāto na vadhya ity adya kṛpā mamābhūt ।। mūḍhāḥ prāñjalayaḥ prāhur dvijāḥ śāstraviśāradāḥ ।। prahlādas tvāṃ na jānāti kruddhaṃ svalpo mahābalam ।।
putraḥ kuputratām eti na mātāpitarau kadā ।। ādāya tadanujñātaṃ prahlādaṃ dhīdhanaṃ yayuḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe narasiṃhaprādurbhāve dvicatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। jaḍa iva vicacāra bāhyakṛtye satatam anantamayam jagat prapaśyan ।।
hṛdi kim api vicintya hṛṣṭaromā bhavasi sadā ca vadāṅga yady aguhyam ।। śṛṇuta sumanasaḥ surāriputrā yad aham ananyaratir vadāmi pṛṣṭaḥ ।। vimṛśata subudhair utaiṣa sevyo drutam atha vā parivarjya eva dūrāt ।। sukuṭilatanubhis tadagnitaptair vividhapurājananāni saṃsmaradbhiḥ ।।
paśyāmi garbhe api sakṛn mukundapādābjayor asmaraṇena kaṣṭam ।। evaṃ bhave asmin parimṛgyamāṇā vīkṣāmahe naiva sukhāṃśaleśam ।। tasmād bhave asmin kila cārurūpe duḥkhākare naiva patanti santaḥ ।। yady asti nānyac charaṇaṃ sukhāya yuktaṃ tadaitat patanaṃ sukhābhe ।।
asti tv ajaṃ śrīpatipādapadma dvaṃdvārcanaprāpyam anantam ādyam ।। rājyaṃ karasthaṃ svam asau visṛjya bhikṣām aṭed dīnamanāḥ sumūḍhaḥ ।। ananyacittena nareṇa kiṃtu uccāryate keśava mādhaveti ।। evaṃ jano janmaphalaṃ labheta no ced bhavābdhau prapated adho adhaḥ ।।
smarantu nityaṃ varadaṃ mukundaṃ sadbhaktiyogena nivṛttakāmāḥ ।। sarveṣu bhūteṣu ca mitrabhāvaṃ bhajantv ayaṃ sarvagato hi viṣṇuḥ ।। ṣaṇḍāmarkāt paraṃ mitraṃ guruṃ cānyaṃ na vidmahe ।। tvayaitac chikṣitaṃ kutra tathyaṃ no vada nistuṣam ।। b
yadā tātaḥ prayāto me taporthaṃ kānanaṃ mahat ।। d mṛtaṃ vijñāya daityendraṃ hiraṇyakaśipuṃ tadā ।। dahyamāno mahābhāgāṃ mārge gacchati satvaram ।। āgatyendraṃ jagādoccair mūḍha muñca pativratām ।।
tac chrutvā nāradavaco mātaraṃ praṇipatya me ।। nāradas tāṃ samānīya āśramaṃ svaṃ śubhavrataḥ ।। tathā me vismṛtaṃ naiva bālābhyāsād danoḥ sutāḥ ।। ekadā guptacaryāyāṃ gato asau rākṣasādhipaḥ ।।
avait putrakṛtaṃ sarvaṃ balavān dānaveśvaraḥ ।। re re kṣudradvijā yūyam atimumūrṣatāṃ gatāḥ ।। iti nirbhartsya tān viprān śvasan rājāviśad gṛham ।। āsannamaraṇo amarṣāt kṛtyam ekaṃ vimṛśya saḥ ।।
adya kṣapāyāṃ prahlādaṃ prasuptaṃ duṣṭam ulbaṇaiḥ ।। tadājñāṃ śirasādāya dadṛśus tam upetya te ।। saṃchinnarāgalobhādimahābandhaṃ kṣapācarāḥ ।। garuḍadhvajabhaktaṃ taṃ buddhvāhibhir abuddhayaḥ ।।
balinas te acalān daityā tasyopari nidhāya ca ।। prahlādaṃ cābdhimadhyasthaṃ tam aurvāgnim ivāparam ।। sa cābhinnacidānandasindhumadhye samāhitaḥ ।। atha brahmāmṛtāmbhodhi, maye svasmin sthite munau ।।
kleśāt kleśān ivoddhūya prahlādam atha vīcayaḥ ।। dhyānena viṣṇubhūtaṃ taṃ bhagavān varuṇālayaḥ ।। tāvad bhagavatādiṣṭaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ pannagāśanaḥ ।। athābabhāṣe prahlādaṃ gambhīradhvanir arṇavaḥ ।।
prahlāda bhagavadbhakta puṇyātmann arṇavo asmy aham ।। ity ambudhigiraḥ śrutvā sa mahātmā hareḥ priyaḥ ।। kadāgataṃ bhagavatā tam athāmbudhir abravīt ।। baddhas tvam ahibhir daityair mayi kṣipto adya vaiṣṇava ।।
idānīm eva garuḍo bhakṣayitvā gato mahān ।। gṛhāṇemāni ratnāni pūjyas tvaṃ me harir yathā ।। dīpān nivedayaty eva bhāskarasyāpi bhaktimān ।। tvādṛśā nirmalātmāno na santi bahavo arkavat ।।
ālapāmi kṣaṇam api nekṣe hy etat phalopamām ।। yayau lajjāṃ praharṣaṃ ca prahlādo bhagavatpriyaḥ ।। mahātman sutarāṃ dhanyaḥ śete tvayi hi sa prabhuḥ ।। tvayy evaikārṇavībhūte śete kila mahātmani ।।
tvaṃ paśyasi sadā dhanyas tatropāyaṃ prayaccha me ।। prahlādaṃ prāha yogīndra tvaṃ paśyasi sadā hṛdi ।। uktveti sindhuḥ prahlādam ātmanaḥ sa jale aviśat ।। bhaktyāstaud iti manvānas taddarśanam asaṃbhavam ।।
saṃśodhayanti yadavekṣaṇayogyatāyai dhīrāḥ sadaiva sa kathaṃ mama gocaraḥ syāt ।। uparyuparyāvaraṇaiḥ subaddham andhaṃ mano me kva hariḥ kva vāham ।। gatvottamastotrakṛtaḥ kathaṃcit paśyanti taṃ draṣṭum aho mamāśā ।। udvegaduḥkhārṇavamagnamānasaḥ srutāśrudhāro nṛpa mūrcchito apatat ।।
duḥsthaṃ tam āśliṣya sudhāmayair bhujais tatraiva bhūpāvir abhūd dayānidhiḥ ।। prasannavaktraṃ kamalāyatākṣaṃ sudīrghabāhuṃ yamunāsavarṇam ।। sthitaṃ samāliṅgya vibhuṃ sa dṛṣṭvā prakampito vismayabhītiharṣaiḥ ।। iti praharṣārṇavamagnacetāḥ svānandamūrchāṃ sa punaś ca bheje ।।
śanair vidhunvan karapallavena spṛśan muhur mātṛvad āliliṅga ।। āluloke jagannāthaṃ vismayāviṣṭacetasā ।। ātmānaṃ sahasottasthau sadyaḥ sabhayasaṃbhramaḥ ।। saṃbhramāt sa bahujño api nānyāṃ pūjoktim asmarat ।।
gṛhītvā sthāpayāmasa prahlādaṃ sa dayānidhiḥ ।। bhūyo athāhlādayan svāmī taṃ jagādeti sāntvayan ।। naivaṃ priyo me bhakteṣu svādhīnapraṇayī bhava ।। bhaktasarveṣṭadānāya tasmāt kiṃ te priyaṃ vada ।।
salaulyam utphulladṛśā paśyann evaṃ ca tanmukham ।। tvaddarśanāmṛtāsvādād antarātmā na tṛpyati ।। tṛptiṃ neṣyati me cittaṃ kalpāyutaśatair api ।। tataḥ smitasudhāpūraiḥ pūrayan sa priyaṃ priyāt ।।
satyaṃ maddarśanād anyad vatsa naivāsti te priyam ।। prahlādo athābravīd dhīmān deva janmāntareṣv api ।। athāha nāthaḥ prahlādaṃ saṃkaṭaṃ khalv idaṃ kṛtam ।। varān anyāṃś ca varaya dhīman daityeśvarātmaja ।।
prasīda sāstu me nātha tvadbhaktiḥ sāttvikī sthirā ।। athābhituṣṭo bhagavān priyam āha priyaṃvadam ।। antarhite ca mayy atra mā khida tvaṃ mahāmate ।। punar dvitridinais tvaṃ māṃ draṣṭā duṣṭavadhodyatam ।।
uktvety ataḥ praṇamataḥ paśyataś cātilālasam ।। tato haṭhād adṛṣṭvā taṃ sarvato bhaktavatsalam ।। śrūyamāṇe atha paritaḥ pratibuddhajanasvane ।। utthāyābdhitaṭād dhīmān prahlādaḥ svapuraṃ yayau ।।
harimanujagatiṃ tv alaṃ ca paśyan gurugṛham utpulakaḥ śanair avāpa ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe narasiṃhaprādurbhāve tricatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। śaśaṃsur daityapataye yaiḥ kṣiptaḥ sa mahārṇave ।। āhūyatāṃ ca ity āha krodhān mṛtyuvaśe sthitaḥ ।।
āsannamṛtyuṃ daityendraṃ dadarśātyūrjitaśriyam ।। sadhūmāgnim iva vyāptam uccāsanacitisthitam ।। kumārgadarśibhir daityair yamadūtair ivāvṛtam ।। athāhākaraṇakrodhaḥ sa khalo bhartsayan sutam ।।
mūḍha re śṛṇu madvākyam etad evāntimaṃ dhruvam ।। uktveti drūtam ākṛṣya candrahāsāsim adbhutam ।। kva cāsti mūḍha te viṣṇuḥ sa tvām adya prarakṣatu ।। yadi paśyāmi taṃ viṣṇum adhunā stambhamadhyagam ।।
prahlādo api tathā dṛṣṭvā dadhyau taṃ parameśvaram ।। tāvatprasphuṭitastambho vīkṣito daityasūnunā ।। tanmadhye dṛśyate rūpaṃ bahuyojanam āyatam ।। mahānetraṃ mahāvaktraṃ mahādaṃṣṭraṃ mahābhujam ।।
karṇāntakṛtavistāravadanaṃ cātibhīṣaṇam ।। narasiṃhaḥ stambhamadhyād nirgatya praṇanāda ca ।। tān hatvā sakalāṃs tatra svapauruṣaparākramāt ।। vārayāmasur abhyetya narasiṃhaṃ mahābhaṭāḥ ।।
tataḥ śastrāṇi varṣanti narasiṃhe pratāpini ।। nanāda ca mahānādaṃ diśaḥ śabdena pūrayan ।। aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi hetihastān samādiśat ।। hatvā tān akhilān yuddhe yudhyamāno nanāda saḥ ।।
tān hatān api vijñāya krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ ।। uvāca ca mahīpāla dānavān baladarpitān ।। ity evaṃ vadatas tasya pramukhe tu mahāsurān ।। tato atidudruvur daityā hataśeṣā diśo diśaḥ ।।
narasiṃhena tāvac ca nabhobhāgaṃ gato raviḥ ।। pragṛhya tu balād rājan narasiṃho mahābalaḥ ।। nakhair kisalayam iva dārayaty āha so asuraḥ ।। tan me tāvad uro nṛsiṃhakarajair vyādīryate sāṃprataṃ daive durjanatāṃ gate tṛṇam api prāyo apy avajñāyate ।।
hṛdayaṃ daityarājasya padmapatram iva dvipaḥ ।। tataḥ kva yāto duṣṭo asāv iti devo ativismitaḥ ।। iti saṃcintya rājendra narasiṃho mahābalaḥ ।। nakharandhrān nipatite bhūmau reṇusame hareḥ ।।
puṣpavarṣaṃ ca varṣanto narasiṃhasya mūrdhani ।। āgatya pūjayāmasur narasiṃhaṃ paraṃ prabhum ।। dharme ratiḥ samastānāṃ janānām abhavat tadā ।। narasiṃho api bhagavān sarvalokahitāya vai ।।
sthito bhaktahitārthāya abhaktānāṃ kṣamāya ca ।। śṛṇoti vā nṛpaśreṣṭha mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।। vaidhavyād duḥkhaśokāc ca duṣṭasaṅgāt pramucyate ।। adharmiṣṭho anabhogī ca śṛṇvan śuddho bhaven naraḥ ।।
kṛtvā virūpaṃ ca purātmamāyayā hiraṇyakaṃ duḥkhakaraṃ nakhaiś chinat ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe narasiṃhaprādurbhāvo nāma catuścatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। baliyāge hatā yena purā daityāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। trailokyaṃ bubhuje jitvā devān indrapurogamān ।।
indraṃ kṛśataraṃ dṛṣṭvā naṣṭarājyaṃ nṛpottama ।। tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ praṇipatya janārdanam ।। sthitvā tatpurato vācam uvāca madhusūdanaḥ ।। ity uktvā tāṃ gato viṣṇuḥ svagṛhaṃ sā samāyayau ।।
ajāyata sa viśveśo bhagavān vāmanākṛtiḥ ।। jātakarmādikāḥ sarvāḥ kriyās tatra cakāra vai ।। aditiṃ capy anujñāpya yajñaśālāṃ baler yayau ।। yajñabhāgān na gṛhṇanti dānavāś ca baler makhāt ।।
viparītam idaṃ dṛṣṭvā śukram āha mahābalaḥ ।। kasmāc ca vahnayaḥ śāntāḥ kasmād bhūś calati dvija ।। ityukto balinā śukro dānavendraṃ vaco abravīt ।। teṣāṃ rājyapradānāya adityām acyuto asura ।।
sa tv āgacchati te yajñaṃ tadpadanyāsakampitā ।। tatsaṃnidhānād asurā na gṛhṇanti havir makhe ।। ṛtvijaś ca na bhāsante homamantro bale adhunā ।। ityuktaḥ sa baliḥ prāha śukraṃ nītimatāṃ varam ।।
yan mayā cādya kartavyaṃ vāmanasyāsya dhīmataḥ ।। tan me vada mahābhāga tvaṃ hi naḥ paramo guruḥ ।। b iti saṃcoditaḥ śukraḥ sa rājñā balinā nṛpa ।। d devānām upakārāya bhavatāṃ saṃkṣayāya ca ।।
āgate vāmane deve tvayā tasya mahātmanaḥ ।। iti śrutvā vacas tasya balir balavatāṃ varaḥ ।। āgate vāmane śukra yajñe me madhusūdane ।। anyeṣām api jantūnām ity uktaṃ te mayādhunā ।।
tvayā vighno na kartavyo vāmane atrāgate dvija ।। kṛtārtho ahaṃ muniśreṣṭha yady āgacchati vāmanaḥ ।। āgatya praviveśātha praśaśaṃsa baler makham ।। upacāreṇa saṃpūjya vākyam etad uvāca ha ।।
tat sarvaṃ tava dāsyāmi māṃ yācasvādya vāmana ।। yācayāmasa deveśo bhūmer dehi padatrayam ।। ityukto vāmanenātha baliḥ prāha ca vāmanam ।। evam ukte tu balinā vāmano balim abravīt ।।
ityukto devadevena tadā tatra svayaṃ baliḥ ।। yāvat sa vāmanakare toyaṃ dātum upasthitaḥ ।। tataś ca vāmanaḥ kruddhaḥ pavitrāgreṇa sattama ।। tato vyapagataḥ śukro viddhaikākṣo narottama ।।
kare nipatite toye vāmano vavṛdhe kṣaṇāt ।। antarikṣaṃ dvitīyena dyaus tṛtīyena sattama ।। puraṃdarāya trailokyaṃ dattvā balim uvāca ha ।। tasmāt te sāṃprataṃ dattaṃ pātālatalam uttamam ।।
vaivasvate antare atīte punar indro bhaviṣyasi ।। praṇamya ca tato gatvā talaṃ bhogam avāptavān ।। samāgatās tribhuvanaṃ rājan devasamanvitaḥ ।। sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।।
kṛtvā prasādaṃ ca divaukasāṃ pater dattvā trilokaṃ sa yayau mahodadhim ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe vāmanaprādurbhāve pañcacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। jāmadagnyaṃ purā yena kṣatram utsāditaṃ śṛṇu ।। ṛṣibhiś ca mahābhāgair jamadagneḥ suto abhavat ।।
duṣṭānāṃ nigrahaṃ kartum avatīrṇo mahītale ।। dattātreyaṃ samārādhya cakravartitvam āptavān ।। jamadagnis tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā caturaṅgabalānvitam ।। vanyādikaṃ mayā dattaṃ bhuktvā gaccha mahāmate ।।
āmantrya rājānam alaṅghyakīrtir muniḥ sa dhenuṃ ca dudoha dogdhrīm ।। sāmantayogyāni śubhāni rājan samicchatāṃ yāni sukānanāni ।। dugdhvā prakalpan munir āha pārthivaṃ gṛhaṃ kṛtaṃ te praviśeha rājan ।। hastyaśvajātyaś ca viśantu śālāṃ bhṛtyāś ca nīceṣu gṛheṣu santu ।।
anyeṣu cānyeṣu gṛheṣu satsu muniḥ punaḥ pārthivam ābabhāṣe ।। snāhi tvam adyātra yathāprakāmaṃ yathā surendro divi nṛtyagītaiḥ ।। snātasya tasyāśu śubhe ca vastre dadau munir bhūpa vibhūṣite dve ।। muniś ca dugdhvānnamayaṃ mahāgiriṃ nṛpāya bhṛtyāya ca dattavān asau ।।
rātrau ca gītādivinodayuktaḥ śete sa rājā muninirmite gṛhe ।। bhūmibhāgaṃ tataḥ kaṃcid dṛṣṭvāsau cintayan nṛpaḥ ।। surabhyā vā mahābhāga brūhi me tvaṃ purohita ।। muneḥ sāmarthyam apy asti siddhiś ceyaṃ hi gor nṛpa ।।
yas tv etāṃ hartum icched vai tasya nāśo dhruvaṃ bhavet ।। rājakāryaṃ ne paśyed vai svapakṣasyaiva poṣaṇāt ।। tathā suvarṇapātrāṇi śayanādīni ca striyaḥ ।। asmābhis tatra dṛṣṭāni nīyatāṃ dhenur uttamā ।।
gatavāham ānayiṣyāmi ājñāṃ me dehi bhūbhuja ।। sacivas tatra gatvātha surabhiṃ hartum ārabhat ।। rājayogyām imāṃ brahman dehi rājñe mahāmate ।। ity uktvā tāṃ balād dhṛtvā netuṃ mantrī pracakrame ।।
tato mantrī suduṣṭātmā muniṃ hatvā tu taṃ nṛpa ।। rājā ca kṣubdhahṛdayo yayau māhiṣmatīṃ purīm ।। trisaptakṛtvaḥ svāṃ kukṣiṃ tāḍayāmasa pārthiva ।। puṣpādīni gṛhītvā tu vanān mātaram abravīt ।।
haniṣyāmi durācāram arjunaṃ duṣṭamantriṇam ।। triḥsaptakṛtvas tasmāt tu haniṣye bhuvi pārthivān ।। māhiṣmatīṃ purīṃ prāpya kārtavīryam athāhvayat ।। tayor yuddham abhūt tatra bhairavaṃ lomaharṣaṇam ।।
tataḥ paraśurāmo abhūn mahābalaparākramaḥ ।। kārtavīryabalaṃ sarvam anekaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ saha ।। chinne bāhuvane tasya śiraś ciccheda bhārgavaḥ ।। divyarūpadharaḥ śrīmān divyagandhānulepanaḥ ।।
krodhāt paraśurāmo api mahābalaparākramaḥ ।। kṣatriyāṇāṃ vadhāt tena bhūmer bhāro avatāritaḥ ।। ity eṣa jāmadagnyākhyaḥ prādurbhāvo mayoditaḥ ।। yaś ca tac chṛṇuyād bhaktyā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
kṣātraṃ ca tejo pravibhajya rājan rāmaḥ sthito adyāpi girau mahendre ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe paraśurāmaprādurbhāvo nāma ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। nihato rāvaṇo yena sagaṇo devakaṇṭakaḥ ।। tasya vai viśravā nāma putro abhūt tasya rākṣasaḥ ।।
tapasā mahatā yuktaḥ sa tu lokān upādravat ।। yakṣāś ca dānavāś caiva tena rājan vinirjitāḥ ।। devādīnāṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha ratnāni vividhani ca ।। tatpurīṃ jagṛhe laṅkāṃ vimānaṃ cāpi puṣpakam ।।
putrāś ca bahavas tasya babhūvur amitaujasaḥ ।। anekakoṭayo rājan laṅkāyāṃ nivasanti ye ।। yakṣāṃś caiva tataḥ sarve ghātayanti divāniśam ।। duḥkhābhibhūtam atyarthaṃ saṃbabhūva narādhipa ।।
siddhā vidyādharāś caiva gandharvāḥ kiṃnarās tathā ।। brahmāṇam agrataḥ kṛtvā śaṃkaraṃ ca narādhipa ।। tatrārādhya hariṃ devās tasthuḥ prāñjalayas tadā ।। prāñjaliḥ praṇato bhūtvā vāsudevam athāstuvan ।।
namaḥ śrīkarasaṃspṛṣṭadivyapādāya viṣṇave ।। tārkṣyāsanāya devāya govindāya namo namaḥ ।। namo aravindapādāya padmanābhāya viṣṇave ।। śubhāṅgāya sunetrāya mādhavāya namo namaḥ ।।
suvaktrāya sukarṇāya śrīdharāya namo namaḥ ।। subhruve cārudehāya cārudantāya śārṅgiṇe ।। sunakhāya suśāntāya suvidyāya gadābhṛte ।। asuraghnāya cogrāya rakṣoghnāya namo namaḥ ।।
namas te lokanāthāya rāvaṇāntakṛte namaḥ ।। svarūpaṃ darśayitvā tu pitāmaham uvāca ha ।। yat kāryaṃ brūhi me brahman yadarthaṃ saṃstutas tvayā ।। sarvadevagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ brahmā prāha janārdanam ।।
sendrāḥ parājitās tena bahuśo rakṣasā vibho ।। devakanyā hṛtās tena balāc chatasahasraśaḥ ।। na samarthā yato devās tvam atas tadvadhaṃ kuru ।। śṛṇuṣvāvahito brahman yad vadāmi hitaṃ vacaḥ ।।
nāmnā daśarathakhyātas tasya putro bhavāmy aham ।। svāṃśair vānararūpeṇa sakalā devatāgaṇāḥ ।। ityukto devadevena brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। svāṃśair vānararūpeṇa avateruś ca bhūtale ।।
iṣṭiṃ tu kārayāmasa putraprāptikarīṃ nṛpaḥ ।। vahniḥ kuṇḍāt samuttasthau nūnaṃ devena noditaḥ ।। datte kauśalyakaikeyyor dve piṇḍe mantramantrite ।। piṇḍābhyām alpam alpaṃ tu subhāginyāḥ prayacchataḥ ।।
piṇḍān devakṛtān prāśya prāpur garbhān aninditān ।। svāṃśair lokahitāyaiva caturdhā jagatīpate ।। jātakarmādikaṃ prāpya saṃskāraṃ munisaṃskṛtam ।। rāmaś ca lakṣmaṇaś caiva saha nityaṃ viceratuḥ ।।
vavṛdhāte mahāvīryau śrutiśabdātilakṣaṇau ।। vedaśāstrāṇi bubudhe śastraśāstraṃ nṛpottama ।। yāgena yaṣṭum ārebhe vidhinā madhusūdanam ।। netuṃ sa yāgarākṣārthaṃ saṃprāpto rāmalakṣmaṇau ।।
daśarathas tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā pratyutthāya mahāmatiḥ ।। sa pūjito muniḥ prāha rājānaṃ rājasaṃmnidhau ।। tat kāryaṃ nṛpaśārdūla kathayāmi tavāgrataḥ ।। yajñasya rakṣaṇārthaṃ me dehi tvaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇau ।।
viṣaṇṇavadano bhūtva viśvāmitram uvāca ha ।। ahaṃ tvayā sahāgatya śaktyā rakṣāmi te makham ।। rāmo api śaknute nūnaṃ sarvān nāśayituṃ nṛpa ।। ato me dehi rāmaṃ ca na cintāṃ kartum arhasi ।।
tuṣṇīṃ sthitvā kṣaṇaṃ rājā munivaryam uvāca ha ।। rājīvalocanaṃ rāmam ahaṃ dāsye sahānujam ।। ato ahaṃ caturaṅgeṇa balena sahito mune ।। viśvāmitraḥ punaḥ prāha rājānam amitaujasam ।।
śeṣanārāyaṇāv etau tava putrau na saṃśayaḥ ।। avatīrṇau na saṃdeho gṛhe tava narādhipa ।। niḥkṣepe ca mahārāja arpayiṣyāmi te sutau ।। tacchāpabhīto manasā nīyatām ity abhāṣata ।।
tataḥ siddhāśramaṃ rājan saṃpratasthe sa kauśikaḥ ।। anuvrajyābravīd etad vaco daśarathas tadā ।। muniprasādād adhunā putravān asmi sattama ।। tvam eva jānāsi mune nītvā śīghraṃ prayaccha me ।।
samāptayajñaś ca punar neṣye rāmaṃ ca lakṣmaṇam ।। ityuktaḥ preṣayāmasa rāmaṃ lakṣmaṇasaṃyutam ।। viśvāmitras tu tau gṛhya ayodhyāyā yayau śanaiḥ ।। tayoḥ prītyā sa rājendra dve vidye prathamaṃ dadau ।।
kṣutpipāsāpanayane punaś caiva mahāmatiḥ ।। āśramāni ca divyāni munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।। gaṅgām uttīrya śoṇasya tīram āsādya paścimam ।। ṛṣibhyaś ca varān prāpya tena nītau nṛpātmajau ।।
gate tatra nṛpaśreṣṭha viśvāmitro mahātapāḥ ।। rāvaṇasya niyogena vasaty asmin mahāvane tayā manuṣyā bahavo muniputrā mṛgās tathā ।। ity evamukto muninā rāmas taṃ munim abravīt ।। strīvadhe tu mahāpāpaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
tasyās tu nidhanād rāma janāḥ sarve nirākulāḥ ।। ity evaṃ vādini munau viśvāmitre niśācarī ।। muninā prerito rāmas tāṃ dṛṣṭvā vivṛtānanām ।। tāṃ vilokya vanitāvadhe ghṛṇāṃ patriṇā saha mumoca rāghavaḥ ।।
vipāṭitaṃ dvidhā rājan sā papāta mamāra ca ।। prāpayāmasa taṃ tatra nānāṛṣiniṣevitam ।। nānānirjharatoyāḍhyaṃ vindhyaśailāntarasthitam ।। rakṣārthaṃ tāv ubhau sthāpya śikṣayitvā viśeṣataḥ ।।
dīkṣāṃ praviṣṭe ca munau viśvāmitre mahātmani ।। mārīcaś ca subāhuś ca bahavaś cānyarākṣasāḥ ।। tān āgatān sa vijñāya rāmaḥ kamalalocanaḥ ।। asṛkpravāhaṃ varṣantaṃ mārīcaṃ bhallakena tu ।।
śeṣāṃs tu hatavān rāmo lakṣmaṇāś ca niśācarān ।। samāpya yāgaṃ vidhivat pūjayāmasa ṛtvijān ।। rāmaṃ ca lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva pūjayāmasa bhaktitaḥ ।। vavarṣa puṣpavarṣaṃ tu rāmadevasya mūrdhani ।।
śrutvā nānākathāḥ puṇyā rāmo bhrātṛsamanvitaḥ ।। vyabhicārān mahendreṇa bhartrā śaptā hi sā purā ।। ahalyā muktaśāpā ca jagāma gautamaṃ prati ।। kṛtadāro mayā neyo rāmaḥ kamalalocanaḥ ।।
śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto anekair jagāma mithilāṃ prati ।। rājaputrā mahāvīryāḥ pūrvaṃ sītābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। yat sītāyāḥ samutpannaṃ dhanur māheśvaraṃ mahat ।। raṅge mahati vistīrṇe sthāpayāmasa tad dhanuḥ ।।
ākarṣaṇād idaṃ yena dhanur bhagnaṃ nṛpātmajāḥ ।। ity evaṃ śrāvite tena janakena mahātmanā ।। dhanuṣā tāḍitāḥ sarve kramāt tena mahīpate ।। teṣu bhagneṣu janakas tad dhanus tryambakaṃ nṛpa ।।
viśvāmitras tataḥ prāpto mithilādhipater gṛham ।। rāmalakṣmaṇasaṃyuktaṃ śiṣyaiś cābhigataṃ tadā ।। rāmaṃ raghupatiṃ cāpi lāvaṇyādiguṇair yutam ।। pūjayitvā yathānyāyaṃ janakaḥ prītamānasaḥ ।।
viśvāmitram uvācātha kiṃ kartavyaṃ mayeti saḥ ।। eṣa rāmo mahārāja viṣṇuḥ sākṣān mahīpatiḥ ।। asmai sītāṃ prayaccha tvaṃ devakanyām iva sthitām ।। tad ānaya bhavadhanur arcayasva janādhipa ।।
anekabhūbhujāṃ bhaṅgi sthāpayāmasa pūrvavat ।। teṣāṃ madhyāt samutthāya rāmaḥ kamalalocanaḥ ।। sajyaṃ kṛtvā mahābāhur jyāghoṣam akarot tadā ।। sītā ca mālam ādāya śubhāṃ rāmasya mūrdhani ।।
tatas te kṣatriyāḥ kruddhā rāmam āsādya sarvataḥ ।। tān nirīkṣya tato rāmo dhanur ādāya vegavān ।। ciccheda śarajālāni teṣāṃ svāstrai rathāṃs tataḥ ।। saṃnahya svabalaṃ sarvaṃ mithilādhipatis tataḥ ।।
lakṣmaṇas ca mahāvīro vidrāvya yudhi tān nṛpān ।। vāhanāni parityajya palāyanaparān nṛpān ।। mithilādhipatis taṃ ca vārayāmasa kauśikaḥ ।। ādāya prativeśātha janakaḥ svagṛhaṃ śubham ।।
śrutvā dūtamukhāt sarvaṃ viditārthaḥ saḥ pārthivaḥ ।। mithilām ājagāmāśu svabalena samanvitaḥ ।। vidhivat kṛtaśulkāṃ tāṃ dadau rāmāya pārthiva ।। tribhyas tu lakṣmaṇādibhyaḥ svakanyā vidhivad dadau ।।
bhrātṛbhir mātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ pitrā balavatā saha ।। dṛṣṭvā daśarathaṃ rājā sītāyāḥ pradadau vasu ।। hastyaśvadāsān api karmayogyān dāsījanāṃś ca pravarāḥ striyaś ca ।। vedādighoṣair bahumaṅgalaiś ca saṃpreṣayāṃ āsa sa pārthivo balī ।।
viśvāmitraṃ namaskṛtya janakaḥ saṃnivṛttavān ।। bhartṛbhaktiṃ kuru śubhe śvaśrūṇāṃ śvaśurasya ca ।। tatas tu rāmaṃ gacchantam ayodhyāṃ prabalānvitam ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā rājapuruṣāḥ sarve te dīnamānasāḥ ।।
sabhāryaḥ saparīvāro bhārgavasya bhayān nṛpa ।। vasiṣṭhaś corjitatapā brahmacārī mahāmuniḥ ।। yuṣmābhir atra rāmārthaṃ na kāryaṃ duḥkham aṇv api ।। ayaṃ hi nṛpate rāma sākṣād viṣṇus tu te gṛhe ।।
yasya saṃkīrtyaṃ nāmāpi bhavabhītiḥ praṇaśyati ।। yatra saṃkīrtyate rāmakathāmātram api prabho ।। ityukte bhārgavo rāmo rāmam āhāgrataḥ sthitam ।। ityukte rāghavaḥ prāha bhārgavaṃ taṃ pathi sthitam ।।
ity uktvā taṃ pṛthak sthitvā rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ ।। tataḥ paraśurāmasya dehān niṣkramya vaiṣṇavam ।। dṛṣṭvā taṃ bhārgavo rāmaḥ prasannavadano abravīt ।। viṣṇur eva bhavāñ jāto jñāto asy adya mayā vibho ।।
duṣṭānāṃ nidhanaṃ kṛtvā śiṣṭāṃś ca paripālaya ।। ity uktvā pūjitas tais tu munibhāvena bhārgavaḥ ।। tatas tu jātaharṣās te janā daśarathaś ca ha ।। divyaśobhāṃ purīṃ kṛtvā sarvato bhadraśālinīm ।।
viśantaṃ rāmam āgatya kṛtadāraṃ raṇe ajitam ।। tau dṛṣṭvā sa muniḥ prāptau rāmaṃ lakṣmaṇam antike ।। viśvāmitraś ca sahasā pratigantuṃ mano dadhe ।। punaḥ punaḥ śrāvya hasan mahāmatir jagāma siddhāśramam evam ātmanaḥ ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe rāmaprādurbhāve saptacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। pitre sumahatīṃ prītiṃ janānām upapādayan ।। prītyā nandaty ayodhyāyāṃ rāme raghupatau nṛpa ।। tato daśaratho rājā prasamīkṣya suśobhanam ।।
abhiṣicya rājyabhāraṃ rāme saṃsthāpya vaiṣṇavam ।। saṃcintya tatparo rājā sarvadikṣu samādiśat ।। rāmābhiṣekadravyāṇi ṛṣiproktāni yāni vai ।। dūtāmātyāḥ samādeśāt sarvadikṣu narādhipān ।।
ayodhyāpuram atyarthaṃ sarvaśobhāsamanvitam ।। puravāsijanānandaṃ deśavāsimanaḥpriyam ।। śrutvetthaṃ mantriṇaḥ prāhus taṃ nṛpaṃ praṇipatya ca ।। rāmābhiṣekam asmākaṃ sarveṣāṃ ca priyaṃkaram ।।
ānīyantāṃ drutaṃ sarve saṃbhārā mama śāsanāt ।। adya śobhānvitā kāryā kartavyaṃ yāgamaṇḍalam ।। tathaiva cakrus te sarve punaḥ punar udīritāḥ ।। kauśalyā lakṣmaṇaś caiva sumitrā nāgaro janaḥ ।।
śvaśruśvaśurayoḥ samyak śuśrūṣaṇaparā tu sā ।। śvobhāviny abhiṣeke tu rāmasya viditātmanaḥ ।। svāṃ svāminīṃ tu kaikeyīm idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। tvatpatis tu mahārājas tava nāśāya codyataḥ ।।
vasuvāhanakośādi rājyaṃ ca sakalaṃ śubhe ।। bharato api gato dūraṃ mātulasya gṛhaṃ prati ।। saivam ākarṇya kaikeyī kubjām idam athābravīt ।। yathā tu sakalaṃ rājyaṃ bharatasya bhaviṣyati ।।
ity uktvā mantharāṃ sā tu unmucya svāṅgabhūṣaṇam ।। nirmālyapuṣpadhṛk kaṣṭā kaśmalāṅgī virūpiṇī ।। bhūbhāge śāntadīpe sā saṃdhyākāle suduḥkhitā ।। mantribhiḥ saha kāryāṇi saṃmantrya sakalāni tu ।।
ṛṣibhis tu vasiṣṭhādyaiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃbhāramaṇḍape ।। gītanṛtyasamakīrṇe śaṅkhakāhalaniḥsvanaiḥ ।। kaikeyyā veśmano dvāraṃ jaradbhiḥ parirakṣitam ।। kaikeyībhavanaṃ vīkṣya sāndhakāram athābravīt ।।
rāmābhiṣekaṃ harṣāya antyajā api menire ।। tvayādya na kṛtaṃ kasmād ity uktvā ca mahīpatiḥ ।। aśobhanāṅgīṃ kaikeyīṃ svapatnīṃ patitāṃ bhuvi ।। āśliṣyotthāya tāṃ rājā śṛṇu me paramaṃ vacaḥ ।।
tasyābhiṣekaṃ rāmasya śvo bhaviṣyati śobhane ।। muñcantī dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca roṣocchvāsaṃ muhur muhuḥ ।। kiṃ te kaikeyi duḥkhasya kāraṇaṃ vada śobhane ।। tat tvaṃ gṛhṇīṣva niḥśaṅkaṃ bhāṇḍārāt sukhinī bhava ।।
yadābhiṣekaṃ saṃprāpte rāme rājīvalocane ।। bhaviṣyati punaḥ pūrṇaṃ rāme rājyaṃ praśāsati ।। ityuktā rājavaryeṇa kaikeyī pāpalakṣaṇā ।। rājānaṃ svapatiṃ vākyaṃ krūram atyantaniṣṭhuram ।।
devāsuramahāyuddhe prītyā yan me varadvayam ।। ityuktaḥ pārthivaḥ prāha kaikeyīm aśubhāṃ tadā ।। kiṃ me pratiśrutaṃ pūrvaṃ dattam eva mayā tava ।। rāmābhiṣekajaṃ harṣaṃ bhajottiṣṭha sukhī bhava ।।
uvāca paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ rājño maraṇakāraṇam ।। śvobhūte gacchatu vanaṃ rāmo ayaṃ kośalātmajaḥ ।। abhiṣekaṃ ca rājyaṃ ca bharatasya bhaviṣyati ।। papāta bhuvi niḥsaṃjño rājā sāpi vibhūṣitā ।।
dūtaṃ sumantram āhaivaṃ rāma ānīyatām iti ।। yāgamaṇḍapamadhyasthaḥ śaṅkhatūryaravānvitaḥ ।। rāma rāma mahābāho ājñāpayati te pitā ।। ityuktas tena dūtena śīghram utthāya rāghavaḥ ।।
praviśantaṃ gṛhaṃ rāmaṃ kaikeyī prāha nirghṛṇā ।। vane vasa mahābāho gatvā tvaṃ dvādaśābdakam ।। na cintyam anyathā vatsa ādarāt kuru me vacaḥ ।। tathety ājñāṃ gṛhītvāsau namaskṛtya ca tāv ubhau ।।
kauśalyāṃ ca namaskṛtya sumitrāṃ gantum udyataḥ ।। vivyathuś cātha saumitriḥ kaikeyīṃ prati roṣitaḥ ।। vārayāmasa dharmajño dharmavāgbhir mahāmatiḥ ।। rāmo rathaṃ khinnasūtaṃ prasthānāyāruroha vai ।।
śraddhayā parayā dattvā vastrāṇi vividhāni ca ।। muñcantam aśrudhārāṇi netrayoḥ śokajāni ca ।। ratham āruhya gacchantaṃ sītayā saha rāghavam ।। rāmaṃ daśarathaṃ viddhi māṃ viddhi janakātmajām ।।
mātraivamukto dharmātmā stanakṣīrārdradehayā ।। gacchato lakṣmaṇo bhrātā sītā caiva pativratā ।। vidhicchinnābhiṣekaṃ taṃ rāmaṃ rājīvalocanam ।। mantriṇaḥ pauramukhyāś ca duḥkhena mahatānvitāḥ ।।
rāma rāma mahābāho gantuṃ nārhasi śobhana ।। ityukto rāghavas tais tu tān uvāca dṛḍhavrataḥ ।। pitrādeśaṃ mayā kāryam abhiyāsyāmi vai vanam ।। āgacchāmi pituḥ pādaṃ mātṝṇāṃ draṣṭum añjasā ।।
taṃ gacchantaṃ punar yātāḥ pṛṣṭhato duḥkhitā janāḥ ।। mātṝś ca pitaraṃ caiva śatrughnaṃ nagarīm imām ।। pālayadhvaṃ mahābhāgās tapase yāmy ahaṃ vanam ।। sītām arpaya rājānaṃ janakaṃ mithileśvaram ।।
ityuktaḥ prāha dharmātmā lakṣmaṇo bhrātṛvatsalaḥ ।। gantum icchasi yatra tvam avaśyaṃ tatra yāmy aham ।। sīte gaccha mamādeśāt pitaraṃ prati śobhane ।। nivartasva hi tāvat tvaṃ yāvad āgamanaṃ mama ।।
yatra gatvā vane vāsaṃ tvaṃ karoṣi mahābhuja ।। viyogaṃ no sahe rājaṃs tvayā satyavatā kvacit ।। gantum icchasi yatra tvam avaśyaṃ tatra yāmy aham ।। yoṣitāṃ ca gaṇān rāmo vārayāmasa dharmavit ।।
gatvāhaṃ daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ tapase dhṛtamānasaḥ ।। lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā vaidehyā ca svabhāryayā ।। guhas tu rāmabhakto asau svabhāvād eva vaiṣṇavaḥ ।। mahatā tapasaānītā guruṇā yā hi vaḥ purā ।।
nānāmunijanair juṣṭā kūrmamatsyasamākulā ।। guhopanītanāvā tu tāṃ gaṅgāṃ sa mahādyutiḥ ।। prayāge tu tatas tasmin snātvā tīrthe yathāvidhi ।। bharadvājāśrame tatra viśrāntas tena pūjitaḥ ।।
bharadvājoktamārgeṇa citrakūṭaṃ śanair yayau ।। tāpasaṃ veṣam āsthāya jahnukanyām atītya vai ।। ayodhyām avasan bhūpa naṣṭasobhāṃ suduḥkhitāḥ ।। rāmapravāsajananaṃ kaikeyyā mukhaniḥsṛtam ।।
kaikeyy uvāca bhūpālaṃ bharataṃ cābhiṣecaya ।। putraśokābhisaṃtapto rājā daśarathas tadā ।। tatas tasya mahāpuryyām ayodhyāyām ariṃdama ।। kauśalyā ca sumitrā ca kaikeyī kaṣṭakāriṇī ।।
tataḥ purohitas tatra vasiṣṭhaḥ sarvadharmavit ।। dūtaṃ vai preṣayāmasa sahamantrigaṇaiḥ sthitaḥ ।। tatra prāpya tathā vārtā saṃnivartya nṛpātmajau ।। krūrāṇi dṛṣṭvā bharato nimittāni ca vai pathi ।।
niḥśobhāṃ nirgataśrīkāṃ duḥkhaśokānvitāṃ purīm ।। duḥkhānvitā janāḥ sarve tau dṛṣṭvā rurudur bhṛśam ।। ruroda bharatas tatra śatrughnaś ca suduḥkhitaḥ ।। duṣṭā tvaṃ duṣṭacittā ca yayā rāmaḥ pravāsitaḥ ।।
sāhasaṃ kiṃ kṛtaṃ duṣṭe tvayā sadyo alpabhāgyayā ।। mamaiva putraṃ rājānaṃ karotv iti matis tava ।। bhrātrā rāmeṇa rahito nāhaṃ rājyaṃ karomi vai ।। dharmajño sarvaśāstrajño matimān bandhuvatsalaḥ ।।
pativratā mahābhāgā sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutā ।। tatra yāsyāmi kaikeyi mahat pāpaṃ tvayā kṛtam ।। sa eva rājā duṣṭātme bhṛtyo ahaṃ tasya vai sadā ।। hā rājan pṛthivīpāla māṃ vihāya suduḥkhitam ।।
bhrātā pitrā samaḥ kvāste jyeṣṭho me karunākaraḥ ।। ity evaṃ vilapantaṃ taṃ bharataṃ mantribhiḥ saha ।। uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha vatsa tvaṃ na śokaṃ kartum arhasi ।। tasya saṃskārakāryāṇi karmāṇi kuru śobhana ।।
avatīrṇo jagatsvāmī svāṃśena bhuvi mādhavaḥ ।। yatrāsau bhagavān vīraḥ karmaṇā tena coditaḥ ।। ityukto bharatas tena vasiṣṭhena mahātmanā ।। agnihotrāgninā dagdhvā pitur dehaṃ vidhānataḥ ।।
śatrughnena saha śrīmān mātṛbhir bāndhavaiḥ saha ।। hastyaśvarathapattībhiḥ saha prāyān mahāmatiḥ ।। tam āyāntaṃ mahāsenaṃ rāmasyānuvirodhinam ।। svaṃ sainyaṃ vartulaṃ kṛtvā saṃnaddhaḥ kavacī rathī ।।
mahābalaparīvāro rurodha bharataṃ pathi ।। prāpayas tvaṃ vanaṃ duṣṭa sāṃprataṃ hantum icchasi ।। ityukto bharatas tatra guhena nṛpanandanaḥ ।। yathā tvaṃ rāmabhakto asi tathāham api bhaktimān ।।
rāmasyānayanārthāya vrajāmy adya mahāmate ।। iti viśvāsam ānīya jāhnavīṃ tena tāritaḥ ।। bharadvājāśramaṃ prāpto bharatas taṃ mahāmunim ।। bharadvājo api taṃ prāha kālena kṛtam īdṛśam ।।
vartate citrakūṭe asau rāmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ ।। tathāpi tatra gaccha tvaṃ yas asau vakti tat kuru ।। lakṣmaṇas tu mahāvīryo duṣṭālokanatatparaḥ ।। uttīrya yamunāṃ yātaś citrakūṭaṃ mahān agam ।।
rāmāya kathayitvāsa tadādeśāt tu lakṣmaṇaḥ ।। sa tato dṛṣṭavān hṛṣṭām āyāntīṃ mahatīṃ camūm ।। he bhrātas tvaṃ mahābāho sītāpārśve sthiro bhava ।। ity ākarṇya vacas tasya lakṣmaṇasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
prāyeṇa bharato asmākaṃ draṣṭum āyāti lakṣmaṇa ।। ārāt saṃsthāpya senāṃ tāṃ bharato vinayānvitaḥ ।। rāmasya nipapātātha vaidehyā lakṣmaṇasya ca ।। parivārya tato rāmaṃ ruruduḥ śokakātarāḥ ।।
lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā vaidehyātha samanvitaḥ ।। mātrādīn abhivādyātha rāmo duḥkhasamanvitaḥ ।। ayodhyāṃ gaccha bharata itaḥ śīghraṃ mahāmate ।। ityukto bharato prāha rāmaṃ rājīvalocanam ।।
yatra tvaṃ tatra yāsyāmi vaidehī lakṣmaṇo yathā ।। nṛṇāṃ pitṛsamo jyeṣṭhaḥ svadharmam anuvartinām ।। tathā tvayā na laṅghyaṃ syād vacanaṃ mama sattama ।। dvādaśābdikam etan me vrataṃ pitṛmukheritam ।।
gaccha tiṣṭha mamādeśe na duḥkhaṃ kartum arhasi ।। yathā pitā tathā tvaṃ me nātra karyā vicāraṇā ।। nandigrāme vasiṣye ahaṃ pāduke dvādaśābdikam ।। tvaṃ dvādaśābdikād ūrdhvaṃ yadi nāyāsi sattama ।।
ity evaṃ śapathaṃ kṛtvā bharato hi suduḥkhitaḥ ।। pāduke śirasā sthāpya bharataḥ prasthitaḥ śanaiḥ ।। tapasvī niyatāhāraḥ śākamūlaphalāśanaḥ ।। rāmasya vākyādarato hṛdi sthitaṃ babhāra bhūbhāram aninditātmā ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe śrīrāmaprādurbhāve aṣṭacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā bhāryayā sītayā saha ।। kadācil lakṣmaṇam ṛte rāmadevaḥ pratāpavān ।। suṣvāpa sa muhūrtaṃ tu tataḥ kāko durātmavān ।।
vidārya vṛkṣam āruhya sthito asau vāyasādhamaḥ ।। śokāviṣṭāṃ tu sītāṃ tām uvāca kamalekṣaṇaḥ ।। ityuktā sā ca taṃ prāha bhartāraṃ vinayānvitā ।। anenaiva kṛtaṃ karma supte tvayi mahāmate ।।
iṣīkāstraṃ samādhaya brahmāstreṇābhimantritam ।। sa tv indrasya suto rājann indralokaṃ viveśa ha ।। viditārthaś ca devendro devaiḥ saha samanvitaḥ ।। tato asau sarvadevais tu devalokād bahiḥ kṛtaḥ ।।
pāhi rāma mahābāho ajñānād apakāriṇam ।। amoghaṃ ca mamaivāstram aṅgam ekaṃ prayaccha vai ।। ityukto asau svakaṃ netram ekam astrāya dattavān ।। tataḥ prabhṛti kākānāṃ sarveṣām ekanetratā ।।
uṣitvā tatra suciraṃ citrakūṭe sa rāghavaḥ ।। sabhrātṛkaḥ sabhāryaś ca tāpasaṃ veṣam āsthitaḥ ।। tato dadarśa tatrasthān ambubhakṣān mahāmunīn ।। pañcāgnimadhyagān anyān anyān ugratapaś carān ।।
tato akhilaṃ vanaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmaḥ sākṣāj janārdanaḥ ।। darśayitvā tu sītāyai vanaṃ kusumitaṃ śubham ।। kṛṣṇāṅgaṃ raktanetraṃ tu sthūlaśailasamānakam ।। meghasvanaṃ sāparādhaṃ śaraṃ saṃdhāya rāghavaḥ ।।
anyair avadhyaṃ hatvā taṃ girigarte mahātanum ।। taṃ natvā tatra viśramya tatkathātuṣṭamānasaḥ ।। tenādiṣṭena mārgeṇa gatvāgastyaṃ dadarśa ha ।। iṣudhi cākṣayaśaraṃ cāpaṃ caiva tu vaiṣṇavam ।।
godāvaryāḥ samīpe tu pañcavaṭyām uvāsa saḥ ।। natvā svakulam ākhyāya sthitavān gṛdhranāyakaḥ ।। kathayitvā tu taṃ prāha sītāṃ rakṣa mahāmate ।। kāryārthaṃ tu gate rāme bhrātrā saha vanāntaram ।।
ity uktvā gatavān rāmaṃ gṛdhrarājaḥ svam āśramam ।। vasantaṃ rāghavaṃ tatra sītayā saha sundaram ।। kṛtvā māyāmayaṃ rūpaṃ lāvaṇyaguṇasaṃyutam ।। gāyantī susvaraṃ gītaṃ śanair āgatya rākṣasī ।।
atha śūrpaṇakhā ghorā māyārūpadharā śubhā ।। bhaja māṃ kānta kalyāṇīṃ bhajantīṃ kāminīm iha ।। ityuktaḥ śūrpaṇakhayā rāmas tām āha pārthivaḥ ।। iti śrutvā tataḥ prāha rākṣasī kāmarūpiṇī ।।
tyaktvainām anabhijñāṃ tvaṃ sītāṃ māṃ bhaja śobhanam ।। parastriyaṃ na gacche ahaṃ tvam ito gaccha lakṣmaṇam ।। ityuktā sā punaḥ prāha rāmaṃ rājīvalocanam ।। tathaivam uktvā matimān rāmaḥ kamalalocanaḥ ।।
iti rāmo mahārājo likhya patraṃ pradattavān ।। gatvā dattavatī tadval lakṣmaṇāya mahātmane ।। na laṅghyaṃ raghavavaco mayā tiṣṭhātmakaśmale ।। tena tatkarṇanāsāṃ tu viccheda tilakāṇḍavat ।।
hā daśāsya mama bhrātaḥ sarvadevavimardaka ।। hā hā kaṣṭaṃ guṇanidhe vibhīṣaṇa mahāmate ।। triśirasaṃ ca sā dṛṣṭvā nivedyātmaparābhavam ।। jñātvā te rāghavaṃ kruddhāḥ preṣayāmasur ūrjitān ।।
agre nijagmus tenaiva rakṣasāṃ nāyakās trayaḥ ।। mahābalaparīvārā janasthānam upāgatāḥ ।। rudatīm aśrudigdhāṅgīṃ bhaginīṃ rāvaṇasya tu ।। saṃsthāpya lakṣmaṇaṃ tatra sītāyā rakṣaṇaṃ prati ।।
caturdaśasahasraṃ tu rākṣasānāṃ mahābalam ।। kharaś ca nihatas tena dūṣaṇaś ca mahābalaḥ ।। hatvā tān rākṣasān duṣṭān rāmaś cāśramam āviśat ।। chinnanāsāṃ ca tāṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇo bhaginīṃ tadā ।।
puṣpakeṇa vimānena gatvāhaṃ tvaṃ ca mātula ।। sauvarṇamṛgarūpaṃ tvam āsthāya tu śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā sā mṛgapotaṃ tvāṃ sauvarṇaṃ tvayi mātula ।। tadvākyāt tatra gachantaṃ dhāvasva gahane vane ।।
tataḥ puṣpakam āruhya māyārūpeṇa cāpy aham ।। tvam api svecchayā paścād āgamiṣyasi śobhana ।। tvam eva gaccha pāpiṣṭha nāhaṃ gacchāmi tatra vai ।। ityuktavati mārīce rāvaṇaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ ।।
tava hastavadhād vīra rāmeṇa maraṇaṃ varam ।। atha puṣpakam āruhya janasthānam upāgataḥ ।। jagāma yatra sā sītā vartate janakātmajā ।। bhāvikarmavaśād rāmam uvāca patim ātmanaḥ ।।
ayodhāyāṃ tu madgehe krīḍanārtham idaṃ mama ।। rakṣaṇārthaṃ tu sītāyā gato asau mṛgapṛṣṭhatah ।। tataḥ sareṇa vivyādha rāmas taṃ mṛgapotakam ।। mārīcaḥ parvatākāras tena naṣṭo babhūva saḥ ।।
gaccha lakṣmaṇa putra tvaṃ yatrāyaṃ śabda utthitaḥ ।। prāyo rāmasya saṃdehaṃ lakṣaye aham mahātmanaḥ ।। na hi rāmasya saṃdeho na bhayaṃ vidyate kvacit ।। lakṣmaṇaṃ prāha vaidehī viruddhavacanaṃ tadā ।।
ityuktaḥ sa vinītātmā asahann apriyaṃ vacaḥ ।। saṃnyāsaveṣam āsthāya rāvaṇo api durātmavān ।। āgato bharataḥ śrīmān ayodhyāyā mahāmatiḥ ।। māṃ ca preṣitavān rāmo vimānam idam āruha ।।
mṛgabālaṃ tu vaidehi krīḍārthaṃ te gṛhītavān ।। saṃprāptarājyas te bhartā rāmaḥ sa rucirānanaḥ ।। ityuktā sā tathā gatvā nītā tena mahātmanā ।। taj jagāma tataḥ śīghraṃ vimānaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ diśam ।।
vimāne khe api rodantyāś cakre sparśaṃ na rākṣasaḥ ।। daśagrīvaṃ mahākāyaṃ dṛṣṭvā sītā suduḥkhitā ।। rakṣasā ghorarūpeṇa trāyasveti bhayārditā ।। drutam āgatya rakṣasva nīyamānām athākulām ।।
ākarṇya gṛdhrarājas tu jaṭāyus tatra cāgataḥ ।। ity uktvā yuyudhe tena jaṭāyus tatra vīryavān ।। tāḍayantaṃ tu taṃ matvā balavān iti rāvaṇaḥ ।। tata utthāpya vegena candrahāsam asiṃ mahat ।।
nipapāta mahīpṛṣṭhe jaṭāyuḥ kṣīṇacetanaḥ ।। candrahāsasya vīryeṇa hato ahaṃ rākṣasādhama ।। sītāpaharaṇaṃ viddhi mṛtyus te duṣṭa rākṣasa ।। rudatī duḥkhaśokārtā jaṭāyuṃ prāha maithilī ।।
tasmād rāmaprasādena viṣṇulokam avāpsyasi ।। tāvat tiṣṭhantu te prāṇā ity uktvā tu khagottamam ।। śīghraṃ nibadhya vastreṇa rāmahastaṃ gamiṣyatha ।। evaṃ hṛtvā sa sītāṃ tu jaṭāyuṃ pātya bhūtale ।।
aśokavanikāmadhye sthāpayitvā sa maithilīm ।। ity ādiśya gṛhaṃ yāto rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ ।। asyāḥ puryā vināśārthaṃ sthāpiteyaṃ durātmanā ।। sītā ca duḥkhitā tatra smarantī rāmam eva sā ।।
yathā jñānakhale devī haṃsayānā sarasvatī ।। vastrabaddhaṃ tayotsṛṣṭaṃ gṛhītvā bhūṣaṇaṃ drutam ।। araṇye abhūn mahāyuddhaṃ jaṭāyo rāvaṇasya ca ।। nivṛtto lakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā tena gatvā svam āśramam ।।
lakṣmaṇaś ca mahātejā ruroda bhṛśaduḥkhitaḥ ।। bhūtale patitaṃ dhīmān utthāpyāśvāsya lakṣmaṇaḥ ।। ativelaṃ mahārāja na śokaṃ kartum arhasi ।। ity evaṃ vadatā tena lakṣmaṇena mahātmanā ।।
bhrātrā saha jagāmātha sītāṃ mṛgayituṃ vanam ।। tathā munīnām api cāśramān bahūṃs tṛṇādivallīgahaneṣu bhūmiṣu ।। priyām apaśyan bhṛśaduḥkhitas tadā jaṭāyuṣaṃ vīkṣya ca ghātitaṃ nṛpaḥ ।। mamādya sarvaṃ samaduḥkhitasya bhoḥ patnīviyogād iha cāgatasya vai ।।
śṛṇuṣva rājan mama vṛttam atra vadāmi dṛṣṭaṃ ca kṛtaṃ ca sadyaḥ ।। jagāma khe dakṣiṇadiṅmukho asau sītā ca mātā vilalāpa duḥkhitā ।। yuddhaṃ ca tenāham atīva kṛtvā hataḥ punaḥ khaḍgabalena rakṣasā ।। mā rāma śokaṃ kuru bhūmipāla jahy adya duṣṭaṃ sagaṇaṃ tu nairṛtam ।।
svasty astu te dvijavara gatis tu paramāstu te ।। vimānena tu ramyeṇa sevyamāno apsarogaṇaiḥ ।। bhrātrā sa gacchan duḥkhārto rākṣasīṃ pathi dṛṣṭavān ।। kṣayaṃ nayantīṃ jantūn vai pātayitvā gato ruṣā ।।
virūpaṃ jaṭharamukhaṃ dīrghabāhuṃ ghanastanam ।। dagdho asau divyarūpī tu khastho rāmam abhāṣata ।। virūpaṃ nāśitaṃ vira muniśāpāc cirāgatam ।। tvaṃ sītāprāptaye sakhyaṃ kuru sūryasutena bhoḥ ।।
bhaviṣyati nṛpaśreṣṭha ṛṣyamūkagiriṃ vraja ।। siddhais tu munibhiḥ śūnyam āśramaṃ praviveśa ha ।। śabarīṃ munimukhyānāṃ sa paryāhatakalmaṣām ।। sāpy enaṃ pūjayitvā tu svām avasthāṃ nivedya vai ।।
divaṃ prasthāpya tāṃ cāpi jagāmānyatra rāghavaḥ ।। priyāviyogena suduḥkhitātmā jagāma yāmyāṃ sa tu rāmadevaḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe rāmaprādurbhāve ekonapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। sugrīvo dṛṣṭavān dūrād dṛṣṭvāha pavanātmajam ।।
paśyantau sarasīṃ divyāṃ padmotpalasamāvṛtām ।। vālidūtāv iha prāptāv iti niścitya sūryajaḥ ।। vānaraiḥ sahitaḥ sarvair agastyāśramam uttamam ।। hanūman pṛccha śīghraṃ tvaṃ gaccha tāpasaveṣadhṛk ।।
jñātvā satyaṃ mama brūhi vāyuputra mahāmate ।। bikṣurūpī sa taṃ prāha rāmaṃ bhrātrā samanvitam ।। araṇye nirjane ghore kutas tvaṃ kiṃ prayojanam ।। pravakṣyāmi nibodha tvaṃ rāmavṛttāntam āditaḥ ।।
tasya putro mahābuddhe rāmo jyeṣṭho mamāgrajaḥ ।। pitur ājñām ayaṃ kurvan rāmo bhrātā mamāgrajaḥ ।। praviṣṭo daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ nānāmunisamākulam ।। bhāryā sītā tatra vane kenāpi pāpmanā hṛtā ।।
ihāyātas tvayā dṛṣṭa iti vṛttāntam īritam ।। avyañjitātmā viśvāsād dhanūmān mārutātmajaḥ ।। āśvāsyānīya sugrīvaṃ tayoḥ sakhyam akārayat ।। sugrīvo vānarendras tu uvāca madhurākṣaram ।।
ahaṃ tu tava bhṛtyaś ca vānaraiḥ sahitaḥ prabho ।। mitraṃ te mama sanmitraṃ tvadduḥkhaṃ tan mamāpi ca ।। vālī nāma mama jyeṣṭho mahābalaparākramaḥ ।। tvām ṛte puruṣavyāghra nāsti hantādya vālinam ।।
sa taṃ vadhiṣyatīty uktaṃ purāṇajñair nṛpātmaja ।। ardhākṛṣṭena bāṇena yugapad raghunandanaḥ ।। vālinā gaccha yudhyasva kṛtacihno raveḥ suta ।। rāmo api tatra gatvātha śareṇaikena vālinam ।।
vitrastaṃ vāliputraṃ tu aṅgadaṃ vinayānvitam ।। tāṃ ca tārāṃ tathā dattvā rāmaś ca ravisūnave ।। rājyam anveṣaya svaṃ tvaṃ kapīnāṃ punar āvraja ।। ityuktaḥ prāha sugrīvo rāmaṃ lakṣmaṇasaṃyutam ।।
vānarāṇāṃ gatir nāsti vane varṣati vāsave ।। cārān saṃpreṣayiṣyāmi vānarān dikṣu rāghava ।। pampāpuraṃ praviśyātha reme tārāsamanvitaḥ ।। nivāsaṃ kṛtavān śaile nīlakaṇṭhe mahāmatiḥ ।।
sītāviyogād vyathitaḥ saumitriṃ prāha lakṣmaṇam ।। lakṣmaṇaṃ prāha kākutstho bhrātaraṃ bhrātṛvatsalaḥ ।। gate tu varṣākāle ahaṃ āgamiṣyāmi te antikam ।। tatra gaccha tvarāyukto yatrāste kapināyakaḥ ।।
ramantaṃ tārayā sārdhaṃ śīghram ānaya māṃ prati ।। tadā tvayaivaṃ vaktavyaḥ sugrīvo anṛtabhāṣakaḥ ।। smṛtvaitad ācara kape rāmavākyaṃ hitaṃ tava ।। dṛṣṭvā sa tatra sugrīvaṃ kapirājaṃ babhāṣa vai ।।
kiṃ tvayā vismṛtaṃ sarvaṃ rāmāgre samayaṃ kṛtam ।। hatvā tu vālinaṃ rājyaṃ yena dattaṃ purā tava ।। pratiśrutya ca rāmasya bhāryāhīnasya bhūpate ।। ye ye ca śatravo rājaṃs te te ca mama śatravaḥ ।।
sītām anveṣituṃ rājan vānarair bahubhir vṛtaḥ ।। tvām ṛte pāpinaṃ duṣṭaṃ rāmadevasya saṃnidhau ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ satyavad vākyaṃ tvayi dṛṣṭaṃ mayādhunā ।। vatsaḥ kṣīrakṣayaṃ dṛṣṭvā parityajati mātaram ।।
na taṃ paśyāmi loke asmin kṛtaṃ pratikaroti yaḥ ।। kṛtaghnasya kape duṣṭa na dṛṣṭā niṣkṛtiḥ purā ।। ehy ehy āgaccha śaraṇaṃ kakutsthaṃ hitapālakam ।। nayiṣe mṛtyusadanaṃ sugrīvaṃ vālinaṃ yathā ।।
lakṣmaṇenaivam ukto asau sugrīvaḥ kapināyakaḥ ।। uvāca ca mahātmānaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ vānarādhipaḥ ।। samayaḥ kṛto mayā rājñā rāmeṇāmitatejasā ।। yāsyāmi nikhilair adya kapibhir nṛpanandana ।।
māṃ dṛṣṭvā tatra kākutstho yad vakṣyati ca māṃ prati ।। santi me harayaḥ śūrāḥ sītānveṣaṇakarmaṇi ।। ityuktaḥ kapirājena sugrīveṇa sa lakṣmaṇaḥ ।। senā cāhūyatāṃ vīra ṛkṣāṇāṃ hariṇām api ।।
ityukto lakṣmaṇenātha sugrīvaḥ sa tu vīryavān ।। so api nirgatya senānīm āha senāpatiṃ tadā ।। guhāsthāś ca giristhāś ca vṛkṣasthāś caiva vānarāḥ ।। sugrīvaḥ śīghram āgatya vavande rāghavaṃ tadā ।।
prasādaṃ kuru sugrīve vinīte cādhunā nṛpa ।। āgacchātra mahāvīra sugrīva kuśalaṃ tava ।। śirasy añjalim ādhāya sugrīvo rāmam abravīt ।। anviṣya tu yadā dattā mayā bhavati nānyathā ।।
natvā rāmaṃ babhāṣainaṃ sugrīvaṃ kapināyakam ।। sītāviyogena ca sadā nāśnāti ca phalādikam ।। etayor atra yāvasthā tāṃ śrutvā bharato anujaḥ ।। yata evam ato rājan sītānveṣanam ācara ।।
jāmbavān atitejasvī natvā rāmaṃ puraḥsthitaḥ ।। yad uktaṃ vāyuputreṇa tat tathety avagaccha bhoḥ ।। pativratā mahābhāgā vaidehī janakātmajā ।। na hi kalyāṇacittāyāḥ sītāyāḥ kenacid bhuvi ।।
ityuktas tena sugrīvaḥ prītātmā kapināyakaḥ ।। anveṣṭuṃ rāmabhāryāṃ tāṃ mahābalaparākramaḥ ।। preṣayāmasa dharmātmā sītānveṣaṇakarmaṇi ।। preṣayāmasa rāmasya subhārānveṣaṇāya vai ।।
sugrīvo vāliputraṃ tam aṅgadaṃ prāha buddhimān ।। jāmbavāṃś ca hanūmāṃś ca maindo dvivida eva ca ।। anuyāsyanti gacchantaṃ tvām adya mama śāsanāt ।। sthānato rūpataś caiva śīlataś ca viśeṣataḥ ।।
ityuktaḥ kapirājena pitṛvyeṇa mahātmanā ।। ityukte dūrataḥ sthāpya vānarān atha jāmbavān ।। ekataḥ sthāpya tān āha nītimān nītimad vacaḥ ।। śrutvā ca tad gṛhāṇa tvaṃ rocate yan nṛpātmaja ।।
jaṭāyuṣā tu sā dṛṣṭvā śaktyā yuddhaṃ prakurvatā ।। tāny asmābhiḥ pradṛṣṭāni sugrīvāyārpitāni ca ।। etasmāt kāraṇāt sītā nītā tenaiva rakṣasā ।। tvāṃ smarantī tu tatrasthā tvadduḥkhena suduḥkhitā ।।
tvaddhyānenaiva svān prāṇān dhārayantī śubhānanā ।। hitam eva ca te rājann udadher laṅghane kṣamam ।। tvaṃ cāpy arhasi sugrīva preṣituṃ mārutātmajam ।। balaṃ kasyāpi vā vīra iti me manasi sthitam ।।
ukte jāmbavataivaṃ tu nītisvalpākṣarānvite ।। vāyuputrasamīpaṃ tu taṃ gatvā vākyam abravīt ।। ayam ikṣvākutilako rājā rāmaḥ pratāpavān ।। praviṣṭo daṇḍakāraṇyaṃ sākṣād dharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।।
asya bhāryā hṛtā tena duṣṭenāpi durātmanā ।। tvayā dṛṣṭo nṛpaḥ pūrvam ayaṃ vīraḥ pratāpavān ।। anena nihataḥ śatrur mama vālir mahābalaḥ ।। mayā ca tat partijñātam asya sāhāyyakarmaṇi ।।
uttīrya sāgaraṃ vīra dṛṣṭvā sītām aninditām ।। atas tvam eva jānāsi svāmikāryaṃ mahāmate ।। tenaivam ukto hanumān sugrīveṇa mahātmanā ।। ityukto vāyuputreṇa rāmas taṃ purataḥ sthitam ।।
sītāṃ smṛtvā suduḥkhārtaḥ kālayuktam amitrajit ।। sugrīvaḥ sthāpyate hy atra mayā sārdhaṃ mahāmate ।। jñātīnāṃ ca tathā prītyai sugrīvasya viśeṣataḥ ।। tatra gaccha mahāvīra yatra sītā vyavasthitā ।।
ato nirīkṣya māṃ bhūyo lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mamānujam ।। nānyathā viśvaset sītā iti me manasi sthitam ।। utthāya tatpuraḥ sthitvā kṛtāñjalir uvāca tam ।। gacchāmi kapibhiḥ sārdhaṃ tvaṃ śokaṃ mā kuruṣva vai ।।
sītāyās tava devyās tu rājan rājīvalocana ।। aṅgulīyakam unmucya dattavān rāmacihnitam ।। rāmaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya lakṣmaṇaṃ ca kapīśvaram ।। sugrīvo api ca tāñ chrutvā vānarān gantum udyatān ।।
śṛṇvantu vānarāḥ sarve śāsanaṃ mama bhāṣitam ।। drutaṃ gatvā tu tāṃ vīkṣya āgantavyam aninditām ।। kartanaṃ vā kariṣyāmi anyathā kaṛnanāsayoḥ ।। atha te vānarā yātāḥ paścimādiṣu dikṣu vai ।।
nadītīreṣu sarveṣu munīnām āśrameṣu ca ।। vṛkṣeṣu vṛkṣagulmeṣu guhāsu ca śilāsu ca ।। himavaty api śaile ca tathā kiṃpuruṣādiṣu ।। madhyadeśeṣu sarveṣu kaśmīreṣu mahābalāḥ ।।
tīrthasthāneṣu sarveṣu saptakoṅkaṇakeṣu ca ।। āgatya te namaskṛtya rāmalakṣmaṇapādayoḥ ।। dṛṣṭā sītā mahābhāgety uktvā tāṃs tatra tasthire ।। sītā dakṣiṇadigbhāge sthitā draṣṭuṃ vane nṛpa ।।
dṛṣṭvā sītām ihāyāti hanūmān nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। lakṣmaṇo apy āha śakunaṃ tatra vākyam idaṃ tadā ।। ity āśvāsya sthitau tatra rāmaṃ sugrīvalakṣmaṇau ।। yatnād anveṣanārthāya rāmapatnīṃ yaśasvinīm ।।
bhakṣaṇena vihīnās te kṣudhayā ca prapīḍitāḥ ।। guhānivāsinī siddhā ṛsipatnī hy aninditā ।। āgatāḥ kasya yūyaṃ tu kutaḥ kiṃ nu prayojanam ।। sugrīvasya vayaṃ bhṛtyā āgatā hy atra śobhane ।।
kāṃdigbhūtā nirāhārā adṛṣṭvā janakātmajām ।। jānāmi rāmaṃ sītāṃ ca lakṣmaṇaṃ ca kapīśvaram ।। rāmakāryāgatās tv atra yūyaṃ rāmasamā mama ।। bhojayitvā yathākāmaṃ bhūyas tān āha tāpasī ।।
āsthito vai vane so api mahendre parvate dvijaḥ ।। sa vakti sītāṃ saṃpātir dūradarśī tu yaḥ khagaḥ ।। avaśyaṃ jānakīṃ sītāṃ drakṣyate pavanātmajaḥ ।। hṛṣṭās tejanam āpannās tāṃ praṇamya pratasthire ।।
tatra sampātim āsīnaṃ dṛṣṭavantaḥ kapīśvarāḥ ।। ke yūyam iti saṃprāptāḥ kasya vā brūta mā ciram ।। rāmadūtā vayaṃ sarve sītānveṣaṇakarmaṇi ।। tvāṃ draṣṭum iha saṃprāptāḥ siddhāyā vacanād dvija ।।
ityukto vānaraiḥ śyeno vīkṣāṃ cakre sudakṣiṇām ।। sthiteti kathitaṃ tena jaṭāyus tu mṛtas tava ।। yogam āsthāya svaṃ dehaṃ visasarja mahāmatiḥ ।। gatvā mahendraśṛṅgaṃ te tam āruhya kṣaṇaṃ sthitāḥ ।।
rāvaṇenaiva bhāryā sā nītā rāmasya niścitam ।। vānarāṇāṃ tu kaś cātra uttīrya lavaṇodadhim ।। punas codadhitaraṇe śaktiṃ brūta hi śobhanāḥ ।। sāgarottaraṇe kiṃtu kāryam anyasya saṃbhavet ।।
kālakṣepo na kartavyo māsārdham adhikaṃ gatam ।। karṇanāsādi naḥ svāṅgaṃ nikṛntati kapīśvaraḥ ।। ityuktās te tathety ūcur vānarā vṛddhavānaram ।। hanūmantaṃ mahāprājñaṃ dakṣaṃ kāryeṣu cādhikam ।।
ityuktas tāṃs tathety āha vānarān pavanātmajaḥ ।। gantuṃ pracakre matim añjanīsutaḥ samudram uttīrya niśācarālayam ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe rāmaprādurbhāve pañcāśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। iyeṣa padam anveṣṭuṃ cāraṇācarite pathi ।।
manasāvandya rāmaṃ ca lakṣmaṇaṃ ca mahāratham ।। jñātīṃś caiva pariṣvajya kṛtvā caiva pradakṣiṇām ।। punarāgamanāyeti vānarair abhipūjitaḥ ।। mārgam ālokayan dūrād ūrdhvaṃ praṇihitekṣaṇaḥ ।।
utpapāta gireḥ śṛṅgān niṣpīḍya girim ambaram ।। rāmakāryaparasyāsya sāgareṇa pracoditah ।। taṃ nirīkṣya nipīḍyātha rayāt saṃbhāṣya sādaram ।। āsyaprāntaṃ praviśyātha vegenāntarviniḥsṛtaḥ ।।
laṅghayitvā tu taṃ deśaṃ sāgaraṃ pavanātmajaḥ ।। tasmin sa parvataśreṣṭhe dinaṃ nītvā dinakṣaye ।। laṅkābhidhāṃ vinirjitya devatāṃ praviveśa ha ।। rākṣaseṣu prasupteṣu nītimān pavanātmajaḥ ।।
śayānaṃ rāvaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā talpe mahati vānaraḥ ।। tathaiva daśabhir vaktrair daṃṣṭropetais tu saṃyutam ।। tasmin sītām adṛṣṭvā tu rāvaṇasya gṛhe śubhe ।। duḥkhito vāyuputras tu saṃpāter vacanaṃ smaran ।।
juṣṭāṃ malayajātena candanena sugandhinā ।। rāmapatnīṃ samadrākṣīd rākṣasībhir surakṣitām ।। āsāṃ cakre haris tatra seyaṃ sīteti saṃsmaran ।। strībhiḥ parivṛtas tatra rāvaṇas tāvad āgataḥ ।।
bhuṣitā bhava vaidehi tyaja rāmāgataṃ manaḥ ।। prāha vākyaṃ śanaiḥ sītā kampamānātha rāvaṇam ।। acirād rāmabāṇās te pibantu rudhiraṃ raṇe ।। dvimāsābhyantare cainaṃ vaśīkuruta mānuṣīm ।।
ity uktvā gatavān duṣṭo rāvaṇaḥ svaṃ niketanam ।। rāvaṇaṃ bhaja kalyāṇi sadhanaṃ sukhinī bhava ।। nihatya rāvaṇaṃ yuddhe sagaṇaṃ māṃ nayiṣyati ।। sa hy āgatya daśagrīvaṃ hatvā māṃ pālayiṣyati ।।
hanyatāṃ hanyatām eṣā bhakṣyatāṃ bhakṣyatām iyam ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ duṣṭarākṣasyo rāvaṇasya vināśanaḥ ।। lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā rāmasya vijayapradaḥ ।। trijatāvākyam ākarṇya sītāpārśvaṃ visṛjya tāḥ ।।
kīrtayan rāmavṛttāntaṃ sakalaṃ pavanātmajaḥ ।। saṃbhāṣya lakṣaṇaṃ sarvaṃ rāmalakṣmaṇayos tataḥ ।। tena sārdham ihāgatya rāmas tava patiḥ prabhuḥ ।। rāvaṇaṃ sagaṇaṃ hatvā tvām ito adāya gacchati ।।
katham atrāgato vīra tvam uttīrya mahodadhim ।। goṣpadavan mayottīrṇaḥ samudro ayaṃ varānane ।। duḥkhamagnāsi vaidehi sthirā bhava śubhānane ।। ity āśvāsya satīṃ sītāṃ duḥkhitāṃ janakātmajām ।।
natvā tāṃ prasthito vīro gantuṃ kṛtamatiḥ kapiḥ ।। toraṇastho nanādoccai rāmo jayati vīryavān ।। tadā tvakṣakumāraṃ tu hatvā rāvaṇasainikam ।। rāvaṇasya puraḥ sthitvā rāmaṃ saṃkīrtya lakṣmaṇam ।।
nirbhartsya rāvaṇaṃ duṣṭaṃ punaḥ saṃbhāṣya jānakīm ।। sītādarśanam āvedya hanūmāṃś caiva pūjitaḥ ।। nihatya rakṣapālāṃs tu pāyayitvā ca tanmadhu ।। kham utpatya ca saṃprāpya rāmalakṣmaṇapādayoḥ ।।
āditaḥ sarvam āvedya samudrataraṇādikam ।। aśokavanikāmadhye sītā devī suduḥkhitā ।। aśrupūrṇamukhī dīnā tava patnī varānanā ।। sarvatrānveṣamāṇena mayā dṛṣṭā pativratā ।।
alaṃkāraś ca sumaṇis tayā te preṣitaḥ prabho ।। idaṃ ca vacanaṃ tubhyaṃ patnyā saṃpreṣitaṃ śṛṇu ।। vāyasābhibhavaṃ rājaṃs tat kila smartum arhasi ।। yat kṛtaṃ tan na kartuṃ ca śakyaṃ devāsurair api ।।
evaṃ tu duḥkhitā sītā tāṃ moktuṃ yatnam ācara ।। śrutvā ca dṛṣṭvā ca ruroda rāmaḥ kapiṃ samāliṅgya śanaiḥ pratasthe ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe rāmaprādurbhāve ekapañcāso adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। rāmo gatvā samudrāntaṃ vānaraiḥ saha vistṛtaiḥ ।।
sugrīvo jāmbavāṃś cātha vānarair atiharṣitaiḥ ।। anujena ca dhīreṇa vīkṣya tasthau saritpatim ।। vibhīṣaṇo mahābuddhiḥ śāstrajñair mantribhiḥ saha ।। evaṃ rāme acalāṃ bhaktim āgatya vinayāt tadā ।।
rāma rāma mahābāho devadeva janārdana ।। ity uktvā nipapātātha prāñjalī rāmapādayoḥ ।। samudratoyais taṃ vīram abhiṣicya vibhīṣaṇam ।। tato vibhīṣaṇenoktaṃ tvaṃ viṣṇur bhuvaneśvaraḥ ।।
ityukto vānaraiḥ sārdhaṃ śiśye tatra sa rāghavaḥ ।। tataḥ kruddho jagannātho rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ ।। tadotthāya vacaḥ prāhaḥ lakṣmaṇaś ca ruṣānvitam ।। bhūtānāṃ rakṣaṇārthāya avatāras tvayā kṛtaḥ ।।
tato rātritraye yāte kruddhaṃ rāmam avekṣya saḥ ।। āha rāmaṃ mahādevaṃ rakṣa mām apakāriṇam ।। nalas ca kathito vīras tena kāraya rāghava ।। tato nalamukhair anyair vānarair amitaujasaiḥ ।।
suvelākhyaṃ giriṃ prāptaḥ sthito asau vānarair vṛtaḥ ।। rāmādeśād athotplutya dūtakarmasu tatparaḥ ।। vismitaṃ taiḥ suragaṇair vīkṣitaḥ so ativīryavān ।। tato vānarasenābhiḥ saṃkhyātītābhir acyutaḥ ।।
rāmaḥ samantād ālokya prāha lakṣmaṇam antike ।। yat pauruṣocitam ihāṅkuritaṃ mayā tad daivasya vaśyam aparaṃ dhanuṣo atha vāsya ।। lakṣmaṇaḥ prāha kātarajanamanovalambinā kiṃ daivena । tāvan niśācarapateḥ paṭim ānametu trailokyamūlavibhujeṣu bhujeṣu darpaḥ ।।
tadā lakṣmaṇaḥ rāmasya karṇe lagitvā pitṛvadhavairasmaraṇe atha tadbaktivīryaparīkṣaṇāya lakṣaṇavijñānāyādiśyatām aṅgadāya dūtyam । rāmaḥ sādhu iti bhaṇitvā aṅgadaṃ sabahumānam avalokya ādiśati ।। aṅgada । sa eva tvaṃ vyāvartayasi tanujatvena pitṛtāṃ tataḥ kiṃ vaktavyaṃ tilakayati sṛṣṭārthapadavīm ।। aṅgado maulimaṇḍalamilatkarayugalena praṇamya yad ājñāpayati devaḥ । avadhāryatām ।।
atyalpaṃ kulaparvatair aviralair badhnāmi vā sāgaraṃ devādeśaya kiṃ karomi sakalaṃ dordaṇḍasādhyaṃ mama ।। śrīrāmas tadvacanamātreṇaiva tadbhaktiṃ sāmarthyaṃ cāvekṣya vadati ।। no cel lakṣmaṇamuktamārgaṇagaṇacchedocchalacchoṇitac chatracchannadigantam antakapurīṃ putrair vṛto yāsyasi ।। aṅgadaḥ ।।
deva । akṣatā vā kṣatā vāpi kṣitipīṭhe luṭhiṣyati ।। uktipratyukticāturyaiḥ parājityāgato ripum ।। vānarāṇāṃ ca bhīto api nirbhīr iva daśānanaḥ ।।
ādiśya sarvato dikṣu putrān āha daśānanaḥ ।। kumbhakarṇo api madbhrātā turyanādaiḥ prabodhitaḥ ।। tasyājñāṃ śirasādāya yuyudhur vānaraiḥ saha ।। vānarair nidhanaṃ prāptāḥ punar anyān yathādiśat ।।
te cāpi yudhya haribhir nīlādyair nidhanaṃ gatāḥ ।। te sarve vānaravarair dāritās tu yamaṃ gatāḥ ।। rākṣasāḥ parvatākārāḥ prāpitā yamasādanam ।। petus te rākṣasāḥ krūrā maindādyair vānarair hatāḥ ।।
utplutyābhyantarasthāṃś ca rākṣasān baladarpitān ।। evaṃ hateṣu sarveṣu rākṣaseṣu daśānanaḥ ।। dvāre sa paścime vīro rākṣasair bahubhir vṛtaḥ ।। rathasthaḥ śaravarṣaṃ ca visṛjan vānareṣu saḥ ।।
palāyamānāṃs tān dṛṣṭvā vānarān rāghavas tadā ।। iti rāmavacaḥ śrutvā prāha vākyaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ ।। tadbāṇachinnā harayaḥ palāyante mahāmate ।। jyāghoṣatalaghoṣābhyāṃ pūrayāmasa khaṃ diśaḥ ।।
sugrīvo jāmbavāṃś caiva hanumān aṅgadas tathā ।। upetya rāvaṇīṃ senāṃ varṣantīṃ sarvasāyakān ।। rāmarāvaṇayor yuddham abhūt tatrāpi bhīṣaṇam ।। tāni chittvātha śastrais tu rāghavaś ca mahābalaḥ ।।
rāvaṇasya dhanus chittvā bhallenaikena rāghavaḥ ।। suvarṇapuṅkhair daśabhiḥ śarair vivyādha vīryavān ।। viveśa mantribhir nītaḥ svapurīṃ devamardakaḥ ।। punaḥ prākāram ullaṅghya kumbhakarṇo vinirgataḥ ।।
vānarān bhakṣayan duṣṭo vicacāra kṣudhānvitaḥ ।। karṇadvayaṃ karābhyāṃ tu cchittvā vakreṇa nāsikām ।। rāghavo ghātayitvā tu vānarendraiḥ samantataḥ ।। vijityendrajitaṃ sākṣād garuḍenāgatena saḥ ।।
vyarthaṃ gate cendrajiti kumbhakarṇe nipātite ।। atikāyamahākāyau devāntakanarāntakau ।। tān niyujya daśagrīvaḥ putrān evaṃ punar bravīt ।। saṃgrāme asmin ripūn hantuṃ yuvāṃ vrajatam udyatau ।।
anayal lakṣmaṇaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ śarais tīkṣṇair yamālayam ।। sugrīveṇa hataḥ kumbho rākṣaso baladarpitaḥ ।। virūpākṣaṃ yudhyamānāṃ gadayā tu vibhīṣaṇaḥ ।। aṅgado jāmbavāṃś cātha harayo anyān niśācarān ।।
jaghāna rāmo atha raṇe bāṇavṛṣṭikaraṃ nṛpa ।। vānareṣu ca sareṣu śaravarṣaṃ vavarṣa saḥ ।। niśceṣṭam akhilaṃ dṛṣṭvā jāmbavat preritas tadā ।। bhūmyāṃ śayānam utthāpya rāmaṃ harigaṇāṃs tathā ।।
dāhayāmasa laṅkāṃ tāṃ hastyaśvaratharakṣasām ।। sa bhrātrā meghanādaṃ taṃ ghātayāmasa rāghavaḥ ।। kāriteṣv atha vighneṣu homajapyādikarmaṇām ।। kvāsau rāma iti brūte mānuṣas tāpasākṛtiḥ ।।
vegavadbhir vinītaiś ca aśvaiś citrarathe sthitaḥ ।। rāmo aham atra duṣṭātmann ehi rāvaṇa māṃ prati ।। anena rākṣasā yotsye tvaṃ tiṣṭheti mahābalaḥ ।। viṃśadbāhuvisṛṣṭais tu śastrāstrair lakṣmaṇaṃ yudhi ।।
devā vyomni vimānasthā vīkṣya tasthur mahāhavam ।। lakṣmaṇaḥ sārathiṃ hatvā tasyāśvān api bhallakaiḥ ।। vakṣaḥsthalaṃ mahāvīryo vivyādha paravīrahā ।। śaktiṃ jagrāha kupito ghaṇṭānādavinādinīm ।।
dṛḍhamuṣṭyā tu nikṣiptā śaktiḥ sā lakṣmaṇorasi ।। lakṣmaṇaṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā rudadbhir vānareśvaraiḥ ।। kva gato hanumān vīro mitro me pavanātmajaḥ ।। ityukte hanumān rājan vīro vikhyātapauruṣaḥ ।।
rāmaḥ prāha mahāvīra viśalyakaraṇī mama ।। tato vegāt samutpatya gatvā droṇagiriṃ kapiḥ ।। cakāra devadeveśāṃ paśyatāṃ rāghavasya ca ।। rāvaṇasya balaṃ śiṣṭaṃ hastyaśvaratharākṣasam ।।
tīkṣṇair jarjaritaṃ kṛtvā tasthivān vānarair vṛtaḥ ।। utthāya rāvaṇaḥ kruddhaḥ siṃhanādaṃ nanāda ca ।। etasminn eva kale tu rāmaṃ prāpya mahāmuniḥ ।। ādityahṛdayaṃ nāma mantraṃ prādāj jayapradam ।।
taddattaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ cāpam atulaṃ sadguṇaṃ dṛḍham ।। sauvarṇapuṅkhais tīkṣṇais tu śarair marmavidāraṇaiḥ ।। tayos tu yudhyatos tatra bhīmaśaktyor mahāmate ।। samutthito nṛpaśreṣṭha rāmarāvaṇayor yudhi ।।
padātir yuyudhe vīro rāmo anuktaparākramaḥ ।। preṣayāmasa devendro mahāntaṃ lokaviśrutam ।। mātulyuktopadeśas tu rāmacandraḥ pratāpavān ।। jaghāna vairiṇaṃ krūraṃ rāmadevaḥ pratāpavān ।।
indrādyā devatāḥ sarvāḥ parasparam athābruvan ।। anyair avadhyam apy enaṃ jaghāna yudhi rāvaṇam ।। pūjayāmo avatīryainam ity uktvā te divaukasaḥ ।। rudrendravasucandrādyā vidhātāraṃ sanātanam ।।
taṃ pūjayitvā vidhivat parivāryopatasthire ।। sugrīvo raviputro ayaṃ vāyuputro ayam āsthitaḥ ।। gandhāmoditadikpālā bhramarālipadānugā ।। papāta puṣpavṛṣṭis tu lakṣmaṇasya ca mūrdhani ।।
amoghākhyena stotreṇa stutvā rāmam avocata ।। tvam eva śāśvataṃ brahma vedānte viditaṃ param ।। tadāśru sarvalokānāṃ devānāṃ karma sādhitam ।। praṇamya rāmaṃ tasmai taṃ bhūyo daśarathaṃ nṛpam ।।
tato bāhubalaprāptaṃ vimānaṃ puṣpakaṃ śubham ।। tatas tu jānakīṃ devīṃ viśokāṃ bhūṣaṇānvitām ।। pratiṣṭhāpya mahādevaṃ setumadhye sa rāghavaḥ ।। rāmeśvara iti khyāto mahādevaḥ pinākadhṛk ।।
rāmas tīrṇapratijño asau bharatāsaktamānasaḥ ।। akarod dharmato rājyaṃ ciraṃ rāmaḥ pratāpavān ।। idaṃ subhaktyā paṭhatāṃ ca śṛṇvatāṃ dadāti rāmaḥ svapadaṃ jagatpatiḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe rāmaprādurbhāve dvipañcāśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
tṛtīyasya tu rāmasya kṛṣṇasya tu samāsataḥ ।। āsīnaṃ devamadhye tu brahmāṇaṃ kamalāsanam ।। te sarve kṣatriyā jātāḥ kaṃsādyāḥ kamalodbhava ।। mama tadbhārahāniḥ syād yathā deva tathā kuru ।।
kṣīrodasyottaraṃ kūlaṃ viṣṇuṃ bhaktivibodhitam ।। narasiṃhaṃ mahādevaṃ gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt ।। pūjayāmasa rājendra tena tuṣṭo jagatpatiḥ ।। tan me kathaya viprendra brahmoktaṃ stotram uttamam ।।
sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ viṣṇutuṣṭikaraṃ param ।। bhūtvaikāgramanā rājann idaṃ stotram udīrayat ।। anādim avyaktam acintyam avyayaṃ vedāntavedyaṃ puruṣottamaṃ harim ।। sarvātmakaṃ sarvagataikarūpaṃ dhyeyasvarūpaṃ praṇamāmi mādhavam ।।
caturbhujaṃ nīrajavarṇam īśvaraṃ rathāṅgapāṇiṃ praṇato asmi keśavam ।। pītāmbaraṃ hāravirājitodaraṃ namāmi viṣṇuṃ satataṃ kirīṭinam ।। gandharvasiddhair upagītam ṛgdhvaniṃ janārdanaṃ bhūtapatiṃ namāmi tam ।। karoti sṛṣṭiṃ jagataḥ kṣayaṃ yas taṃ vāsudevaṃ praṇato asmi keśavam ।।
nihatya yuddhe madhukaiṭabhāv ubhau taṃ vedavedyaṃ praṇato asmy ahaṃ sadā ।। hitāya kaurmaṃ vapur āsthito yas taṃ viṣṇum ādyaṃ praṇato asmi bhāskaram ।। yo bhūmim etāṃ sakalāṃ samuddharaṃs taṃ vedamūrtiṃ praṇamāmi sūkaram ।। jaghāna yas tīkṣṇanakhair diteḥ sutaṃ taṃ nārasiṃhaṃ puruṣaṃ namāmi ।।
jagattrayaṃ kramya dadau puraṃdare tad evaṃ ādyaṃ praṇato asmi vāmanam ।। taṃ jāmadagnyaṃ kṣitibhāranāśakaṃ nato asmi viṣṇuṃ puruṣottamaṃ sadā ।। jaghāna bhṛtyai jagatāṃ sanātanaṃ taṃ rāmadevaṃ satataṃ nato asmi ।। tathādya bhūmeḥ kuru bhārahāniṃ prasīda viṣṇo bhagavan namas te ।।
āvir babhūva bhagavān śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।। stutyānayāhaṃ saṃtuṣṭaḥ pitāmaha divaukasaḥ ।। yato asmi prakaṭībhūto durlabho api hariḥ surāḥ ।। padmayone vadādya tvaṃ śrutvā tat karavāṇi te ।।
daityānāṃ gurubhāreṇa pīḍiteyaṃ mahī bhṛśam ।। tenāgataḥ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ nānyad astīti kāraṇam ।। sthānaṃ nirāmayāḥ sarve padmayonis tu gacchatu ।। sitakṛṣṇe ca macchaktī kaṃsādīn ghātayiṣyataḥ ।।
gateṣu tridivaukaḥsu devadevo janārdanaḥ ।। preṣayāmasa te śaktī sitakṛṣṇe svake nṛpa ।। tadvat kṛṣṇā ca devakyāṃ vasudevād babhūva ha ।। devakīnandanaḥ kṛṣṇas tayoḥ karma śṛṇuṣva me ।।
rāmeṇa nihatā rājan tathā kṛṣṇena pūtanā ।। śakaṭaś cārjunau vṛkṣau tadvat kṛṣṇena ghātitau ।। kāliyo damitas toye kālindyāṃ viṣapannagaḥ ।। gokulaṃ rakṣatā tena ariṣṭaś ca nipātitaḥ ।।
akrūreṇa ca tau nītau mathurāyāṃ mahātmanā ।। svaṃ svaṃ rūpaṃ jale tasya akrūrasya vibhūtidam ।। babhūvuḥ prītamanaso hy akrūraś ca nṛpātmaja ।। kṛṣṇo jaghāna rāmaś ca tadvastraṃ brahmaṇe dadau ।।
tatas tasya varān dattvā durlabhān rāmakeśavau ।। tatkauṭilyam apānīya virūpaṃ kārmukaṃ tataḥ ।। hatvā kuvalayākhyaṃ ca gajaṃ rāmajanārdanau ।। yuddhe tu rāmo nijaghāna mallaṃ śailopamaṃ muṣṭikam avyayātmā ।।
yuddhvā tu tenātha ciraṃ jaghāna taṃ daityamallaṃ janasaṃsadīśaḥ ।। yuddhārtham utthāya kṛtakṣaṇaṃ taṃ muṣṭiprahāreṇa jaghāna vīraḥ ।। svayaṃ ca dehe vinipatya tasya hatvā tathorvyāṃ nicakarṣa kṛṣṇaḥ ।। sunābhasaṃjño balavīryayukto rāmeṇa nīto yamasādanaṃ kṣaṇāt ।।
kṛtvā nṛpaṃ cograsenaṃ yadūnāṃ sabhāṃ sudharmāṃ dadatur mahendrīm ।। guroḥ kṛte pañcajanaṃ nihatya yamaṃ ca jitvā gurave sutaṃ dadau ।। divyāstrapūrair amarāv imāv ubhau śubhāṃ purīṃ cakratuḥ sāgarānte ।। dagdhvā mahāntaṃ yavanaṃ hy upāyād varaṃ ca dattvā nṛpater jagāma ।।
vṛndāvane gopajanaiḥ subhāṣitaḥ sīreṇa rāmo yamunāṃ cakarṣa ।। kṣātreṇa saṃprāpya tadā sa rukmiṇīṃ kṛṣṇo api reme puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ ।। jaghānāṣṭapadenaiva rukmiṇaṃ cānṛtānvitam ।। hatvā tu narakaṃ cāpi jagrāha ca mahad dhanam ।।
gṛhītvā pārijātaṃ tu tato dvārāvatīṃ purīm ।। kurūṇāṃ bhayam utpādya mocayāmasa vīryavān ।। rāmeṇa tadbalaṃ nītaṃ kṣayaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ kṣaṇāt ।। tato arjunasya sāhāyyaṃ kurvatā kaṃsaśatruṇā ।।
tīrthayātrā kṛtā tadvad rāmeṇa jagataḥ kṛte ।। evaṃ tau rāmakṛṣṇau tu kṛtvā duṣṭavadhaṃ nṛpa ।। saṃkṣepād rāmakṛṣṇasya kālkyaṃ śṛṇu mamādhunā ।। kṛtvā tu bhūmer nṛpa bhārahāniṃ punaś ca viṣṇuṃ pratijagmatus te ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe kṛṣṇaprādurbhāve nāma tripañcāśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। prādurbhāvaṃ hareḥ puṇyaṃ kalkyākhyaṃ pāpanāśanam ।। vṛddhiṃ gate tathā pāpe vyādhisaṃpīḍite jane ।। sāmbhalākhye mahāgrāme nānājanasamākule ।।
aśvam āruhya khaḍgena mleccchān utsādayiṣyati ।। kṛtvā ca yāgaṃ bahukāñcanākhyaṃ saṃsthāpya dharmaṃ divam āruroha ।। imaṃ sadā yas tu nṛsiṃhabhaktaḥ śṛṇoti nityaṃ sa tu yāti viṣṇum ।। nārāyaṇasya devasya śṛṇvatāṃ kalmaṣāpahāḥ ।।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś ca munisattama ।। kimāhārāḥ kimācārā bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।। b śṛṇudhvam ṛṣayaḥ sarve bharadvājena saṃyutāḥ ।। d tasmāt kalir mahāghoraḥ sarvapāpasya sādhakaḥ ।।
ghore kaliyuge prāpte dvijadevaparāṅmukhāḥ ।। asūyāniratāś caiva vṛthāhaṃkāradūṣitāḥ ।। aham evādhika iti sarva eva vadanti vai ।। ataḥ svalpāyuṣaḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।।
vidyāgrahaṇaśūnyatvād adharmo vartate punaḥ ।। kāmakrodhaparā mūḍhā vṛthā saṃtāpapīḍitāḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ sarve dharmaparāṅmukhāḥ ।। uttamā nīcatāṃ yānti nīcāś cottamatāṃ tathā ।।
dharmakañcukasaṃvītā dharmavidhvaṃsakāriṇaḥ ।। yo yo aśvarathanāgāḍhyaḥ sa sa rājā bhaviṣyati ।। patīn putrān vañcayitvā gamiṣyanti striyo anyataḥ ।। khaṇḍavarṣī ca parjanyaḥ panthānas taskarāvṛtāḥ sarvaḥ sarvaṃ ca jānāti vṛddhān anupasevya ca ।।
kiṃkarāś ca bhaviṣyanti śūdrāṇāṃ ca dvijātayaḥ ।। patiṃ ca vanitā dveṣṭi kalau ghore samāgate ।। parānnalolupā nityaṃ bhaviṣyanti dvijātayaḥ ।। ghore kaliyuge prāpte naraṃ dharmaparāyaṇam ।।
na vratāni cariṣyanti brāhmaṇā vedanindakāḥ ।। dvijāḥ kurvanti dambhārthaṃ pitṛyajñādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।। kṣīropādhinimittena goṣu prītiṃ prakurvate ।। dānayajñajapādīnāṃ vikrīṇante phalaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
kaleḥ prathamapāde api vinindanti hariṃ narāḥ ।। śūdrastrīsaṅganiratā vidhavāsaṅgalolupāḥ ।। na ca dvijātiśūsrūṣāṃ na svadharmapravartanam ।। sukhāya parivītāś ca jaṭilā bhasmadhūrdharāḥ ।।
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ pāṣaṇḍā viprasattamāḥ ।। gītavādyaratā viprā vedavādaparāṅmukhāḥ ।। alpadravyā vṛthāliṅgā vṛthāhaṃkāradūṣitāḥ ।। pratigrahaparā nityaṃ dvijāḥ sanmārgaśīlinaḥ ।।
viśvāsahīnāḥ puruṣā devavedadvijātiṣu ।। svadharmatyāginaḥ sarve kṛtaghnā bhinnavṛttayaḥ ।। parāpavādaniratā ātmastutiparāyaṇāḥ ।। atyāhlādaparās tatra bhuñjānāḥ paraveśmani ।।
tatraiva nindāniratā bhuktvā caikatra saṃsthitāḥ ।। atyantakāminaś caiva saṃkīryante parasparam ।। na bhāryā na patiś caiva bhavitā tatra saṃkare ।। anāvṛṣṭibhayaprāyā gaganāsaktadṛṣṭayaḥ ।।
annopādhinimittena śiṣyān gṛhṇanti bhikṣavaḥ ।। kurvantyo gurubhartṛṇām ājñā bhetsyanti tā hitāḥ ।। tadā tadā kaler vṛddhir anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। sarvadharmeṣu naṣṭeṣu yāti niḥśrīkatāṃ jagat ।। b
evaṃ kaleḥ svarūpaṃ tat kathitaṃ viprasattamāḥ ।। d tapaḥ paraṃ kṛtayuge tretāyāṃ dhyānam eva hi ।। yatate daśabhir varṣais tretāyāṃ hāyanena tat ।। dhyāyan kṛte yajan yajñais tretāyāṃ dvāpare arcayan ।।
samastajagadādhāraṃ paramārthasvarūpiṇam ।। aho atīva mahābhāgyāḥ sakṛd ye keśavārcakāḥ ।। nyūnātiriktatā na syāt kalau vedoktakarmaṇām ।। hare keśava govinda vāsudeva jaganmaya ।।
itīrayanti ye nityaṃ na hi tān bādhate kaliḥ ।। te sabhāgyā mahātmānas tatsaṃgatiratā api ।। haripūjāratā ye ca te kṛtārthā na saṃśayaḥ ।। samastapuṇyaphaladaṃ kalau viṣṇoḥ prakīrtanam ।।
।। ity śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe kalilakṣaṇakīrtanaṃ catuḥpañcāśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। vāmanena sa viddhākṣaḥ stutvā tallabdhavān katham ।। jāhnavīsalile sthitvā devam abhyarcya vāmanam ।। hṛdi saṃcintya tuṣṭāva narasiṃhaṃ sanātanam ।।
balidarpaharaṃ śāntaṃ śāśvataṃ puruṣottamam ।। viśuddhaṃ jñānasaṃpannaṃ namāmi harim acyutam ।। anādim ajaraṃ nityaṃ namāmi garuḍadhvajam ।। pūjitaṃ ca hṛṣikeśaṃ taṃ namāmi jagadgurum ।।
jyotīrūpam anaupamyaṃ narasiṃhaṃ namāmy aham ।। yasyāvatārarūpāṇi samarcanti namāmi tam ।। trātaṃ yatra jagal līnaṃ taṃ namāmi janārdanam ।। taṃ devam amalaṃ divyaṃ praṇamāmi jagatpatim ।।
taṃ sarvasākṣiṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇamāmi sanātanam ।। prādur babhūva tasyāgre śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।। kimarthaṃ jāhnavītīre stuto ahaṃ tad bravīhi me ।। taddoṣasyāpanuttyarthaṃ stutavān asmi sāṃpratam ।।
