saṃtuṣṭo asmi tataḥ śukra stotreṇānena te mune ।। pāñcajanyena taccakṣuḥ pasparśa ca janārdanaḥ ।। babhūva nirmalaṃ cakṣuḥ pūrvavan nṛpasattama ।। jagāmādarśanaṃ sadyaḥ śukro api svāśramaṃ yayau ।।
śukreṇa kiṃ te kathayāmi rājan punaś ca māṃ pṛccha manorathāntaḥ ।। ।। ity śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe śukravarapradāno nāma pañcapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। śrotum icchāmi sakalaṃ pratiṣṭhāyāḥ paraṃ vidhim ।। pravakṣyāmi yathāśāstraṃ śṛṇu bhūpāla puṇyadam ।।
sa pūrvaṃ sthiranakṣatre bhūmiśodhanam ārabhet ।। pūrayec chuddhamṛdbhis tu jalāktaiḥ śarkarānvitaiḥ ।। prāsādaṃ kārayet tatra vāstuvidyāvidā nṛpa ।। śilābhittikam utkṛṣṭaṃ tadalābheṣṭikāmayam ।।
jātikāṣṭhamayaiḥ stambhais tallagnaiḥ phaladānvitaiḥ ।। itthaṃ tu kārayitvā hi harer veśma suśobhanam ।। ativṛddhātibālais tu kārayen nākṛtiṃ hareḥ ।। viśvakarmoktamārgeṇa purāṇoktāṃ nṛpottama ।।
saumyānanāṃ suśravanāṃ sunāsāṃ ca sulocanām ।। kārayet samadṛṣṭiṃ tu padmapatrāyatekṣaṇām ।। bimbauṣṭhīṃ suṣṭhucibukāṃ sugrīvāṃ kārayed budhaḥ ।। nābhisaṃlagnadivyāraṃ parito nemisaṃyutam ।।
pāñcajanyam iti khyātaṃ daityadarpaharaṃ śubham ।। sustanīṃ cāruhṛdayāṃ sujaṭharāṃ samāṃ śubhām ।। keyūrabāhukāṃ divyāṃ sunābhivalibhaṅgikām ।। evaṃ tāṃ kārayitvā tu pratimāṃ rājasattama ।।
pūrvapakṣe śubhe kāle pratimāṃ sthāpayed budhaḥ ।। caturdvāraṃ caturdikṣu caturbhis toraṇair yutam ।। pratimāṃ kṣālya vidvadbhiḥ ṣattriṃśadbhir ghaṭodakaiḥ ।। tatrāpi snāpayet paścāt pañcagavyaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।।
haridrākuṅkumādyais tu candanaiś copalepayet ।। puṇyāhaṃ tatra kṛtvā tu ṛgbhis tā prokṣya vāribhiḥ ।। vāsayet saptarātraṃ tu trirātraṃ vā nadījale ।। adhivāsya jale devam evaṃ pārthivapuṃgava ।।
tato bherīninādais tu vedaghoṣaiś ca keśavam ।। kṛtvā punas tataḥ snāpya viṣṇubhaktair alaṃkriyāt ।। caturbhir adhyayanaṃ kāryaṃ caturbhir pālanaṃ tathā ।। pūṣpākṣatānnamiśreṇa dadyād dikṣu balīn nṛpa ।।
pratyekaṃ sāyaṃ saṃdhyāyāṃ madhyarātre tathoṣasi ।। japan puruṣasūktaṃ tu ekatas tu punaḥ punaḥ ।। ahorātroṣito bhūtvā yajamāno dvijaiḥ saha ।। devasūktaṃ dvijaiḥ sārdham upasthāpya ca tāṃ dṛḍham ।।
prokṣayed devadeveśam ācāryaḥ kuśavāriṇā ।। juhuyāj jātakarmādi gāyatryā vaiṣṇavena tu ।। ācāryas tu svayaṃ kuryād astrair bandhaṃ ca kārayet ।। parodiveti yāmyāyāṃ vāruṇyāṃ niṣaveti ca ।।
paromātreti sūktābhyāṃ sarvatrājyāhutīr nṛpa ।। tataḥ sa dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād ṛtvigbhyaś ca yathārhataḥ ।। yajamānas tato dadyād vibhave sati kāñcanam ।। ekaviṃśatinā vāpi snapanaṃ kārayed budhaḥ ।।
yavavrīhiyutaiḥ pātrair uddhṛtair ucchritāṅkuraiḥ ।। snapanaṃ kārayitvā tu yathāvibhavavistaram ।। evaṃ yaḥ kurute rājan pratiṣṭhāṃ devacakriṇaḥ ।। vimānena vicitreṇa trissaptakulajair vṛtaḥ ।।
bāndhavāṃs teṣu saṃsthāpya viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। pratiṣṭhāvidhir ayaṃ viṣṇor mayaivaṃ te prakīrtitaḥ ।। paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ caiva sarvapāpapraṇāśanaḥ ।। tadā hy asau yāti hareḥ padaṃ tu yatra sthito ayaṃ na nivartate punaḥ ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe pratiṣṭhāvidhir nāma ṣaṭpañcāśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। yeṣāṃ saṃgatimātreṇa viṣṇuloko na dūrataḥ ।। saṃyatā dharmasaṃpannāḥ sarvārthān sādhayanti te ।। varṇāśramācārayutāḥ sarveṣāṃ supriyaṃvadāḥ ।।
śāntāś ca saumyavadanā nityaṃ dharmaparāyaṇāḥ ।। dambhamāyāvinirmuktāḥ kāmakrodhavivarjitāḥ ।। viṣṇukīrtanasaṃjātaharṣā romāñcitā janāḥ ।। īdṛgvidhā mahātmāno viṣṇubhaktāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।
iti proktaṃ tvayā vidvan bhṛguvarya guro mama ।। yaiḥ kṛtais tuṣyate devo narasiṃhaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। munibhiḥ saha saṃvādaṃ hārītasya mahātmanaḥ ।। praṇipatyābruvan sarve munayo dharmakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।।
varṇānām āśramāṇāṃ ca dharmaṃ prabrūhi śāśvatam ।। suṣvāpa bhogiparyaṅke śayane tu śriyā saha ।। tanmadhye cābhavad brahmā vedavedāṅgabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। asṛjat kṣatriyān bāhvor vaiśyāṃs tu ūruto asṛjat ।।
dharmaśāstraṃ ca maryādāṃ provāca kamalodbhavaḥ ।। dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ svargamokṣaphalapradam ।। tasya dharmaṃ pravakṣyāmi tadyogyaṃ deśam eva ca ।। tasmin deśe vaser dharmaṃ kuru brāhmaṇapuṃgava ।।
tair eva satataṃ yas tu pravṛttaḥ sukham edhate ।। dānaṃ pratigrahaś ceti karmaṣaṭkam ihocyate ।। śuśrūṣākāraṇaṃ caiva trividhaṃ parikīrtitam ।। vidhinā pratigṛhṇaṃś ca gṛhadharmapasiddhaye ।।
nityaṃ naimittakaṃ kāmyaṃ karma kuryāt prayatnataḥ ।। sāyaṃ prātar upāsīta vidhināgniṃ dvijottamaḥ ।। atithiṃ cāgataṃ bhaktyā pūjayec chaktito gṛhī ।। svadāranirato nityaṃ paradāravivarjitaḥ ।।
svakarmaṇi ca saṃprāpte pramādaṃ naiva kārayet ।। dharmam evaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt sa yāti brahmaṇaḥ padam ।। vadāmi rājādijanasya dharmaṃ pṛthak pṛthag bodhata vipravaryāḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe brāhmaṇadharmakathanaṃ nāma saptapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
yena yena pravartante vidhinā kṣatriyādayaḥ ।। kuryād adhyayanaṃ samyag yajed yajñān yathāvidhi ।। svadāranirato nityaṃ paradāravivarjitaḥ ।। devabrāhmaṇabhaktaś ca pitṛkāryaparas tathā ।।
uttamāṃ gatim āpnoti kṣatriyo athaivam ācaran ।। dānadharmaṃ yathāśaktyā guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ tathā ।। svadāranirato dāntaḥ paradāravivarjitaḥ ।। yajñādhyayanadānāni kuryān nityam atandritaḥ ।।
etad vaiśyasya karmoktaṃ svadharmam anutiṣṭataḥ ।। varṇatrayasya śuśrūṣāṃ kuryāc chūdraḥ prayatnataḥ ।। ayācitaṃ pradātavyaṃ kṛṣiṃ vṛttyartham ācaret ।। dhāraṇaṃ jīrṇavastrasya viprasyocchiṣṭamārjanam ।।
purāṇaśravaṇaṃ viprān narasiṃhasya pūjanam ।। satyasaṃbhāṣaṇaṃ caiva rāgadveṣavivarjanam ।। sthānam aindram avāpnoti naṣṭapāpas tu puṇyabhāk ।। śṛṇudhvam atrāśramadharmam ādyaṃ mayocyamānaṃ kramaśo munīndrāḥ ।।
guroḥ priyahitaṃ kāryaṃ karmaṇā manasā girā ।। udakumbhaṃ guror dadyāt tathā cendhanam āharet ।। vidhiṃ hitvā prakurvāṇo na svādhyāyaphalaṃ labhet ।। na tatphalam avāpnoti kurvāṇo vidhivicyutaḥ ।।
śaucācāram aśeṣaṃ tu śikṣayed gurusaṃnidhau ।। dhārayed apramattas tu brahmacārī samāhitaḥ ।। guroḥ kule na bhikṣeta na jñātikulabandhuṣu ।। ācamya prayato nityam aśnīyād gurvanujñayā ।।
vastrādikam athānyac ca gurave pratipādayet ।। brahmacārī vratī nityaṃ na kuryād dantaśodhanam ।। nṛtyagītakathālāpaṃ maithunaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।। kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca parivādaṃ tathā nṛṇām ।।
ekaḥ śayīta sarvatra na retaḥ skandayet kvacit ।। snātvārkam arcayitvāgniṃ punar mām ity ṛcaṃ japet ।। upāsīta yathānyāyaṃ brahmacārivrate sthitaḥ ।। yathāyogaṃ prakurvīta mātāpitros tu bhaktitaḥ ।।
tad eṣāṃ śāsane tiṣṭhed brahmacārī vimatsaraḥ ।। gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā tadā svasvecchayā vaset ।। sarāgo narakaṃ yāti pravrajan hi dhruvaṃ dvijaḥ ।। saṃnyased akṛtodvāho brāhmaṇo brahmacaryavān ।।
tena bhūyaḥ prajāyeta brahmacārī dṛḍhavrataḥ ।। saṃprāpya vidyām api durlabhāṃ tāṃ phalaṃ hi tasyāḥ sakalaṃ hi vindati ।। guror dattavaraḥ samyak samāvartanam ārabhet ।। sarvāvayavasaṃyuktāṃ sadvṛttām udvahet tataḥ ।।
vācālām atilomāṃ ca na vyaṅgāṃ bhīmadarśanām ।। na pakṣiahipreṣyanāmnīṃ na ca bhīṣaṇanāmikām ।। tanvoṣṭhakeśadaśanāṃ mṛdvaṅgīm udvahet striyam ।। yathāyogaṃ tathā hy evaṃ vivāhaṃ varṇadharmataḥ ।।
kuryāt snānaṃ tato vidvān dantadhāvanapūrvakam ।। tasmāc chuṣkam athārdraṃ vā bhakṣayed dantadhāvanam ।। apāmārgaṃ ca bilvaṃ ca arkaś codumbaras tathā ।। dantadhāvanakāṣṭhaṃ ca vakṣyāmi tatpraśastatām ।।
aṣṭāṅgulena mānena tatpramāṇam ihocyate ।। pratipaddarśaṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyāṃ caiva sattamāḥ ।। alābhe dantakāṣṭhasya pratiṣiddhe ca taddine ।। snātvā mantravad ācamya punar ācamanaṃ caret ।।
ādityena saha prātar mandehā nāma rākṣasāḥ ।। udakāñjalivikṣepo gāyatryā cābhimantritaḥ ।। tataḥ prayāti savitā brāhmaṇai rakṣito divi ।। tasmān na laṅghayet saṃdhyāṃ sāyaṃ prātar dvijaḥ sadā ।।
sāyaṃ mantravad ācamya prokṣya sūryasya cāñjalim ।। pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ sanakṣatrām upakramya yathāvidhi ।। tatas tv āvasathaṃ prāpya homaṃ kuryāt svayaṃ budhaḥ ।। tataḥ śiṣyahitārthāya svādhyāyaṃ kiṃcid ācaret ।।
kuśapuṣpendhanādīni gatvā dūrāt samāharet ।। vidhiṃ snānasya vakṣyāmi samāsāt pāpanāśanam ।। sudhīḥ snānārtham ādāya suklāṃ kuśatilaiḥ saha ।। nadyāṃ tu vidyamānāyāṃ na snāyād alpavāriṣu ।।
mṛttoyena svakaṃ deham abhiprakṣālya yatnataḥ ।। śubhe jale praviśyātha named varuṇam appatim ।। tataḥ snānaṃ samāsādyā apa ācamya mantrataḥ ।। kuśāgrasthena toyena prokṣyātmānaṃ prayatnataḥ ।।
tato nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ saṃsmaran praviśej jalam ।। snātvā kuśatilais tadvad devarṣīn pitṛbhiḥ saha ।। jalatīraṃ samāsādya dhaute śukle ca vāsasī ।। na raktam ulbaṇaṃ vāso na nīlaṃ tat praśasyate ।।
tataḥ prakṣālayet pādau mṛttoyena vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। pādau śirasi cābhyukṣet trir ācamya tu saṃspṛśet ।। aṅguṣṭhakaniṣṭhikābhyāṃ nābhau hṛdi talena ca ।। anena vidhinācamya brāhmaṇaḥ śuddhamānasaḥ ।।
prāṇāyāmāṃs tu kurvīta yathāśāstram atandritaḥ ।। trividho japayajñaḥ syāt tasya bhedaṃ nibodhata ।। trayāṇāṃ japayajñānāṃ śreyaḥ syād uttarottamam ।। śabdam uccārayed vācā japayajñaḥ sa vācikaḥ ।।
kiṃcin mantraṃ svayaṃ vindyād upāṃśuḥ sa japaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। śabdārthacintanaṃ dhyānaṃ tad uktaṃ mānasaṃ japaḥ ।। prasannā vipulān bhogān dadyān muktiṃ ca śāśvatīm ।। jāpinaṃ nopasarpanti dūrad evāpayānti te ।।
japed ahar ahaḥ snātvā sāvitrīṃ tanmanā dvijaḥ ।। gāyatrīṃ yo japen nityaṃ na sa pāpair hi lipyate ।। udutyaṃ ca japen mantraṃ citraṃ taccakṣur ity api ।। svena tīrthena devādīn adbhiḥ saṃtarpayed budhaḥ ।।
pitṝn pitṛgaṇāṃś caiva nityaṃ saṃtarpayed budhaḥ ।। darbheṣu darbhapāṇiḥ syād brahmayajñavidhānataḥ ।। tato arghaṃ bhānave dadyāt tilapuṣpajalānvitam ।। jale devaṃ namaskṛtya tato gṛhagataḥ punaḥ ।।
vaiśvadevaṃ tataḥ kuryād balikarma yathāvidhi ।। adṛṣṭapūrvam atithim āgataṃ prāk samarcayet ।। svāgatenāgnayas tuṣṭā bhavanti gṛhamedhinām ।। pādaśaucena pitaraḥ prītim āyānti tasya ca ।।
tasmād atithaye kāryaṃ pūjanaṃ gṛhamedhinā ।। bhikṣāṃ ca bhikṣave dadyāt parivrāḍbrahmacāriṇe ।। dadyāc ca manasā nityaṃ bhikṣāṃ bhikṣoḥ prayatnataḥ ।। avaśyam eva dātavyaṃ svargasopānakārakam ।।
vaiśvadevākṛtaṃ doṣaṃ śakto bhikṣur vyapohitum ।। bālavṛddhāṃs tataḥ śeṣaṃ svayaṃ bhuñjīta vai gṛhī ।। annaṃ pūrvaṃ namaskṛtya prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā ।। tataḥ svādukaraṃ cānnaṃ bhuñjīta susamāhitaḥ ।।
itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ kaṃcit kālaṃ nayed budhaḥ ।। kṛtahomaś ca bhuñjīta rātrāv atithim arcayet ।। nāntarā bhojanaṃ kuryād agnihotrasamo vidhiḥ ।। smṛtyuktān sakalān pūrvaṃ purāṇoktān api dvijaḥ ।।
tathākṣayyatṛtīyāyāṃ śiṣyān nādhyāpayed budhaḥ ।। adhyāpanam athābhyajya snānakāle vivarjayet ।। hiraṇyadānaṃ godānaṃ bhūmidānaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ svargaloke mahīyate ।।
śrāddhaṃ ca śraddhayā kuryāt sa yāti brahmaṇaḥ padam ।। sa tasmān muktim āpnoti brahmaṇā saha sattamāḥ ।। samyag gṛhasthasya sato hi dharmaṃ kurvan prayatnād dharim eti muktaḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe gṛhasthadharmo nāmāṣṭapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
dharmam agryaṃ mahābhāgāḥ kathyamānaṃ nibodhata ।। svabhāryāṃ tanaye sthāpye svaśiṣyaiḥ praviśed vanam ।। dhārayañ juhuyād agnau vaitānavidhinā sthitaḥ ।। kandamūlaphalair vāpi kuryān nityakriyāṃ budhaḥ ।।
pakṣe gate vā aśnīyān māsānte vā parākakṛt ।। ṣaṣṭhāhnakāle hy athavā athavā vāyubhakṣakaḥ ।। haimantike jale sthitvā nayet kālaṃ tapaś caran ।। agniṃ cātmani vai kṛtvā vrajed vāthottarāṃ diśam ।।
smarann atīndriyaṃ brahma brahmaloke mahīyate ।। vimuktapāpo hi manaḥpraśāntaḥ prayāti viṣṇoḥ sadanaṃ dvijendraḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe vānaprasthadharmo nāma ekonaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। śraddhayā yad anuṣṭhāya yatir mucyeta bandhanāt ।।
caturtham āśramaṃ gacchet saṃnyasya vidhinā dvijaḥ ।। dattvā śrāddham ṛṣibhyaś ca manujebhyas tathātmane ।। agniṃ svātmani saṃsthāpya mantravat pravrajet punaḥ ।। dadyāc ca bhūmāv udakaṃ sarvabhūtābhayaṃkaram ।।
veṣṭitaṃ kṛṣṇagovālarajjvā ca caturaṅgulam ।। gṛhṇīyād dakṣiṇe haste mantreṇaiva tu mantravit ।। pāduke cāpi gṛhṇīyāt kuryān nānyasya saṃgraham ।। saṃgṛhya kṛtasaṃnyāso gatvā tīrtham anuttamam ।।
vāriṇā tarpayitvā tu mantravad bhāskaraṃ namet ।। gāyatrīṃ ca yathāśakti japtvā dhyāyet paraṃ padam ।। sāyāhnakāle viprāṇāṃ gṛhāṇi vicared yatiḥ ।। tato nivṛttya tatpātram abhyukṣyācamya saṃyamī ।।
bhuñjīta parṇapuṭake pātre vā vagyato yatiḥ ।। kovidārakarañjeṣu na bhūñjīta kadācana ।। japadhyānetihāsais tu dinaśeṣaṃ nayed yatiḥ ।। kāṃsyasyeva tu yatpātraṃ gṛhasthasya tathaiva ca ।।
bhuktapātre yatir nityaṃ bhakṣayen mantrapūrvakam ।। kṛtasaṃdhyas tato rātriṃ nayed devagṛhādiṣu ।। tatpadaṃ samavāpnoti yat prāpya na nivartate ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe yatidharmo nāma ṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
yataḥ svargāpavargau tu prāpnuyus te dvijādayaḥ ।। yasyābhyāsabalād yānti mokṣaṃ ceha mumukṣavaḥ ।। tasmād yogaparo bhūtvā dhyāyen nityaṃ kriyāntare ।। dhāraṇābhir vaśīkṛtya punar durdharṣaṇaṃ manaḥ ।।
sukṣmāt sūkṣmataraṃ dhyāyej jagadādhāram acyutam ।। rahasy ekāntam āsīta dhyāyed ātmahṛdi sthitam ।। yaś ca sarvajanair jñeyaḥ so aham asmīti cintayet ।। śrutismṛtyuditaṃ karma tattadūrdhvaṃ samācaret ।।
evaṃ tapaś ca vidyā ca ubhāv api tapasvinaḥ ।। evaṃ tapaś ca vidyā ca saṃyukte bheṣajaṃ mahat ।। tathaiva jñānakarmabhyāṃ prāpyate brahma śāśvatam ।। dehadvandvaṃ vihāyāśu mukto bhavati bandhanāt ।।
na tāvad dehaliṅgasya vināśo vidyate kvacit ।। saṃkṣepeṇa dvijaśreṣṭhā dharmas teṣāṃ sanātanaḥ ।। praṇamya tam ṛṣiṃ jagmur muditās te svam ālayam ।। śrutvā ca kurute dharmaṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।।
ūrujasya tu yat karma pādajasya tathā nṛpa ।। anyathā vartamāno hi sadyaḥ patati yāty adhaḥ ।। tasmāt svadharmaṃ kurvīta nityam evam anāpadi ।। svadharmaṃ ye anutiṣṭhanti te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।।
varṇadharmānusāreṇa narasiṃhaṃ tathārcayet ।। satyātmakaṃ citsukharūpam ādyaṃ vihāya dehaṃ padam eti viṣṇoḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe yogādhyāyo nāmaikaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। bhūyaḥ kathaya rājendra śuśrūṣā tatra kā nṛpa ।।
tvayoktaṃ mama viprendra tat kathaṃ pūjanaṃ bhavet ।। tāni sthānāni tān mantrāṃs tvam ācakṣva mahāmune ।। yat kṛtvā munayaḥ sarve paraṃ nirvāṇam āpnuyuḥ ।। pratimāsv alpabuddhīnāṃ yogināṃ hṛdaye hariḥ ।।
eteṣu ca hareḥ samyag arcanaṃ munibhiḥ smṛtam ।। ānuṣṭubhasya sūktasya viṣṇus tasya ca devatā ।। dadyāt puruṣasūktena yaḥ puṣpāṇy apa eva ca ।। ādyayāvāhayed devam ṛcā tu puruṣottamam ।।
caturthyārghyaḥ pradātavyaḥ pañcamyācamanīyakam ।। yajñopavītam aṣṭamyā navamyā gandham eva ca ।। dvādaśyā ca tathā dīpaṃ trayodaśyārcanaṃ tathā ।। ṣoḍaśyodvāsanaṃ kuryāc cheṣakarmāṇi pūrvavat ।।
ṣaṇmāsāt siddhim āpnoti devadevaṃ samarcayan ।। haviṣāgnau jale puṣpair dhyānena hṛdaye harim ।। śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ dhyātvā viṣṇum upāsate ।। keyūravān makarakuṇḍalavān kirīṭī hārī hiraṇmayavapur dhṛtaśaṅkhacakraḥ ।।
sa sarvapāpaṃ pravihāya vaiṣṇavaṃ padaṃ prayāty acyutatuṣṭikṛn naraḥ ।। bhaktyaikalabhye puruṣe purāṇe muktyai kimarthaṃ kriyate na yatnaḥ ।। anena nityaṃ kuru viṣṇupūjāṃ prāptuṃ tadiṣṭaṃ yadi vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe viṣṇor arcāvidhir nāma dviṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
viṣṇor devātidevasya pūjanaṃ prati me adhunā ।। vedajñair eva nānyais tu tasmāt sarvahitaṃ vada ।। gandhapuṣpādibhir nityam arcayed acyutaṃ naraḥ ।। samastayajñaphaladaḥ sarvaśāntikaraḥ śubhaḥ ।।
oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya । anenābhyarcito devaḥ prīto bhavati tatkṣaṇāt ।। oṃ namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ ।। sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇusāyujyam āpnuyāt ।।
harer arcanam avyagraṃ sarvayajñaphalaṃ nṛpa ।। evaṃ kṛte nṛpaśreṣṭha narasiṃhaprasādataḥ prāpnoti vaiṣṇavaṃ tejo yat kāṅkṣanti mumukṣavaḥ ।। tṛṇabindumuneḥ śāpān mukto hy aṣṭākṣarāj japāt ।। ko apadharmaḥ kathaṃ strītvaṃ prāpto me vada kāraṇam ।।
viṣṇubhaktiprajananaṃ śṛṇvatāṃ paṭhatām idam ।। vairāgyasyāpi jananaṃ saṃbhūtaṃ bāhyavastuṣu ।। dhruvaṃ virāgīkṛtamānasānāṃ svargasya rājyaṃ na ca kiṃcid eva ।। vimṛśya caitan munayo apy ajasraṃ mokṣādhikāraṃ paricintayanti ।।
maitryādisaṃyogaparāṅmukhānāṃ vimuktibhājāṃ na tapo na bhogaḥ ।। nūnaṃ harārādhanakāraṇena kailāsam abhyeti vimuktikāmaḥ ।। samarcayantīṃ girijāṅghriyugmaṃ dhvajām ivānaṅgamahārathasya ।। susūkṣmavastrāntaradṛśyagātrāṃ nīhāramadhyād iva candralekhām ।।
dūrādhvagaṃ svagṛham etya susaṃcitārthas tasthau tadā surapatir viṣayābhilāṣī ।। tato dhanaṃ durlabham eva paścād dhanādhipatyaṃ sukṛtena labhyam ।। yaḥ svaṃ parityajya vimuktikāmas tiṣṭhāmi me durmatir asti citte ।। kṣetraṃ supakvaṃ parihṛtya dvāre kiṃ nāma cāraṇyakṛṣiṃ karoti ।।
akarmiṇo bhāgyavivarjitāś ca vāñchanti te mokṣapathaṃ vimūḍhāḥ ।। sarvādhir ākulamatiḥ parimuktadhairyaḥ sasmāra māram amarādhipacakravartī ।। purā maheśena kṛtāṅganāśo dhairyāl layaṃ gacchati ko viśaṅkaḥ ।। śīghraṃ samādeśaya mā vilambaṃ tasyāpadaṃ saṃprati bho diśāmi ।।
niṣpannam arthaṃ sahasaiva matvā jagāda vākyaṃ sa vihasya vīraḥ ।। soḍhuṃ samartho atha paro api loke ko nāma te māra śarābhighātam ।। etām anaṅgāyatalocanākhyāṃ madaṅgasaṅgaikarasāṃ vidhehi ।। saṃdhāya bāṇaṃ kusumāyudho api sasmāra māraḥ parimohanaṃ sudhīḥ ।।
vihāya pūjāṃ hasate sureśaṃ kaḥ kāmakodaṇḍaravaṃ saheta ।। saṃmohayantīva manāṃsi puṃsāṃ kasyeha kāntā vada puṇyabhājaḥ ।। kṛtākulā kāmaśilīmukhena sagadgadaṃ vākyam uvāca mandam ।। prabrūhi kāryaṃ ca tavāsti nātha kas tvaṃ vades tiṣṭhasi kāmarūpaḥ ।।
tvayā vinā jīvitam apy analpaṃ svargasya rājyaṃ mama niṣphalaṃ syāt ।। vimānam āruhya calatpatākaṃ sureśakaṇṭhagrahaṇaṃ cakāra ।। adṛṣṭadevāsurasaṃcarāsu vicitraratnāṅkurabhāsurāsu ।। svayaṃ ca yasyā laghupuṣpaśayyāṃ cakāra cāturyanidhiḥ sakāmaḥ ।।
mokṣādhikaṃ sneharasātimṛṣṭaṃ parāṅganāliṅganasaṅgasaukhyam ।। sasaṃbhramāḥ saṃbhramakhinnagātrāḥ sagadgadaṃ procur asāhasajñāḥ ।। saṃvīkṣamāṇaḥ kakubho api kāntāṃ vigṛhya vegād iha so api taskaraḥ ।। jagāda bhūyo na ca kiṃcid eva babhūva vai vṛkṣa ivāgnidagdhaḥ ।।
mohāpanodāya matiṃ dadhānaḥ sa kaṇṭhakubjo api samājagāma ।। viniḥśvasan gāḍhasakampagātraḥ svasthaṃ mano apy āśu vidhāya dīnaḥ ।। taṃ jīvitaṃ yat kriyate sudharmas tad ādhipatyaṃ yadi naṣṭavigraham ।। viśāmi cāgniṃ na ca veda kaścit parābhavo astīti ca ko mṛtānām ।।
hṛtā ca kenāpi vayaṃ na vidmo dhruvaṃ na tasyāsti bhayaṃ ca mṛtyoḥ ।। ākarṇyatāṃ nātha na cāsti yogyaḥ kāntāviyoge nijadehaghātaḥ ।। anekaśaḥ santi tavātra nāryaḥ ko nāma citte kriyate viṣādaḥ ।। bhṛśaṃ na jalpanti rudanti sādhavaḥ parābhavaṃ bāhyakṛtaṃ sahante ।।
sahāyakāryaṃ kurute hi saṃprati svayaṃ hi yasyāvarajo vibhīṣaṇaḥ ।। dhruvaṃ prasannā na bhavanti durjanāḥ kṛtopakārā harivajraniṣṭhurāḥ ।। uvāca vākyaṃ sa ca kaṇṭhakubjo yuktaṃ tvayoktaṃ ca dhanādhinātha ।। parābhavaṃ nānyakṛtaṃ sahante noṣṇaṃ jalaṃ jvālayate tṛṇāni ।।
svabāhuvīryārjitavittabhogināṃ svabandhuvargeṣu hi ko virodhaḥ ।। vibhīṣaṇasya sāmīpyaṃ jagāmāśu vicārayan ।। prāptaṃ pratyājagāmāśu vinayena samanvitaḥ ।। saṃtaptamānaso bhūpa jagādedaṃ vaco mahat ।।
nivedayādhunāsmākaṃ niścayān mārjayāmi tat ।। tadaikāntaṃ samāsādya kathayāmasa vedanām ।। b gṛhītā kiṃ svayaṃ yātā nihatā kenacid dviṣā ।। d etad bandho mahat kaṣṭaṃ mama nārīsamudbhavam ।।
prāṇān vai ghātayiṣyāmi anāsādya ca vallabhām ।। b ānayiṣyāmi te kāntāṃ yatra tatra sthitāṃ vibho ।। d tato vibhīṣaṇas tatra nāḍījaṅghāṃ niśācarīm ।। dhanadasya ca yā kāntā citrasenāvidhānataḥ ।।
tāṃ ca jānīhi saṃvīkṣya devarājādiveśmasu ।। jagāma tridivaṃ śīghraṃ devarājādiveśmasu ।। yasyāḥ samaṃ dhruvaṃ rūpaṃ vidyate na carācare ।। saṃprāpto mandarāc chīghraṃ preritaś citrasenayā ।।
tatra paśyan sa tāṃ tanvīṃ nijasthāne sabhāgatām ।। tāṃ vīkṣya devarājo api sa kāmavaśago abhavat ।। tasyāḥ pārśve samānetuṃ dhruvaṃ cāntaḥpure tadā ।। āgaccha bhava tanvaṅgi devarājasamīpagā ।।
ityuktā sā tadā tābhyāṃ jagāda madhurākṣaram ।। b devarājaḥ svayaṃ yan me pārśvaṃ cātrāgamiṣyati ।। d tau tadā vāsavaṃ gatvā ūcatur vacanaṃ śubham ।। sarvadā dāsabhūtas te yācase tad dadāmy aham ।।
tato ahaṃ vaśagā deva bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ ।। mama rūpasamā rāmā kāntā te cāsti vā na vā ।। darśayiṣyāmi sarvaṃ te devi kāntāparigraham ।। tato jagāda bhūyaḥ sa kiṃcid gūḍhaṃ mama sthitam ।।
vimucyaikāṃ ca yuvatīṃ sarvaṃ te darśitaṃ mayā ।। b sā rāmā mandare cāsti avijñātā surāsuraiḥ ।। d tataḥ sa devarājo api tayā sārdhaṃ ca bhūpate ।। tasya vai gacchamānasya vimānenārkavarcasā ।।
taṃ vīkṣya nāradaṃ vīro lajjamāno api vāsavaḥ ।। tataḥ kṛtāśīḥ sa munir avadat trideveśvaram ।। nāḍījaṅghe asti kuśalaṃ rākṣasānāṃ mahātmanām ।। evam uktā ca muninā sā kṛṣṇavadanābhavat ।।
nārado api gataḥ snātuṃ kailāse mānasaṃ saraḥ ।। yatrāśramo asti vai nūnaṃ tṛṇabindor mahātmanaḥ ।। hantum icchati deveśo nāḍījaṅghāṃ niśācarīm ।। dhṛtā krandati sā rājann indreṇāpi niśācarī ।।
tadāgatya muniśreṣṭhas tṛṇabindur mahātapāḥ ।। jalpaty evaṃ munau tasmin mahendreṇa niśācarī ।। sa cukopa muniśreṣṭhaḥ prekṣamāṇo muhur muhuḥ ।। tatas tvaṃ mama śāpena niścayāt strī bhaviṣyasi ।।
ahaṃ svāmī surāṇāṃ ca śāpaṃ mā dehi me adhunā ।। mamātra tapaso bhāvān na nighnanti parasparam ।। jagāma tridivaṃ bhūpa hataśaktiparākramaḥ ।। devā duḥkhaṃ samāpannā dṛṣṭvā strītvaṃ gataṃ harim ।।
jagmuś ca brahmasadanaṃ tathā dīnā śacī tadā ।। devā ūcuś ca te sarve vāsavena samanvitāḥ ।। sa muniḥ kopavān brahman naiva gacchaty anugraham ।। svakarmaṇopayāto sau strītvaṃ strīvadhakāraṇāt ।।
jahāra citrasenāṃ ca suguptāṃ dhanadāṅganām ।। tena karmavipākena strībhāvaṃ vāsavo gataḥ ।। tat sarvaṃ sādhayiṣyāmo vayaṃ śacyā samanvitāḥ ।। tāṃ ca tasmai pradāsyāmaḥ sarve kṛtvā parāṃ matim ।।
nandane cārcanaṃ kartā sarvadā yakṣarakṣasām ।। mumoca yakṣabhavanaṃ priyakaṣṭānuvartinīm ।। dhaneśaṃ kathayāmasa citrasenāsamāgamam ।। sakhīṃ svām atulāṃ prāpya caritārthā babhūva sā ।।
gokulaṃ kṛṣṇahīnaṃ tu tathendreṇāmarāvatī ।। vāsavasya samākhyāhi yataḥ strītvād vimucyate ।। tīrthaṃ cānyan na paśyāmi muktvaikaṃ viṣṇupūjanam ।। karotu vidhivac chakraḥ strītvād yena ca mucyate ।।
oṃ namo narāyaṇāyeti japa tvam ātmaśuddhaye ।। strībhāvāc ca vinirmuktas tadā viṣṇoḥ prasādataḥ ।। mayā bhṛguniyuktena kuru sarvam atandritaḥ ।। te muktapāpāḥ paradāragāmino viśanti viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ dhruvam ।।
narasiṃhaṃ samārādhya prāptavān vaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।। sahasrānīkacaritaṃ kim anyat kathayāmi te ।। saṃprāpya sa jñānam atīva nirmalaṃ tenaiva viṣṇuṃ pratipadyate janaḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sahasrānīkacarite aṣṭākṣaramantrakathanaṃ nāma triṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।।
sāṃkhyaṃ kecit praśaṃsanti yogam anye pracakṣate ।। kṣamāṃ kecit praśaṃsanti tathaiva ca dayārjavam ।। samyagjñānaṃ paraṃ kecit kecid vairāgyam uttamam ।। ātmadhyānaṃ paraṃ kecit sāṃkhyatattvārthavedinaḥ ।।
upāyaḥ padabhedena bahudhaivaṃ pracakṣyate ।। vyāmoham eva gacchanti vimuktāḥ pāpakarmabhiḥ ।। vaktum arhasi sarvajña mama sarvārthasādhakam ।। atraivodāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam ।।
brāhmaṇaḥ śrutasaṃpannaḥ puṇḍarīko mahāmatiḥ ।। jitendriyo jitakrodhaḥ saṃdhyopāsanadhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। samidbhiḥ sādhuyatnena sāyaṃ prātar hutāśanam ।। tapassvādhyāyanirataḥ sākṣād brahmasuto yathā ।।
mātāpitṛbhyāṃ śuśrūṣur bhikṣāhārī janapriyaḥ ।। buddhir āsīn mahārāja saṃsārārṇavatāraṇī pitaraṃ mātaraṃ caiva bhrātṛn atha pitāmahān ।। parityajya mahodāras tṛṇānīva yathāsukham ।। anityaṃ yauvanaṃ rūpam āyuṣyaṃ dravyasaṃcayam ।।
purāṇoditamārgeṇa sarvatīrthāni vai mune ।। gaṅgāṃ ca yamunāṃ caiva gomatīm atha gaṇḍakīm ।। prayāgaṃ narmadāṃ caiva mahānadyo nadān api ।। anyāni ca mahātejās tīrtāni sa mahāvrataḥ ।।
kadācit prāptavān vīraḥ śālagrāmaṃ tapodhanaḥ ।। āsevyamānam ṛṣibhis tattvavidbhis tapodhanaiḥ ।। bhūṣitaṃ cakranadyā ca cakrāṅkitaśilātalam ।। kecic cakrāṅkitās tasmin prāṇinaḥ puṇyadarśanāḥ ।।
tasmin kṣetre mahāpuṇye śālagrāme mahāmatiḥ ।। snātvā devahrade tīrthe sarasvatyāṃ ca suvrataḥ ।। tathānyāny api tīrthāni tasminn eva cacāra saḥ ।। manaḥ prasādam agamat tasya tasmin mahātmanaḥ ।।
tatraiva siddhim ākāṅkṣan samārādhya jagatpatim ।। uvāsa ciram ekākī nirdvandvaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। yamaiś ca niyamaiś caiva tathā cāsanabandhanaiḥ ।। dhāraṇābhis tathā dhyānaiḥ samādhibhir atandritaḥ ।।
ārādhya devadeveśaṃ tadgatenāntarātmanā ।। prasādaṃ param ākāṅkṣan viṣṇos tadgatamānasaḥ ।। puṇḍarīkasya rājendra kālo agacchan mahāṃs tataḥ ।। jagāma sumahātejāḥ sākṣādādityasaṃnibhaḥ ।।
viṣṇubhaktiparītātmā vaiṣṇavānāṃ hite rataḥ ।। mahāmatiṃ mahāprājñaṃ sarvāgamaviśāradam ।। arghaṃ dattvā yathāyogyaṃ praṇāmam akarot tataḥ ।। ātodyahastaḥ sumukho jaṭāmaṇḍalabhūṣaṇaḥ ।।
iti saṃcintayan vipraḥ papraccha paramadyutiḥ ।। tvaddarśanaṃ hy apuṇyānāṃ prāyeṇa bhuvi durlabham ।। puṇḍarīka harer bhaktas tvādṛśaḥ satataṃ dvija ।। punāti bhagavadbhaktaś cāṇḍālo api yadṛcchayā ।।
ityukto nāradenāsau bhaktiparyākulātmanā ।। provāca madhuraṃ vipras taddarśanasuvismitaḥ ।। b dhanyo ahaṃ dehinām adya supūjyo ahaṃ surair api ।। d anugṛhṇīṣva devarṣe tvadbhaktasya viśeṣataḥ ।।
kartavyaṃ paramaṃ guhyam upadeṣṭuṃ tvam arhasi ।। tvaṃ gatiḥ saravalokānāṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। b anekānīha śāstrāṇi karmāṇi ca tathā dvija ।। d vailakṣaṇyaṃ ca jagatas tasmād eva dvijottama ।।
ity evaṃ prāhur apare tatraiva layam eva ca ।। anyair matimatāṃ śreṣṭha tattvālokanatatparaiḥ ।। vadanti ṛṣayaḥ sarve nānāmataviśāradāḥ ।। paramārtham idaṃ guhyaṃ ghorasaṃsāramocanam ।।
na gṛhṇāti nṛṇāṃ dṛṣṭir vartamānārthaniścitā ।। yat proktaṃ brahmaṇā pūrvaṃ pṛcchato mama suvrata ।। praṇipatya yathānyāyaṃ pṛṣṭavān aham avyayam ।। etan me tattvataḥ sarvaṃ tvam ācakṣva pitāmaha ।।
sa eva sarvabhūtānāṃ nara ity abhidhīyate ।। tāny eva cāyanaṃ tasya tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tasminn eva punas tac ca pralaye saṃpralīyate ।। nārāyaṇaḥ paraṃ jyotir ātmā nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ ।।
yac ca kiṃcij jagaty asmin dṛśyate śrūyate api vā ।। evaṃ viditvā taṃ devāḥ sākāraṃ vyāharan muhuḥ ।। kiṃ tasya dānaiḥ kiṃ tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tapobhiḥ kim adhvaraiḥ ।। etaj jñānaṃ varaṃ nāto yogaś caiva paras tathā ।।
bahavo api yathā mārgā viśanty evaṃ mahat puram ।। sa hi sarvagato devaḥ sūkṣmo avyaktaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। viṣṇur vibhur acintyātmā nityaḥ sadasadātmakaḥ ।। yasmāt prāptaṃ sthitiṃ kṛtsnaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।।
yasmād vā sarvabhūtānāṃ tattvādyānāṃ yugakṣaye ।। tam āhuḥ puruṣaṃ kecit kecid īśvaram avyayam ।। kecit kālam anādyantaṃ kecij jīvaṃ sanātanam ।। kecit kṣetrajñam ity āhuḥ kecit ṣaḍviṃśakaṃ tathā ।।
ete cānye ca munibhiḥ saṃjñābhedāḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ ।। ekaṃ yadi bhavec chāstraṃ jñānaṃ niḥsaṃśayaṃ bhavet ।। āloḍya sarvaśāstrāṇi vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। tyaktvā vyāmohakān sarvān tasmāc chāstrārthavistarān ।।
evaṃ jnātvā tu satataṃ devadevaṃ tam avyayam ।। śrutvedaṃ brahmaṇā proktaṃ jñānayogaṃ sudurlabham ।। namo nārāyaṇāyeti ye vidur brahma śāśvatam ।। tasmān nārāyaṇas tāta paramātmā sanātanaḥ ।।
nārāyaṇo jagadvyāpī paramātmā sanātanaḥ ।। śravaṇāt paṭhanāc caiva nididhyāsanatatparaiḥ ।। niḥspṛhā nityasaṃtuṣṭā jñāninaḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ ।। apakṣapatitāḥ śāntāḥ sarvasaṃkalpavarjitāḥ ।।
tyaktatrayā mahātmāno vāsudevaṃ hariṃ gurum ।। tasmāt tvam api viprendra nārāyaṇaparo bhava ।। helayā kīrtito yo vai svaṃ padaṃ diśati dvija ।। tam evoddiśya deveśaṃ kuru nityam atandritaḥ ।।
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ ।। bhūṣito vā dvijaśreṣṭha na liṅgaṃ dharmakāraṇam ।। te api yānti paraṃ sthānaṃ narā nārāyaṇāśrayāḥ ।। dāso aham vāsudevasya devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ।।
kiṃ punas tatgataprāṇaḥ puruṣa saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। paropakāraniratas trailokyasyaikabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। namo astu keśavāyeti punaḥ punar udīrayan ।। hṛtpuṇḍarīke govindaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya janārdanam ।।
uvāsa ciram ekākī puruṣārthavicakṣaṇaḥ ।। nidrāpi tasya naivāsīt puruṣārthavirodhinī ।। janmajanmāntarārūḍhasaṃskāreṇa ca sa dvijaḥ ।। avāpa paramāṃ siddhiṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ vītakalmaṣaḥ ।।
nivasanti dvijaśreṣṭha praśāntendriyavṛttayaḥ ।। prādur āsīj jagannāthaḥ puṇḍarīkāyatekṣaṇaḥ ।। śrīvatsavakṣāḥ śrīvāsaḥ kaustubhena vibhūṣitaḥ ।। meruśṛṅgam ivāruḍhaḥ kālameghas taḍiddyutiḥ ।।
virājamāno deveśaś cāmaravyajanādibhiḥ ।। papāta śirasā bhūmau sādhvasāvanato dvijaḥ ।। jagāma mahatīṃ tṛptiṃ puṇḍarīkas tadānaghaḥ ।। tatas tam āha bhagavān padmanābhas trivikramaḥ ।।
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva dāsyāmi yat te manasi vartate ।। idaṃ vijñāpayam āsa puṇḍarīko mahāmatiḥ ।। yad dhitaṃ mama deveśa tad ājñāpaya mādhava ।। puṇḍarīkaṃ mahābhāgaṃ kṛtāñjalim upasthitam ।।
madrūpadhārī nityātmā mamaiva pārṣado bhava ।। devadundubhayo neduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca ।। jaguś ca siddhagandharvāḥ kiṃnarāś ca viśeṣataḥ ।। jagāma garuḍārūḍhaḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ ।।
taccittas tadgataprāṇas tadbhaktānāṃ hite rataḥ ।। śṛṇuṣva tatkathāḥ puṇyāḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīḥ ।। prīto bhavati viśvātmā tat kuruṣva suvistaram ।। nāpnuvanti gatiṃ puṇyāṃ nārāyaṇaparāṅmukhāḥ ।।
nirupamam upameyaṃ yogināṃ jñānagamyaṃ tribhuvanagurum īśaṃ tvāṃ prapanno asmi viṣṇo ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe puṇḍarīkanāradasaṃvāde catuḥṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। nāmāni ca suguhyāni vada pāpaharāṇi ca ।। bhagavantaṃ devadevaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।।
bhaktair anyaiḥ suraśreṣṭha muktikāmair viśeṣataḥ ।। tāny ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi tvattaḥ padmāyatekṣaṇa ।। tvadbhaktānāṃ hitārthāya tan me vada sureśvara ।। kṣetrāṇi caiva guhyāni tava vakṣyāmi tattvataḥ ।।
anantaṃ kapiladvīpe prabhāse ravinandanam ।। ṛṣabhe tu mahāviṣṇuṃ dvārakāyāṃ tu bhūpatim ।। vallīvaṭe mahāyogaṃ citrakūṭe narādhipam ।। śālagrāme tapovāsam acintyaṃ gandhamādane ।।
garuḍadhvajaṃ tu sakale govindaṃ nāma sāyake ।। kedāre mādhavaṃ vindyād vārāṇasyāṃ tu keśavam ।। tṛṇabinduvane vīram aśokaṃ sindhusāgare ।। viśvāsayūpe viśvaīśaṃ narasiṃhaṃ mahāvane ।।
puruṣottamaṃ daśapure kubjake vāmanaṃ viduḥ ।। devadāruvane guhyaṃ kāveryāṃ nāgaśāyinam ।। kumāratīrthe kaumāraṃ lohite hayaśīrṣakam ।। hariharaṃ tu bhadrāyāṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpāt pramucyate ।।
lokanātham ayodhyāyāṃ kuṇḍine kuṇḍineśvaram ।। āḍhye viṣṇupadaṃ vidyāc chūkare śūkaraṃ viduḥ ।। trikūṭe nāgamokṣaṃ ca merupṛṣṭhe ca bhāskaram ।। yaśaskaraṃ vipāśāyāṃ māhiṣmatyāṃ hutāśanam ।।
śivanadyāṃ śivakaraṃ gayāyāṃ ca gadādharam ।। aṣṭaṣaṣṭiś ca nāmāni kathitāni mayā tava ।। etāni mama nāmāni rahasyāni prajāpate ।। gavāṃ śatasahasrasya dattasya phalam āpnuyāt ।।
duḥsvapnaṃ na bhavet tasya matprasādān na saṃśayaḥ ।। vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo mama loke sa modate ।। vaiṣṇavais tu viśeṣeṇa teṣām muktiṃ dadāmy aham ।। imaṃ stavaṃ yaḥ paṭhate sa mānavaḥ prāpnoti viṣṇor amṛtātmakaṃ padam ।।
।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe ādye dharmārthamokṣadāyini viṣṇuvallabhe pañcaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। punar anyāni nāmāni yāni tāni nibodha me ।। sarayūḥ sarasvatī ca candrabhāgā carmaṇvatī ।। narmadā ca mahāpuṇyā tīrthāny etāni cottare ।।
tathā brahmagireś cāpi mekhalābhiḥ samanvitāḥ ।। godāvarī mahāpuṇyā sarvatra caturānana ।। hareṇa sārdhaṃ prītyā tu vasāmi munipūjitaḥ ।। sahye tv āmalakagrāme sthito ahaṃ kamalodbhava ।।
yeṣu snātvā ca pītvā ca pāpān mucyati mānavaḥ ।। brahmaṇe gatavān brahman brahmāpi svapuraṃ gataḥ ।। tāni me vada dharmajña vistareṇa yathārthataḥ ।। tatrāsau devadeveśaḥ pūjyate brahmaṇā svayam ।।
sahyāmalakatīrthasya utpattyādi mahāmune ।। āsīd brahman mahogro ayaṃ nāmnāyaṃ cocyate budhaiḥ ।। darśanīyāni divyāni durlabhāni mahāmune ।। sa dṛṣṭas tu mahāvṛkṣo mahāphalasamanvitaḥ ।।
dhyānena dṛṣṭavāṃs tatra punar āmalakaṃ tarum ।। utthāya ca punaḥ paśyet pratimām eva kevalām ।। tatas tv ārādhayāmasa devadeveśam avyayam ।। dvādaśabhiḥ saptabhis tu saṃkhyābhiḥ pujito hariḥ ।।
śrīsahyāmalakagrāme devadeveśam avyayam ।। tasya pādatale tīrthaṃ niḥsṛtaṃ paścimāmukham ।। cakratirthe naraḥ snātvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। śaṅkhatīrthe naraḥ snātvā vājapeyaphalaṃ labhet ।।
brahmaṇaḥ kuṇḍikā pūrvaṃ gaṅgātoyaprapūritā ।। nāmnā tatkuṇḍikātīrthaṃ śilāgṛhasamanvitam ।। trirātropoṣito bhūtvā yas tatra snāti mānavaḥ ।। kuṇḍikātīrthād uttare piṇḍasthānāc ca dakṣiṇe ।।
trirātram uṣito yas tu tatra snānaṃ samācaret ।। śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā pitṛbhyaś ca piṇḍasthāneṣu yo narah ।। sutṛptāḥ pitaro yānti pitṛlokaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। sarvapāpakṣayaṃ prāpya viṣṇuloke sa modate ।।
sarvakratuphalaṃ prāpya nākapṛṣṭhe mahīyate ।। āyurbhogaphalaṃ prāpya svargaloke mahīyate ।। vārāhatīrthe viprendra sahye yaḥ snānam ācaret ।। ākāśagaṅgānāmnā ca sahyāgre tīrtham uttamam ।।
tasyāṃ bhaktyā tu yaḥ snāti naro dvijavarottamam ।। brahmann amalasahyādrer yadyadtoyavinirgamaḥ ।। sahyādriṃ gatavān nityaṃ snātvā pāpāt pramucyate ।। dattvā supuṣpāṇi hariṃ sa bhaktyā vihāya pāpaṃ praviśet sa viṣṇum ।।
sarvatīrthamayī gaṅgā sarvadevamayo hariḥ ।। evaṃ te kathitaṃ vipra kṣetramāhātmyam uttamam ।। devadevasya pādasya talād bhuvi niniḥsṛtam ।। snānāc ca tatra manujā na punar bhavanti pādau praṇamya śirasā madhusūdanasya ।।
kālena tīrthasalilāni punanti pāpāt pādodakaṃ bhagavatas tu punāti sadyaḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapuraṇe tīrthapraśaṃsāyāṃ ṣaṭsaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। mānasāni hi tīrthāni phaladāni viśeṣataḥ ।। satyaṃ tīrthaṃ dayā tīrthaṃ tīrtham indriyanigrahaḥ ।।
svadharmācaraṇaṃ tīrthaṃ tīrtham agner upāsanam ।। ekabhuktaṃ tathā naktam upavāsaṃ ca vai mune ।। tatraikabhuktaṃ kurvāṇaḥ puṇyāṃ gatim avāpnuyāt ।। aṣṭamyāṃ tu trayodaśyāṃ sa prāpnoty abhivāñchitam ।।
narasiṃhaṃ samabhyarcya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। snātvārkamadhye viṣṇuṃ ca dhyātvā rogāt pramucyate ।। sauranaktaṃ vijānīyān na naktaṃ niśi bhojanam ।। tarpayitvā pitṛn devān ṛṣīṃś ca tilatandulaiḥ ।।
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। arghyaṃ dadyāt samabhyarcya agastyāya mahāmune ।। mantreṇānena vai dadyāc chitapuṣpādinārcite ।। mitrāvaruṇayoḥ putra kumbhayone namo astu te ।।
samudraḥ śoṣito yena so agastyaḥ prīyatāṃ mama ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktas tamas tarati dustaram ।। purāṇaṃ nārasiṃhaṃ ca munīnāṃ saṃnidhau mayā ।। vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva sarvam eva prakīrtitam ।।
tebhyaś ca bhṛguṇā proktaṃ mārkaṇḍeyāya vai tataḥ ।। prasādān narasiṃhasya prāptaṃ vyāsena dhīmatā ।। purāṇaṃ narasiṃhasya mayā ca kathitaṃ tava ।। yaḥ śṛṇoti śucir bhūtvā purāṇaṃ hy etad uttamam ।।
yo bhaktyā śrāvayed bhaktān nityaṃ naraharer idam ।। śrutvaivaṃ snātakaiḥ sārdhaṃ bharadvājo mahāmatiḥ ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ nṛsiṃhātmakam ।। prasanne devadeveśe sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet ।।
prakṣīṇapāpabandhās te muktiṃ yānti narā iti ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe mānasatīrthavrataṃ nāma saptaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।। narp ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvaduḥkhanivāraṇam ।। ye paṭhanty api śṛṇvanti ślokaṃ ślokārdham eva vā ।।
viṣṇvarpitam idaṃ puṇyaṃ purāṇaṃ sarvakāmadam ।। śatajanmārjitaiḥ pāpaiḥ sadya eva vimocitāḥ ।। kiṃ tīrthair gopradānair vā tapobhir vā kim adhvaraiḥ ।। yaḥ paṭhet prātar utthāya yad asya ślokaviṃśatim ।।
etat pavitraṃ pūjyaṃ ca na vācyam akṛtātmanām ।। etat purāṇaśravaṇam ihāmutra sukhapradam ।। bahunātra kim uktena bhūyo bhūyo munīśvarāḥ ।। bhāradvājamukhāḥ sarve kṛtakṛtyā dvijottamāḥ ।।
sūtaṃ hṛṣṭāḥ prapūjyātha sarve svasvāśramaṃ yayuḥ ।। ।। iti śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇe sūtabharadvājādisaṃvāde sarvaduḥkhopaharaṃ śrīnarasiṃhapurāṇasya māhātmyaṃ samāptam ।। narp ।।
